Uttarajjhaya

22/7/1997
This text in Roman has been transcribed by M. Yamazaki and Y. Ousaka 
from the one in Devanagari, based on Charpentier's edition 
[Uttaradhyanam-sutra, Uppsala 1922].

set to UTF-8.)

U/1 viṇayasuyaṃ prathamam adhyayanam /
 saṃjogā vippamukkassa | aṇagārassa bhikkhuṇo /
 viṇayaṃ pāukarissāmi | āṇupuvviṃ suṇeha me 
 āṇāniddesakare | gurūṇam uvavāyakārae /
 iṃgiyāgārasaṃpanne | se viṇīe tti vuccaī 
 āṇāniddesakare | gurūṇam aṇuvavāyakārae /
 paḍaṇīe asaṃbuddhe | aviṇīe tti vuccaī 
 jahā suṇī pūikaṇṇī | nikkasijjai savvaso /
 evaṃ dussīlapaḍiṇīe | muharī nikkasijjaī 
 kaṇakuṇḍagaṃ caittāṇaṃ | viṭhaṃ bhuṃjai sūyare /
 evaṃ sīlaṃ caittāṇaṃ | dussīle ramaī mie 
 suṇiyā bhāvaṃ sāṇassa | sūyarassa narassa ya /
 viṇae ṭhavejja appāṇam | icchanto hiyam appaṇo 
 tamhā viṇayamesijjā | sīlaṃ paḍilabhejjae /
 buddhaputte niyāgaṭhī | na nikkasijjai kaṇhuī 
 nisante siyāmuharī | buddhāṇam antie sayā /
 aṭhajuttāṇi sikkhijjā | niraṭhāṇi u vajjae 
 aṇusāsio na kuppijjā | khaṃtiṃ sevijja paṇḍie /
 khuḍḍehiṃ saha saṃsaggiṃ | hāsaṃ kīḍaṃ ca vajjae 
 mā ya caṇḍāliyaṃ kāsī | bahuyaṃ mā ya ālave /
 kāleṇa ya ahijjittā | tao jhāijja egago 
 āhacca caṇḍāliyaṃ kau | na niṇhavijja kayāi vi /
 kaḍaṃ kaḍe tti bhāsejjā | akaḍaṃ no kaḍe tti ya 
 mā galiyasse va kasaṃ | vayaṇam icche puṇo puṇo /
 kasaṃ va daṭhum āiṇṇe | pāvagaṃ parivajjae 
 aṇāsavā thūlavayā kusīlā | miuṃ pi caṇḍaṃ pakarinti sīsā /
 cittāṇuyā lahu dakkhovaveyā | pasāyae te hu durāsayaṃ pi 
 nāpuṭho vāgare kiṃci | puṭho vā nāliyaṃ vae /
 kohaṃ asaccaṃ kuvvejjā | dhārejjā piyamappiyaṃ 
 appā ceva dameyavvo | appā hu khalu duddamo /
 appā danto suhī hoi | assiṃ loe parattha ya 
 vari me appā danto | saṃjameṇa taveṇa ya /
 māhaṃ parehi dammanto | bandhaṇehi vahehi ya 
 paḍaṇīyaṃ ca buddhāṇaṃ | vāyā aduva kammuṇā /
 āvī vā jai vā rahasse | neva kujjā kayāi vi 
 na pakkhao na purao | neva kiccāṇa piṭhao /
 na juṃje ūruṇā ūruṃ | sayaṇe no paḍissuṇe 
 neva palhatthiyaṃ kujjā | pakkhapiṇḍaṃ ca saṃjae /
 pāe pasārie vāvi | na ciṭhe guruṇantie 
 āyāriehiṃ vāhitto | tusiṇīo na kayāi vi /
 pasāyapehī niyāgaṭhī | uvaciṭhe guruṃ sayā 
 ālavante lavante vā | na nisīejja kayāi vi /
 caiūṇam āsaṇaṃ dhīro | jao jattaṃ paḍissuṇe 
 āsaṇagao na pucchejjā | neva sejjāgao kayā /
 āgammukkuḍuo santo | pucchijjā paṃjalīuḍo 
 evaṃ viṇayajuttassa | suttaṃ atthaṃ ca tadubhayaṃ /
 pucchamāṇassa sīsassa | vāgarijja jahāsuyaṃ 
 musaṃ parihare bhikkhū | na ya ohāriṇiṃ vae /
 bhāsādosaṃ parihare | māyaṃ ca vajjae sayā 
 na lavejja puṭho sāvajjaṃ | na niraṭhaṃ na mammayaṃ /
 appaṇaṭhā paraṭhā vā | ubhayassantareṇa vā 
 samaresu agāresu | sandhīsu ya mahāpahe /
 ego egatthie saddhiṃ | neva ciṭhe na saṃlave 
 jam me buddhāṇusāsanti | sīeṇa pharuseṇa vā /
 mama lābho tti pehāe | payao taṃ paḍissuṇe 
 aṇusāsaṇam ovāyaṃ | dukkaḍassa ya coyaṇaṃ /
 hiyaṃ taṃ maṇṇaī paṇṇo | besaṃ hoi asāhuṇo 
 hiyaṃ vigayabhayā buddhā | pharusaṃ pi aṇusāsaṇaṃ /
 besaṃ taṃ hoi mūḍhāṇaṃ | khantisohikaraṃ payaṃ 
 āsaṇe uvaciṭhejjā | aṇucce akue thire /
 appuṭhāī niruṭhāī | nisīejjappakukkue 
 kāleṇa nikkhame bhikkhū | kāleṇa ya paḍikkame /
 akālaṃ ca vivajjittā | kāle kālaṃ samāyare 
 parivāḍīe na ciṭhejjā | bhikkhū dattesaṇaṃ care /
 paḍirūveṇa esittā | miyaṃ kāleṇa bhakkhae 
 nāidūramaṇāsanne | nannesiṃ cakkhuphāsao /
 ego ciṭhejja bhattaṭhā | laṃghiyā taṃ naikkame 
 nāiucce na nīe vā | nāsanne nāidūrao /
 phāsuyaṃ parakaḍaṃ piṇḍaṃ | paḍigāhejja saṃjae 
 appapāṇe 'ppabīyaṃmi | paḍicchannaṃmi saṃvuḍe /
 samayaṃ saṃjae bhuṃje | jayaṃ aparisāḍiyaṃ 
 sukaḍi tti supakki tti | succhinne suhaḍe maḍe /
 suṇiṭhie suladdhi tti | sāvajjaṃ vajjae muṇī 
 ramae paṇḍie sāsaṃ | hayaṃ bhaddaṃ va vāhae /
 bālaṃ sammai sāsanto | galiyassaṃ va vāhae 
 khaḍḍuyā me caveḍā me | akkosā ya vahā ya me /
 kallāṇam aṇusāsanto | pāvadiṭhi tti mannaī 
 putto me bhāya nāi tti | sāhū kallāṇa mannaī /
 pāvadiṭhi u appāṇaṃ | sāsaṃ dāsu tti mannaī 
 na kovae āyariyaṃ | appāṇaṃ pi na kovae /
 buddhovaghāī na siyā | na siyā tottagavesae 
 āyariyaṃ kuviyaṃ naccā | pattieṇa pasāyae /
 vijjhavejja paṃjalīuḍo | vaejja na puṇu tti ya 
 dhammajjiyaṃ ca vavahāraṃ | buddhehāyariyaṃ sayā /
 tam āyaranto vavahāraṃ | garahaṃ nābhigacchaī 
 maṇogayaṃ vakkagayaṃ | jāṇittāyariyassa u /
 taṃ parigijjha vāyāe | kammuṇā uvavāyae 
 vitte acoie niccaṃ | khippaṃ havai sucoie /
 jahovaiṭhaṃ sukayaṃ | kiccāiṃ kuvvaī sayā 
 naccā nayai mehāvī | loe kittī se jāyae /
 havaī kiccāṇaṃ saraṇaṃ | bhūyāṇaṃ jagaī jahā 
 pujjā jassa pasīyanti | saṃbuddhā puvvasaṃthuyā /
 pasannā lābhaissanti | viulaṃ aṭhiyaṃ suyaṃ 
 sa pujjasatthe suviṇīyasaṃsae | maṇoruī ciṭhai kammasaṃpayā /
 tavosamāyārisamāhisaṃvuḍe | mahajjuī paṃca vayāiṃ pāliyā 
 sa devagandhavvamaṇussapūie | caittu dehaṃ malapaṃkapuvvayaṃ /
 siddhe vā havai sāsae | deve vā apparae mahiḍḍhie  tti bemi ||
                  || viṇaya-suyaṃ samattaṃ 

U/2 parīsahajjhayaṇaṃ dvitīyam adhyayanam /

suyaṃ me āusaṃ teṇaṃ bhagavayā evam akkhāyaṃ | iha khalu 
bāvīsaṃ parīsahā samaṇeṇaṃ bhagavayā mahāvīreṇaṃ kāsaveṇaṃ 
 paveiyā, je bhikkhū soccā naccā jiccā abhibhūya bhikkhāyariyāe 
 paricvvayanto puṭho no niṇhavejjā | kayare te 
khalu bāvīsaṃ parīsahā samaṇeṇaṃ bhagavayā mahāvīreṇaṃ 
 kāsaveṇaṃ paveiyā, je bhikkhū soccā naccā jiccā abhibhūya 
bhikkhāyariyāe parivvayanto puṭho no niṇhavejjā | ime te 
khalu bāvīsaṃ parīsahā samaṇeṇaṃ bhagavayā mahāvīreṇaṃ kāsaveṇaṃ 
 paveiyā, je bhikkhū soccā naccā jiccā abhibhūya bhikkhāyariyāe 
 parivvayanto puṭho no niṇhavejjā | taṃ jahā 
digiṃchāparīsahe 1 pivāsāparīsahe 2 sīyaparīsahe 3 usiṇaparīsahe 4 
daṃsamasayaparīsahe 5 acelaparīsahe 6 araiparīsahe 7 
itthīparīsahe 8 cariyāparīsahe 9 nisīhiyāparīsahe 10 
sejjāparīsahe 11 akkosaparīsahe 12 vahaparīsahe 13 
jāyaṇāparīsahe 14 alābhaparīsahe 15 rogaparīsahe 16 
taṇaphāsaparīsahe 17 jallaparīsahe  18 sakkārapurakkāraparīsahe 19 
pannā-parīsahe 20 annāṇaparīsahe 21 daṃsaṇaparīsahe 22    
     parīsahāṇaṃ pavibhattī | kāsaveṇaṃ paveiyā /
     taṃ bhe udāharissāmi | āṇupuvviṃ suṇeha me 
   1 digiṃchāparigae dehe | tavassī bhikkhū thāmavaṃ /
     na chinde na chindāvae | na pae na payāvae 
     kālīpavvaṃgasaṃkāse | kise dhamaṇisaṃtae /
     māyanne asaṇapāṇassa | adīṇamaṇaso care 
   2 tao puṭho pivāsāe | doguṃchī lajjasaṃjae /
     sīodagaṃ na sevijjā | viyaḍassesaṇaṃ care 
     chinnāvāesu panthesu | āure supivāsie /
     parisukkhamuhadīṇe | taṃ titikkhe parīsahaṃ 
   3 carantaṃ virayaṃ lūhaṃ | sīyaṃ phusai egayā /
     nāivelaṃ muṇī gacche | soccāṇaṃ jiṇasāsaṇaṃ 
     na me nivāraṇam atthi | chavittāṇaṃ na vijjaī /
     ahe tu aggiṃ sevāmi | ii bhikkhū na cintae 
   4 usiṇaṃ pariyāveṇaṃ | paridāheṇa tajjie /
     ghiṃsu vā pariyāveṇaṃ | sāyaṃ no paridevae 
     uṇhāhitatte mehāvī | siṇāṇaṃ vi no patthae /
     gāyaṃ no parisiṃcejjā | na vīejjā ya appayaṃ 
   5 puṭho ya daṃsamasaehiṃ | samareva mahāmuṇī /
     nāgo saṃgāmasīse vā | sūro abhihaṇe paraṃ 
     na saṃtase na vārejjā | maṇaṃ pi na paosae /
     uvehe na haṇe pāṇe | bhuṃjante maṃsasoṇiyaṃ 
   6 parijuṇṇehi vatthehiṃ | hokkhāmi tti acelae /
     aduvā sacele hokkhāmi | ii bhikkhū na cintae 
     egayācelae hoi | sacele āvi egayā /
     eyaṃ dhammahiyaṃ naccā | nāṇī no paridevae 
   7 gāmāṇugāmaṃ rīyantaṃ | aṇagāraṃ akiṃcaṇaṃ /
     araī aṇuppavesejjā | taṃ titikkhe parīsahaṃ 
     araiṃ piṭhao kiccā | virae āyarakkhie /
     dhammārāme nirārambhe | uvasante muṇī care 
   8 saṃgo esa maṇūsāṇaṃ | jāo logaṃmi itthio /
     jassa eyā parinnāyā | sukaḍaṃ tassa sāmaṇṇaṃ 
     eyam ādāya mehāvī | paṃkabhūyā u itthio /
     no tāhiṃ viṇihammejjā | carejjattagavesae 
   9 ega eva care lāḍhe | abhibhūya parīsahe /
     gāme vā nagare vāvi | nigame vā rāyahāṇie 
     asamāṇe care bhikkhū | neva kujjā pariggahaṃ /
     asaṃsatte gihatthehiṃ | aṇieo parivvae 
  10 susāṇe sunnagāre vā | rukkhamūle va egao /
     akukkuo nisīejjā | na ya vittāsae paraṃ 
     tattha se ciṭhamāṇassa | uvasaggābhidhārae /
     saṃkābhīo na gacchejjā | uṭhittā annam āsaṇaṃũ
  11 uccāvayāhiṃ sejjāhiṃ | tavassī bhikkhu thāmavaṃ /
     nāivelaṃ vihammejjā | pāvadiṭhī vihammaī 
     pairikkuvassayaṃ laddhuṃ | kallāṇam aduvā pāvayaṃ /
     kim egarāiṃ karissai | evaṃ tattha 'hiyāsae 
  12 akkosejjā pare bhikkhuṃ | na tesiṃ paḍisaṃjale /
     sariso hoi bālāṇaṃ | tamhā bhikkhū na saṃjale 
     soccāṇaṃ pharusā bhāsā | dāruṇā gāmakaṇagā /
     tusiṇīo uvehejjā | na tāo maṇasī kare 
  13 hao na saṃjale bhikkhū | maṇaṃ pi na paosae /
     titikkhaṃ paramaṃ naccā | bhikkhū dhammaṃ samāyare 
     samaṇaṃ saṃjayaṃ dantaṃ | haṇejjā koi katthaī /
     natthi jīvassa nāsu tti | evaṃ pehejja saṃjae 
  14 dukkaraṃ khalu bho niccaṃ | aṇagārassa bhikkhuṇo /
     savvaṃ se jāiyaṃ hoi | natthi kiṃci ajāiyaṃ 
     goyaraggapaviṭhassa | pāṇī no suppasārae /
     seo agāravāsu tti | ii bhikkhū na cintae 
  15 paresu ghāsam esejjā | bhoyaṇe pariṇiṭhie /
     laddhe piṇḍe aladdhe vā | nāṇutappejja paṇḍie 
     ajjevāhaṃ na labbhāmi | avi lābho sue siyā /
     jo evaṃ paḍisaṃcikkhe | alābho taṃ na tajjae 
  16 naccā uppaiyaṃ dukkhaṃ | veyaṇāe duhaṭhie /
     adīṇo thāvae pannaṃ | puṭho tatthahiyāsae 
     teicchaṃ nābhinandejjā | saṃcikkhattagavesae /
     evaṃ khu tassa sāmaṇṇaṃ | jaṃ na kujjā na kārave 
  17 acelagassa lūhassa | saṃjayassa tavassiṇo /
     taṇesu sayamāṇassa | hujjā gāyavirāhaṇā 
     āyavassa nivāeṇa | aulā havai veyaṇā /
     evaṃ naccā na sevanti | tantujaṃ taṇatajjiyā 
  18 kilinnagāe mehāvī | paṃkeṇa va raeṇa vā /
     ghiṃsu vā pariyāveṇa | sāyaṃ no paridevae 
     veejja nijjarāpehī | āriyaṃ dhammaṇuttaraṃ /
     jāva sarīrabheu tti | jallaṃ kāeṇa dhārae 
  19 abhivāyaṇam abbhuṭhāṇaṃ | sāmī kujjā nimantaṇaṃ /
     je tāiṃ paḍisevanti | na tesiṃ pīhae muṇī 
     aṇukkasāī appicche | annāesī alolue /
     rasesu nāṇugijjhejjā | nāṇutappejja pannavaṃ 
  20 se nūṇaṃ mae puvvaṃ | kammāṇāṇaphalā kaḍā /
     jeṇāhaṃ nābhijāṇāmi | puṭho keṇai kaṇhuī 
     aha pacchā uijjanti | kammāṇāṇaphalā kaḍā /
     evam assāsi appāṇaṃ | naccā kammavivāgayaṃ 
  21 niraṭhagammi virao | mehuṇāo susaṃvuḍo /
     jo sakkhaṃ nābhijāṇāmi | dhammaṃ kallāṇapāvagaṃ 
     tavovahāṇam ādāya | paḍimaṃ paḍivajjao /
     evaṃ pi viharao me | chaumaṃ na niyaaī 
  22 natthi nūṇaṃ pare loe | iḍḍhī vāvi tavassiṇo /
     aduvā vaṃcio mi tti | ii bhikkhū na cintae 
     abhū jiṇā atthi jiṇā | aduvā vi bhavissaī /
     musaṃ te evam āhaṃsu | ii bhikkhū na cintae 
     ee parīsahā savve | kāsaveṇa niveiyā /
     je bhikkhū na vihammejjā | puṭho keṇai kaṇhuī  tti bemi ||     
          || parīsahajjhayaṇaṃ samattaṃ 

U/3 cāuraṃgijjaṃ tṛtīyam adhyayanam /
        
cattāri param aṃgāṇi | dullahāṇīha jantuṇo /
māṇusattaṃ suī saddhā | saṃjamaṃmi ya vīriyaṃ 
samāvannāṇa saṃsāre | nāṇāgottāsu jāisu /
kammā nāṇāvihā kau | puḍho vissaṃbhiyā payā 
egayā devaloesu | naraesu vi egayā /
egayā āsuraṃ kāyaṃ | āhākammehiṃ gacchaī 
egayā khattio hoi | tao caṇḍālavokkaso /
tao kīḍapayaṃgo ya | tao kunthupivīliyā 
evam āvaajoṇīsu | pāṇiṇo kammakivvisā /
na nivijjanti saṃsāre | savvaṭhesu va khattiyā 
kammasaṃgehiṃ sammūḍhā | dukkhiyā bahuveyaṇā /
amāṇusāsu joṇīsu | viṇihammanti pāṇiṇo 
kammāṇaṃ tu pahāṇāe | āṇupuvvī kayāi u /
jīvā sohim aṇuppattā | āyayanti maṇussayaṃ 
māṇussaṃ viggahaṃ laddhuṃ | suī dhammassa dullahā /
jaṃ soccā paḍivajjanti | tavaṃ khantim ahiṃsayaṃ 
āhacca savaṇaṃ laddhuṃ | saddhā paramadullahā /
soccā neāuyaṃ maggaṃ | bahave paribhassaī 
suiṃ ca laddhuṃ saddhaṃ ca | vīriyaṃ puṇa dullahaṃ /
bahave royamāṇā vi | no ya -aṃ paḍivajjae 
māṇusattaṃmi āyāo | jo dhammaṃ socca saddahe /
tavassī vīriyaṃ laddhuṃ | saṃvuḍe niddhuṇe rayaṃ 
sohī ujjuyabhūyassa | dhammo suddhassa ciṭhaī /
nivvāṇaṃ paramaṃ jāi | ghayasitti vva pāvae 
vigiṃca kammuṇo heuṃ | jasaṃ saṃciṇu khantie /
sarīraṃ pāḍhavaṃ hiccā | uḍḍhaṃ pakkamaī disaṃ 
visālisehiṃ sīlehiṃ | jakkhā uttarauttarā /
mahāsukkā va dippantā | mannantā apuṇaccavaṃ 
appiyā devakāmāṇaṃ | kāmarūvaviuvviṇo /
uḍḍhaṃ kappesu ciṭhanti | puvvā vāsasayā bahū 
tattha ṭhiccā jahāṭhāṇaṃ | jakkhā āukkhae cuyā /
uventi māṇusaṃ joṇiṃ | se dasaṃge 'bhijāyaī 
khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraṇṇaṃ ca | pasavo dāsaporusaṃ /
cattāri kāmakhandhāṇi | tattha se uvavajjaī 
mittavaṃ nāyavaṃ hoi | uccāgoe ya vaṇṇavaṃ /
appāyake mahāpanne | abhijāe jasobale 
bhoccā māṇussae bhoe | appaḍirūve ahāuyaṃ /
puvviṃ visuddhasaddhamme | kevalaṃ bohi bujjhiyā 
cauraṃgaṃ dullahaṃ mattā | saṃjamaṃ paḍivajjiyā /
tavasā dhuyakammaṃse | siddhe havai sāsae  tti bemi ||
      || cāuraṃgijjaṃ samattaṃ 

U/4 asaṃkhayaṃ catuturthaṃ adhyayanam /
    
asaṃkhayaṃ jīviya mā pamāyae | jarovaṇīyassa hu natthi tāṇaṃ /
evaṃ vijāṇāhi jaṇe pamatte | ki- -ū vihiṃsā ajayā gahinti 
je pāvakammehi dhaṇaṃ maṇūsā | samāyayantī amaiṃ gahāya /
pahāya te pāsapayaie nare | verāṇubaddhā narayaṃ uventi 
teṇe jahā sandhimuhe gahīe | sakammuṇā kiccai pāvakārī /
evaṃ payā pecca ihaṃ ca loe | kaḍāṇa kammāṇa na mukkha atthi 
saṃsāram āvanna parassa aṭhā | sāhāraṇaṃ jaṃ ca karei kammaṃ /
kammassa te tassa u veyakāle | na bandhavā bandhavayaṃ uventi 
vitteṇa tāṇaṃ na labhe pamatte | imaṃmi loe aduvā paratthā /
dīvappaṇaṭhe va aṇantamohe | neyāuyaṃ daṭhum adaṭhum eva 
sattesu yāvī paḍibuddhajīvī | na vīsase paṇḍie āsupanne /
ghorā muhuttā abalaṃ sarīraṃ | bhāruṇḍapakkhī va carappamatte 
care payāiṃ parisaṃkamāṇo | jaṃ kiṃci pāsaṃ iha maṇṇamāṇo /
lābhantare jīviya vūhaittā | pacchā parinnāya malāvadhaṃsī 
chandaṃniroheṇa uvei mokkhaṃ | āse jahā sikkhiya vammadhārī /
puvvāiṃ vāsāiṃ carappamatte | tamhā muṇī khippam uvei mokkhaṃ 
sa puvvam evaṃ na labhejja pacchā | esovamā sāsayavāiyāṇaṃ /
visīyaī siḍhile āuyaṃmi | kālovaṇīe sarīrassa bhee 
khippaṃ na sakkei vivegameuṃ | tamhā samuṭhāya pahāya kāme /
samicca loyaṃ samayā mahesī | āyāṇurakkhī caramappamatte 
muhuṃ muhuṃ mohaguṇe jayantaṃ | aṇegarūvā samaṇaṃ carantaṃ /
phāṃsā phusantī asamaṃjasaṃ ca | na tesi bhikkhū maṇasā pausse 
mandā ya phāsā bahulohaṇijjā | tahappagāresu maṇaṃ na kujjā /
rakkhijja kohaṃ viṇaejja māṇaṃ | māyaṃ na seve payahejja lohaṃ 
je 'saṃkhayā tucchā parappavāī | te pijjadosāṇugayā parabbhā /
ee ahamme tti duguṃchamāṇo | kaṃkhe guṇe jāva sarīrabheu  tti bemi ||
        ||asaṃkhyaṃ samattaṃ 

U/5 akāmamaraṇijjaṃ pañcamaṃ adhyayanam /
     
aṇṇavaṃsi mahoghaṃsi | ege tiṇṇe duruttaraṃ /
tattha ege mahāpanne | imaṃ paṇham udāhare 
santime ya duve ṭhāṇā | akkhāyā māraṇantiyā /
akāmamaraṇaṃ ceva | sakāmamaraṇaṃ tahā 
bālāṇaṃ tu akāmaṃ tu | maraṇaṃ asaiṃ bhave /
paṇḍiyāṇaṃ sakāmaṃ tu | ukkoseṇa saiṃ bhave 
tatthimaṃ paḍhamaṃ ṭhāṇaṃ | mahāvīreṇa desiyaṃ /
kāmagiddhe jahā bāle | bhisaṃ kūrāiṃ kuvvaī 
je giddhe kāmabhogesu | ege kūḍāya gacchaī /
na me diṭhe pare loe | cakkhudiṭhā imā raī 
hatthāgayā ime kāmā | kāliyā je aṇāgayā /
ko jāṇai pare loe | atthi vā natthi vā puṇo 
jaṇeṇa saddhiṃ hokkhāmi | ii bāle pagabbhaī /
kāmabhogāṇurāeṇaṃ | kesaṃ saṃpaḍivajjaī 
tao se daṇḍaṃ samārabhaī | tasesu thāvaresu ya /
aṭhāe ya aṇaṭhāe | bhūyagāmaṃ vihiṃsaī 
hiṃse bāle musāvāī | māille pisuṇe saḍhe /
bhuṃjamāṇe suraṃ maṃsaṃ | seyam eyaṃ ti mannaī 
kāyasā vayasā matte | vitte giddhe ya itthisu /
duhao malaṃ saṃciṇai | siṃsuṇāgu vva maiyaṃ 
tao puṭho āyaṃkeṇaṃ | gilāṇo paritappaī /
pabhīo paralogassa | kammāṇuppehi appaṇo 
suyā me narae ṭhāṇā | asīlāṇaṃ ca jā gaī /
bālāṇaṃ kūrakammāṇaṃ | pagāḍhā jattha veyaṇā 
tatthovavāiyaṃ ṭhāṇaṃ | jahā meyam aṇussuyaṃ /
āhākammehiṃ gacchanto | so pacchā paritappaī 
jahā sāgaḍio jāṇaṃ | samaṃ hiccā mahāpahaṃ /
visamaṃ maggam oiṇṇo | akkhe bhaggaṃmi soyaī 
evaṃ dhammaṃ viukkammaṃ | ahammaṃ paḍivajjiyā /
bāle maccumuhaṃ patte | akkhe bhagge va soyaī 
tao sa maraṇantaṃmi | bāle santasaī bhayā /
akāmamaraṇaṃ maraī | dhutte va kalinā jie 
eyaṃ akāmamaraṇaṃ | bālāṇaṃ tu paveiyaṃ /
etto sakāmamaraṇaṃ | paṇḍiyāṇaṃ suṇeha me 
maraṇaṃ pi sapuṇṇāṇaṃ | jahā meyam aṇussuyaṃ /
vippasaṇṇam aṇāghāyaṃ | saṃjayāṇa vusīmao 
na imaṃ savvesu bhikkhūsu | na imaṃ savvesu 'gārisu /
nāṇāsīlā agāratthā | visamasīlā ya bhikkhuṇo 
santi egehiṃ bhikkhūhiṃ | gāratthā saṃjam uttarā /
gāratthehi ya savvehiṃ | sāhavo saṃjam uttarā 
cīrājiṇaṃ nagiṇiṇaṃ | jaḍī saṃghāḍimuṇḍiṇaṃ /
eyāṇi vi na tāyanti | dussīlaṃ pariyāgayaṃ 
piṇḍola evva dussīle | naragāo na muccaī /
bhikkhāe vā gihatthe vā | suvvae kammaī divaṃ 
agārisāmāiyaṃgāṇi | saḍḍhī kāeṇa phāsae /
posahaṃ duhao pakkhaṃ | egarāyaṃ na hāvae 
evaṃ sikkhāsamāvanne | gihivāse vi suvvae /
muccaī chavipavvāo | gacche jakkhasalogayaṃ 
aha je saṃvuḍe bhikkhū | doṇhaṃ annayare siyā /
savvadukkhapahīṇe vā | deve vāvi mahiḍḍhie 
uttarāiṃ vimohāiṃ | juīmantāṇupuvvaso /
samāiṇṇāiṃ jakkhehiṃ | āvāsāiṃ jasaṃsiṇo 
dīhāuyā iḍḍhimantā | samiddhā kāmarūviṇo /
ahuṇovavannasaṃkāsā | bhujjo accimalippabhā 
tāṇi ṭhāṇāṇi gacchanti | sikkhittā saṃjamaṃ tavaṃ /
bhikkhāge vā gihitthe vā | je santi paḍinivvuḍā 
tesiṃ soccā sapujjāṇaṃ | saṃjayāṇa vusīmao /
na saṃtasanti maraṇante | sīlavantā bahussuyā 
tuliyā visesamādāya | dayādhammassa khantie /
vippasīejja mehāvī | tahābhūeṇa appaṇā 
tao kāle abhippee | saḍḍhī tālisamantie /
viṇaejja lomaharisaṃ | bheyaṃ dehassa kaṃkhae 
aha kālaṃmi saṃpatte | āghāyāya samussayaṃ /
sakāmamaraṇaṃ maraī | tiṇham annayaraṃ muṇī  tti bemi ||
       || akāmamaraṇijjaṃ samattaṃ 

U/6 khuḍḍāganiyaṇṭhijjaṃ ṣaṣṭham adhyayanam /
    
jāvantavijjāpurisā | savve te dukkhasaṃbhavā /
luppanti bahuso mūḍhā | saṃsāraṃmi aṇantae 
samikkha paṃḍie tamhā | pāsajāī pahe bahū /
appaṇā saccam esejjā | mettiṃ bhūesu kappae 
māyā piyā nhusā bhāyā | bhajjā puttā ya orasā /
nālaṃ te mama tāṇāe | luppantassa sakammuṇā 
eyam aṭhaṃ sapehāe | pāse samiyadaṃsaṇe /
chinda geddhiṃ siṇehaṃ ca | na kaṃkhe puvvasaṃthuyaṃ 
gavāsaṃ maṇikuṃḍalaṃ | pasavo dāsaporusaṃ /
savvam eyaṃ caittāṇaṃ | kāmarūvī bhavissasi 
ajjhatthaṃ savvao savvaṃ | dissa pāṇe piyāyae /
na haṇe pāṇiṇo pāṇe | bhayaverāo uvarae 
āyāṇaṃ narayaṃ dissa | nāyaejja taṇām avi /
doguṃchī appaṇo pāe | dinnaṃ bhuṃjejja bhoyaṇaṃ 
iham ege u mannanti | appaccakkhāya pāvagaṃ /
āyāriyaṃ vidittāṇaṃ | savvadukkhāṇa muccaī 
bhaṇantā akarentā ya | bandhamokkhapaiṇṇiṇo /
vāyāviriyametteṇa | samāsāsenti appayaṃ 
na cittā tāyae bhāsā | kuo vijjāṇusāsaṇaṃ /
visannā pāvakammehiṃ | bālā paṃḍiyamāṇiṇo 
je kei sarīre sattā | vaṇṇe rūve ya savvaso /
maṇasā kāyavakkeṇaṃ | savve te dukkhasanbhavā 
āvannā dīham addhāṇaṃ | saṃsāraṃmi aṇantae /
tamhā savvadisaṃ passaṃ | appamatto parivvae 
bahiyā uḍḍham ādāya | nāvakaṃkhe kayāi vi /
puvvakammakhayaṭhāe | imaṃ dehaṃ samuddhare 
vivicca kammuṇo heuṃ | kālakaṃkhī parivvae /
māyaṃ piṃḍassa pāṇassa | kaḍaṃ laddhūṇa bhakkhae 
sannihiṃ ca na kuvvejjā | levamāyāe saṃjae /
pakkhī pattaṃ samādāya | niravekkho parivvae 
esaṇāsamio lajjū | gāme aṇiyao care /
appamatto pamattehiṃ | piṃḍavāyaṃ gavesae 
      || khuḍḍāganiyaṃṭhijjaṃ samattaṃ 
            
U/7 elayaṃ saptamam adhyayanam /
       
jahāesaṃ samuddissa | koi posejja elayaṃ /
oyaṇaṃ javasaṃ dejjā | posejjā vi sayaṃgaṇe 
tao se puṭhe parivūḍhe | jāyamee mahodare /
pīṇie viule dehe | āesaṃ parikaṃkhae 
jāva na ei āese | tāva jīvai so duhī /
aha pattaṃmi āese | sīsaṃ chettūṇa bhujjaī 
jahā se khalu urabbhe | āesāe samīhie /
evaṃ bāle ahammiṭhe | īhaī narayāuyaṃ 
hiṃse bāle musāvāī | addhāṇaṃsi vilovae /
annadattahare teṇe | māī kaṃ nu hare saḍhe 
itthīvisayagiddhe ya | mahāraṃbhapariggahe /
bhuṃjamāṇe suraṃ maṃsaṃ | parivūḍhe paraṃdame 
ayakakkarabhoī ya | tuṃḍille ciyalohie /
āuyaṃ narae kaṃkhe | jahāesaṃ va elae 
āsaṇaṃ sayaṇaṃ jāṇaṃ | vittaṃ kāme ya bhuṃjiyā /
dussāhaḍaṃ dhaṇaṃ hiccā | bahuṃ saṃciṇiyā rayaṃ 
tao kammagurū jantū | paccuppannaparāyaṇe /
aya vva āgayāese | maraṇantaṃmi soyaī 
tao āuparikkhīṇe | cuyā dehā vihiṃsagā /
āsurīyaṃ disaṃ bālā | gacchanti avasā tamaṃ 
jahā kāgaṇie heuṃ | sahassaṃ hārae naro /
apacchaṃ ambagaṃ bhoccā | rāyā rajjaṃ tu hārae 
evaṃ māṇussagā kāmā | devakāmāṇa antie /
sahassaguṇiyā bhujjo | āuṃ kāmā ya divviyā 
aṇegavāsānauyā | jā sā pannavao ṭhiī /
jāṇi jīyanti dummehā | ūṇavāsayāue 
jahā ya tinni vāṇiyā | mūlaṃ ghettūṇa niggayā /
ego 'ttha lahaī lābhaṃ | ego mūleṇa āgao 
ego mūlaṃ pi hārittā | āgao tattha vāṇio /
vavahāre uvamā esā | evaṃ dhamme viyāṇaha 
māṇusattaṃ bhave mūlaṃ | lābho devagaī bhave /
mūlaccheeṇa jīvāṇaṃ | naragatirikkhattaṇaṃ dhuvaṃ 
duhao gaī bālassa | āvaī vahamūliyā /
devattaṃ māṇusattaṃ ca | jaṃ jie lolayāsaḍhe 
tao jie saī hoi | duvihaṃ doggaiṃ gae /
dullahā tassa ummuggā | addhāe suirādavi 
evaṃ jiyaṃ sapehāe | tuliyā bālaṃ ca paṃḍiyaṃ /
mūliyaṃ te pavesanti | māṇusiṃ joṇim enti je 
vemāyāhiṃ sikkhāhiṃ | je narā gihisuvvayā /
uventi māṇusaṃ joṇiṃ | kammasaccā hu pāṇiṇo 
jesiṃ tu viulā sikkhā | mūliyaṃ te aicchithā /
sīlavantā savīsesā | adīṇā janti devayaṃ 
evam addīṇavaṃ bhikkhuṃ | āgāriṃ ca viyāṇiyā /
kaha- -u jiccam elikkhaṃ | jiccamāṇe na saṃvide 
jahā kusagge udagaṃ | samuddeṇa samaṃ miṇe /
evaṃ māṇussagā kāmā | devakāmāṇa antie 
kusaggamettā ime kāmā | sanniruddhaṃmi āue /
kassa heuṃ purākāuṃ | jogakkhemaṃ na saṃvide 
iha kāmāṇiyaṭhassa | attaṭhe avarajjhaī /
soccā neyāuyaṃ maggaṃ | jaṃ bhujjo paribhassaī 
iha kāmaṇiyaṭhassa | attaṭhe nāvarajjhaī /
pūidehaniroheṇaṃ | bhave devi tti me suyaṃ 
iḍḍhī juī jaso vaṇṇo | āuṃ suham aṇuttaraṃ /
bhujjo jattha maṇussesu | tattha se uvavajjaī 
bālassa passa bālattaṃ | ahammaṃ paḍivajjiyā /
ciccā dhammaṃ ahammiṭhe | narae uvavajjaī 
dhīrassa passa dhīrattaṃ | saccadhammāṇuvattiṇo /
ciccā adhammaṃ dhammiṭhe | devesu uvavajjaī 
tuliyāṇa bālabhāvaṃ | abālaṃ ceva paṇḍie /
caiūṇa bālabhāvaṃ | abālaṃ sevaī muṇi  tti bemi ||
      || elayajjhayaṇaṃ samattaṃ 

U/8 kāvilīyaṃ aṣamam adhyayanam /
     
adhuve asāsayaṃmī | saṃsāraṃmi dukkhapaurāe /
kiṃ nāma hojja taṃ kammayaṃ | jeṇāhaṃ doggaiṃ na gacchejjā 
vijahittu puvvasaṃjoyaṃ | na siṇehaṃ kahiṃci kuvvejjā /
asiṇehasiṇehakarehiṃ | dosapaosehi muccae bhikkhū 
to nāṇadaṃsaṇasamaggo | hiyanissesāya savvajīvāṇaṃ /
tesiṃ vimokkhaṇaṭhāe | bhāsaī muṇivaro vigayamoho 
savvaṃ ganthaṃ kalahaṃ ca | vippajahe tahāvihaṃ bhikkhū /
savvesu kāmajāesu | pāsamāṇo na lippaī tāī 
bhogāmisadosavisanne | hiyanisseyasabuddhivoccatthe /
bāle ya mandie mūḍhe | bajjhaī macchiyā va khelaṃmi 
dupariccayā ime kāmā | no sujahā adhīrapurisehiṃ /
aha santi suvvayā sāhū | je taranti ataraṃ vaṇiyā vā 
samaṇā mu ege vayamāṇā | pāṇavahaṃ miyā ayāṇantā /
mandā nirayaṃ gacchanti | bālā pāviyāhiṃ diṭhīhiṃ 
na hu pāṇavahaṃ aṇujāṇe | muccejja kayāi savvadukkhāṇaṃ /
evāriehiṃ akkhāyaṃ | jehiṃ imo sāhudhammo pannatto 
pāṇe ya nāivāejjā | se samīi tti vuccaī tāī /
tao se pāvayaṃ kammaṃ | nijjāi udagaṃ va thalāo 
jaganissiehiṃ bhūehiṃ | tasanāmehiṃ thāvarehiṃ ca /
no tesim ārabhe daṃḍaṃ | maṇasā vayasā kāyasā ceva 
suddhesaṇāo naccāṇaṃ | tattha ṭhavejja bhikkhū appāṇaṃ /
jāyāe ghāsam esejjā | rasagiddhe na siyā bhikkhāe 
pantāṇi ceva sevejjā | sīyapiṃḍaṃ purāṇakummāsaṃ /
adu vakkasaṃ pulāgaṃ vā | javaṇaṭhāe nisevae maṃghuṃ 
je lakkhaṇaṃ ca suviṇaṃ | aṃgavijjaṃ ca je pauṃjanti /
na hu te samaṇā vuccanti | evaṃ āyariehiṃ akkhāyaṃ 
ihajīviyaṃ aṇiyamettā | pabhaṭhā samāhijoehiṃ /
te kāmabhogarasagiddhā | uvavajjanti āsure kāe 
tatto vi ya uvvaittā | saṃsāraṃ bahuṃ aṇupariyaḍanti /
bahukammalevalittāṇaṃ | bohī hoi sudullahā tesiṃ 
kasiṇaṃ pi jo imaṃ loyaṃ | paḍipuṇṇaṃ dalejja ikkassa /
teṇāvi se na saṃtusse | ii duppūrae ime āyā 
jahā lāhā tahā loho | lāhā loho pavaḍḍhaī /
domāsakayaṃ kajjaṃ | koḍīe vi na niṭhiyaṃ 
no rakkhasīsu gijjhejjā | gaṃḍavacchāsu 'egacittāsu /
jāo purisaṃ palobhittā | khellanti jahā va dāsehiṃ 
nārīsu novagijjhejjā | itthī vippajahe aṇāgāre /
dhammaṃ ca pesalaṃ naccā | tattha ṭhavejja bhikkhū appāṇaṃ 
ii esa dhamme akkhāe | kavileṇaṃ ca visuddhapanneṇaṃ /
tarihinti je u kāhinti | tehiṃ ārāhiyā duve loga  tti bemi ||
      || kāvilīyaṃ samattaṃ 
      
U/9 namipavvajjā navamam adhyayanam /
    
caiūṇa devalogāo | uvavanno māṇusaṃmi logaṃmi /
uvasantamohaṇijjo | saraī porāṇiyaṃ jāiṃ 
jāiṃ sarittu bhayavaṃ | sahasaṃbuddho aṇuttare dhamme /
puttaṃ ṭhavettu rajje | abhiṇikkhamaī namī rāyā 
se devalogasarise | anteuravaragao vare bhoe /
bhuṃjittu namī rāyā | budho bhoge pariccayaī 
mihilaṃ sapurajaṇavayaṃ | balam orohaṃ ca pariyaṇaṃ savvaṃ /
ciccā abhinikkhanto | egantam ahiḍḍhio bhayavaṃ 
kolāhalagabhūyaṃ | āsī mihilāe pavvayantaṃmi /
taiyā rāyarisiṃmi | namiṃmi abhiṇikkhamantaṃmi 
abbhuṭhiyaṃ rāyarisiṃ | pavvajjāṭhāṇam uttamaṃ /
sakko māhaṇarūveṇa | imaṃ vayaṇam abbavī 
ki- -u bho ajja mihilā | kolāhalagasaṃkulā /
suvvanti dāruṇā saddā | pāsāesu gihesu ya 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
mihilāe ceie vacche | sīyacchāe maṇorame /
pattapupphaphalovee | bahūṇaṃ bahuguṇe sayā 
vāeṇa hīramāṇaṃmi | ceiyaṃmi maṇorame /
duhiyā asaraṇā attā | ee kandanti bho khagā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
esa aggī ya vāū ya | eyaṃ ḍajjhai mandiraṃ /
bhayavaṃ anteuraṃ teṇaṃ | kīsa -aṃ nāvapekkhaha 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
suhaṃ vasāmo jīvāmo | jesi mo natthi kiṃcaṇa /
mihilāe ḍajjhamāṇīe | na me ḍajjhai kiṃcaṇa 
cattaputtakalattassa | nivvāvārassa bhikkhuṇo /
piyaṃ na vijjaī kiṃci | appiyaṃ pi na vijjaī 
bahuṃ khu muṇiṇo bhaddaṃ | aṇagārassa bhikkhuṇo /
savvao vippamukkassa | egantam aṇupassao 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
pāgāraṃ kāraittāṇaṃ | gopuraālagāṇi ca /
ussūlagasayagghīo | tao gacchasi khattiyā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
saddhaṃ nagaraṃ kiccā | tavasaṃvaram aggalaṃ /
khantiṃ niuṇapāgāraṃ | tiguttaṃ duppadhaṃsayaṃ 
dhaṇuṃ parakkamaṃ kiccā | jīvaṃ ca iriyaṃ sayā /
dhiiṃ ca keyaṇaṃ kiccā | sacceṇa palimanthae 
tavanārāyajutteṇa | bhittūṇaṃ kammakaṃcuyaṃ /
muṇī vigayasaṃgāmo | bhavāo parimuccae 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
pāsāe kāraittāṇaṃ | vaddhamāṇagihāṇi ya /
bālaggapoiyāo ya | tao gacchasi khattiyā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
saṃsayaṃ khalu so kuṇaī | jo maggo kuṇaī gharaṃ /
jattheva gantum icchejjā | tattha kuvvejja sāsayaṃ 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
āmose lomahāre ya | gaṃṭhibhee ya takkare /
nagarassa khemaṃ kāūṇaṃ | tao gacchasi khattiyā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
asaiṃ tu maṇussehiṃ | micchā daṃḍo pajuṃjaī /
akāriṇo 'ttha bajjhanti | muccaī kārao jaṇo 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
je kei patthivā tujjhaṃ | nānamanti narāhivā /
vase te ṭhāvaittāṇaṃ | tao gacchasi khattiyā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
jo sahassaṃ sahassāṇaṃ | saṃgāme dujjae jiṇe /
egaṃ jiṇejja appāṇaṃ | esa se paramo jao 
appāṇam eva jujjhāhi | kiṃ te jujjheṇa bajjhao /
appaṇāmevamappāṇaṃ | jaittā suham ehae 
paṃcindiyāṇi kohaṃ | māṇaṃ māyaṃ taheva lohaṃ ca /
dujjayaṃ ceva appāṇaṃ | savvaṃ appe jie jiyaṃ 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
jaittā viule janne | bhoittā samaṇamāhaṇe /
dattā bhoccā ya jiṭhā ya | tao gacchasi khattiyā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
jo sahassaṃ sahassāṇaṃ | māse māse gavaṃ dae /
tassa vi saṃjamo seo | adintassa vi kiṃcaṇa 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
ghorāsamaṃ caittāṇaṃ | annaṃ patthesi āsamaṃ /
iheva posaharao | bhavāhi maṇuyāhivā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
māse māse tu jo bālo | kusaggeṇa tu bhuṃjae /
na so sukkhāyadhammassa | kalaṃ agghai solasiṃ 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
hiraṇṇaṃ suvaṇṇaṃ maṇimuttaṃ | kaṃsaṃ dūsaṃ ca vāhaṇaṃ /
kosaṃ vaḍḍhāvaittāṇaṃ | tao gacchasi khattiyā 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
suvaṇṇaruppassa u pavvayā bhave | siyā hu kelāsasamā asaṃkhayā /
narassa luddhassa na tehiṃ kiṃci | icchā u āgāsasamā aṇantiyā 
puḍhavī sālī javā ceva | hiraṇṇaṃ pasubhis saha /
paḍipuṇṇaṃ nālam egassa | ii vijjā tavaṃ care 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namiṃ rāyarisiṃ | devindo iṇam abbavī 
accherayam abbhudae | bhoe cayasi patthivā /
asante kāme patthesi | saṃkappeṇa vihammasi 
eyam aṭhaṃ nisāmittā | heūkāraṇacoio /
tao namī rāyarisī | devindaṃ iṇam abbavī 
sallaṃ kāmā visaṃ kāmā | kāmā āsīvisovamā /
kāme patthemāṇā | akāmā janti doggaiṃ 
ahe vayanti koheṇaṃ | māṇeṇaṃ ahamā gaī /
māyā gaīpaḍigghāo | lobhāo duhao bhayaṃ 
avaujjhiūṇa māhaṇa | rūvaṃ viuvviūṇa indattaṃ /
vandai abhitthuṇanto | imāhi mahurāhiṃ vaggūhiṃ 
aho te nijjio koho | aho māṇo parājio /
aho nirakkiyā māyā | aho lobho vasīkao 
aho te ajjavaṃ sāhu | aho te sāhu maddavaṃ /
aho te uttamā khantī | aho te mutti uttamā 
ihaṃ si uttamo bhante | pacchā hohisi uttamo /
loguttam uttamaṃ ṭhāṇaṃ | siddhiṃ gacchasi nīrao 
evaṃ abhitthuṇanto | rāyarisiṃ uttamāe saddhāe /
payāhiṇaṃ karento | puṇo puṇo vandaī sakko 
to vandiūṇa pāe | cakkaṃkusalakkhaṇe muṇivarassa /
āgāseṇuppaio | laliyacalakuṃḍalatirīḍī 
namī namei appāṇaṃ | sakkhaṃ sakkeṇa coio /
caiūṇa gehaṃ vedehī | sāmaṇṇe pajjuvaṭhio 
evaṃ karenti saṃbuddhā | paṃḍiyā paviyakkhaṇā /
viṇiyaanti bhogesu | jahā se namī rāyarisī  tti bemi ||
      || namipavajjā samattā 

U/10 dumapattayaṃ daśamam adhyayanam ||
 
dumapattae paṇḍuyae jahā | nivaḍai rāigaṇāṇa accae /
evaṃ maṇuyāṇa jīviyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
kusagge jaha osabindue | thovaṃ ciṭhai lambamāṇae /
evaṃ maṇuyāṇa jīviyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
ii ittariyammi āue | jīviyae bahupaccavāyae /
vihuṇāhi rayaṃ pure kaḍaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
dullahe khalu māṇuse bhave | cirakāleṇa vi savvapāṇiṇaṃ /
gāḍhā ya vivāga kammuṇo | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
puḍhavikkāyamaigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālaṃ saṃkhāīyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
āukkāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālaṃ saṃkhāīyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
teukkāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālaṃ saṃkhāīyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
vāukkāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālaṃ saṃkhāīyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
vaṇassaikāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālam aṇantadurantayaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
beindiyakāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālaṃ saṃkhijjasanniyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
teindiyakāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālaṃ saṃkhijjasanniyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
caurindiyakāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
kālaṃ saṃkhijjasanniyaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
paṃcindiyakāyam aigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
sattaṭhabhavagahaṇe | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
deve neraie yamaigao | ukkosaṃ jīvo u saṃvase /
ikkekkabhavagahaṇe | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
evaṃ bhavasaṃsāre | saṃsarai suhāsuhehi kammehiṃ /
jīvo pamāyabahulo | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
laddhūṇa vi māṇusattaṇaṃ | āriattaṃ puṇarāvi dullahaṃ /
bahave dasuyā milakkhuyā | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
laddhūṇa vi āriyattaṇaṃ | ahīṇapaṃcendiyayā hu dullahā /
vigalindiyayā hu dīsaī | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
ahīṇapaṃcendiyattaṃ pi se lahe | uttamadhammasuī hu dullahā /
kutitthinisevae jaṇe | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
laddhūṇa vi uttamaṃ suiṃ | saddahaṇā puṇarāvi dullahā /
micchattanisevae jaṇe | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
dhammaṃ pi hu saddahantayā | dullahayā kāeṇa phāsayā /
iha kāmaguṇehi mucchiyā | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
parijūrai te sarīrayaṃ | kesā paṇḍurayā havanti te /
se soyabale ya hāyaī | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
parijūrai te sarīrayaṃ | kesā paṇḍurayā havanti te /
se cakkhubale ya hāyaī | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
parijūrai te sarīrayaṃ | kesā paṇḍurayā havanti te /
se ghāṇabale ya hāyaī | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
parijūrai te sarīrayaṃ | kesā paṇḍurayā havanti te /
se jibbhabale ya hāyaī | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
parijūrai te sarīrayaṃ | kesā paṇḍurayā havanti te /
se phāsabale ya hāyaī | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
parijūrai te sarīrayaṃ | kesā paṇḍurayā havanti te /
se savvabale ya hāyaī | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
araī gaṇḍaṃ visūiyā | āyaṃkā vivihā phusanti te /
vihaḍai viddhaṃsai te sarīrayaṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
vocchinda siṇeham appaṇo | kumuyaṃ sāraiyaṃ va pāṇiyaṃ /
se savvasiṇehavajjie | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
ciccāṇa dhaṇaṃ ca bhāriyaṃ | pavvaio hi si aṇagāriyaṃ /
mā vantaṃ puṇo vi āie | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
avaujjhiya mittabandhavaṃ | viulaṃ ceva dhaṇohasaṃcayaṃ /
mā taṃ biiyaṃ gavesae | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
na hu jiṇe ajja dissaī | bahumae dissai maggadesie /
saṃpai neyāue pahe | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
avasohiya kaṇagā pahaṃ | oiṇṇo si pahaṃ mahālayaṃ /
gacchasi maggaṃ visohiyā | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
abale jaha bhāravāhae | mā magge visame vagāhiyā /
pacchā pacchāṇutāvae | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
tiṇṇo hu si aṇṇavaṃ mahaṃ | kiṃ puṇa ciṭhasi tīram āgao /
abhitura pāraṃ gamittae | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
akalevaraseṇim ussiyā | siddhiṃ goyama loyaṃ gacchasi /
khemaṃ ca sivaṃ aṇuttaraṃ | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
buddhe parinivvuḍe care | gāmagae nagare va saṃjae /
santīmaggaṃ ca vūhae | samayaṃ goyama mā pamāyae 
buddhassa nisamma bhāsiyaṃ | sukahiyam aṭhapaovasohiyaṃ /
rāgaṃ dosaṃ ca chindiyā | siddhigaiṃ gae goyame  tti bemi ||
     || dumapattayaṃ samattaṃ 

U/11 bahussuyapujjam ekādaśaṃ adhyayanam ||

saṃjogā vippamukkassa | aṇagārassa bhikkhuṇo /
āyāraṃ pāukarissāmi | āṇupuvviṃ suṇeha me 
je yāvi hoi nivvijje | thaddhe luddhe aṇiggahe /
abhikkhaṇaṃ ullavaī | aviṇīe abahussue 
aha paṃcahiṃ ṭhāṇehiṃ | jehiṃ sikkhā na labbhaī /
thambhā kohā pamāeṇaṃ | rogeṇālassaeṇa ya 
aha aṭhahiṃ ṭhāṇehiṃ | sikkhāsīli tti vuccaī /
ahassire sayā dante | na ya mammam udāhare 
nāsīle na visīle | na siyā ailolue /
akohaṇe saccarae | sikkhāsīli tti vuccaī 
aha coddasahiṃ ṭhāṇehiṃ | vaamāṇe u saṃjae /
aviṇīe vuccaī so u | nivvāṇaṃ ca na gacchai 
abhikkhaṇaṃ kohī havai | pabandhaṃ ca pakuvvaī /
mettijjamāṇo vamai | suyaṃ laddhūṇa majjaī 
avi pāvaparikkhevī | avi mittesu kuppaī /
suppiyassāvi mittassa | rahe bhāsai pāvayaṃ 
paiṇṇavāī duhile | thaddhe luddhe aṇiggahe /
asaṃvibhāgī aviyatte | aviṇīe tti vuccaī 
aha pannarasahiṃ ṭhāṇehiṃ | suviṇīe tti vuccaī /
nīyāvattī acavale | amāī akuūhale 
appaṃ ca ahikkhivaī | pabandhaṃ ca na kuvvaī /
mettijjamāṇo bhayaī | suyaṃ laddhuṃ na majjaī 
na ya pāvaparikkhevī | na ya mittesu kuppaī /
appiyassāvi mittassa | rahe kallāṇa bhāsaī
kalahaḍamaravajjie | buddhe abhijāie /
hirimaṃ paḍisaṃlīṇe | suviṇīe tti vuccaī
vase gurukule niccaṃ | jogavaṃ uvahāṇavaṃ /
piyaṃkare piyaṃvāī | se sikkhaṃ laddhum arihaī 
jahā saṃkhammi payaṃ | nihiyaṃ duhao vi virāyai /
evaṃ bahussue bhikkhū | dhammo kittī tahā suyaṃ 
jahā se kamboyāṇaṃ | āiṇṇe kanthae siyā /
āse javeṇa pavare | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahāiṇṇasamārūḍhe | sūre daḍhaparakkame /
ubhao nandighoseṇaṃ | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā kareṇuparikiṇṇe | kuṃjare saṭhihāyaṇe /
balavante appaḍihae | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se tikkhasiṃge | jāyakhandhe virāyaī /
vasahe jūhāhivaī | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se tikkhadāḍhe | udagge duppahaṃsae /
sīhe miyāṇa pavare | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se vāsudeve | saṃkhacakkagayādhare /
appaḍihayabale johe | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se cāurante | cakkavaī mahiḍḍhie /
coddasarayaṇāhivaī | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se sahassakkhe | vajjapāṇī purandare /
sakke devāhivaī | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se timiraviddhaṃse | ucciṭhante divāyare /
jalante iva teeṇa | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se uḍuvaī cande | nakkhattaparivārie /
paḍipuṇṇe puṇṇamāsīe | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se sāmāiyāṇaṃ | koṭhāgāre surakkhie /
nāṇādhannapaḍipuṇṇe | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā sā dumāṇa pavarā | jambū nāma sudaṃsaṇā /
aṇāḍhiyassa devassa | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā sā naīṇa pavarā | salilā sāgaraṃgamā /
sīyā nīlavantapavahā | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se nagāṇa pavare | sumahaṃ mandare girī /
nāṇosahipajjalie | evaṃ havai bahussue 
jahā se sayaṃbhuramaṇe | udahī akkhaodae /
nāṇārayaṇapaḍipuṇṇe | evaṃ havai bahussue 
samuddagambhīrasamā durāsayā | acakkiyā keṇai duppahaṃsayā /
suyassa puṇṇā viulassa tāiṇo | khavittu kammaṃ gaim uttamaṃ gayā 
tamhā suyamahiṭhijjā | uttamaṭhagavesae /
jeṇappāṇaṃ paraṃ ceva | siddhiṃ saṃpāuṇejjāsi  tti bemi ||
      || bahussuyapujjaṃ samattaṃ 

U/12 hariesijjaṃ dvādaśam adhyayanam ||
 
sovāgakulasaṃbhūo | guṇuttaradharo muṇī /
hariesabalo nāma | āsi bhikkhū jiindio 
iriesaṇabhāsāe | uccārasamiīsu ya /
jao āyāṇanikkheve | saṃjao susamāhio 
maṇagutto vayagutto | kāyagutto jiindio /
bhikkhaṭhā bambhaijjammi | jannavāḍe uvaṭhio 
taṃ pāsiūṇam ejjantaṃ | taveṇa parisosiyaṃ /
pantovahiuvagaraṇaṃ | uvahasanti aṇāriyā 
jāīmayapaḍithaddhā | hiṃsagā ajiindiyā /
abambhacāriṇo bālā | imaṃ vayaṇam abbavī 
kayare āgacchai dittarūve | kāle vigarāle phokkanāse /
omacelae paṃsupisāyabhūe | saṃkaradūsaṃ parivariya kaṇṭhe 
ko re tuvaṃ iya adaṃsaṇijje | kāe va āsāihamāgao si /
omacelayā paṃsupisāyabhūyā | gaccha kkhalāhi kim ihaṃ ṭhio si 
jakkhe tahiṃ tinduyarukkhavāsī | aṇukampao tassa mahāmuṇissa /
pacchāyaittā niyagaṃ sarīraṃ | imāiṃ vayaṇāim udāharitthā 
samaṇo ahaṃ saṃjao bambhayārī | virao dhaṇapayaṇapariggahāo /
parappavittassa u bhikkhakāle | annassa aṭhā ihamāgao mi 
viyarijjai khajjai bhujjaī | annaṃ pabhūyaṃ bhavayāṇam eyaṃ /
jāṇeha me jāyaṇajīviṇu tti | sesāvasesaṃ labhaū tavassī 
uvakkhaḍaṃ bhoyaṇa māhaṇāṇaṃ | attaṭhiyaṃ siddham ihegapakkhaṃ /
na ū vayaṃ erisam annapāṇaṃ | dāhāmu tujjhaṃ kim ihaṃ ṭhiosi 
thalesu bīyāi vavanti kāsagā | taheva ninnesu ya āsasāe /
eyāe saddhāe dalāha majjhaṃ | ārāhae puṇṇam iṇaṃ khu khittaṃ 
khettāṇi amhaṃ viiyāṇi loe | jahiṃ pakiṇṇā viruhanti puṇṇā /
je māhaṇā jāivijjovaveyā | tāiṃ tu khettāi supesalāiṃ 
koho ya māṇo ya vaho ya jesiṃ | mosaṃ adattaṃ ca pariggahaṃ ca /
te māhaṇā jāivijjāvihūṇā | tāiṃ tu khettāi supāvayāiṃ 
tubbhettha bho bhāradharā girāṇaṃ | aṭhaṃ na jāṇeha ahijja vee /
uccāvayāiṃ muṇiṇo caranti | tāiṃ tu khettāi supesalāiṃ 
ajjhāvayāṇaṃ paḍikūlabhāsī | pabhāsase kiṃ tu sagāsi amhaṃ /
avi eyaṃ viṇassau annapāṇaṃ | na ya -aṃ dāhāmu tumaṃ niyaṇṭhā 
samiīhi majjhaṃ susamāhiyassa | guttīhi guttassa jiindiyassa /
jai me na dāhittha ahesaṇijjaṃ | kim ajja jannāṇa lahittha lāhaṃ 
ke ettha khattā uvajoiyā vā | ajjhāvayā vā saha khaṇḍiehiṃ /
eyaṃ daṇḍeṇa phalaeṇa hantā | kaṇṭhammi ghettūṇa khalejja jo -aṃ 
ajjhāvayāṇaṃ vayaṇaṃ suṇettā | uddhāiyā tattha bahū kumārā /
daṇḍehi vittehi kasehi ceva | samāgayā taṃ isi tālayanti 
ranno tahiṃ kosaliyassa dhūyā | bhadda tti nāmeṇa aṇindiyaṃgī /
taṃ pāsiyā saṃjaya hammamāṇaṃ | kuddhe kumāre parinivvavei 
devābhiogeṇa nioieṇaṃ | dinnā mu rannā maṇasā na jhāyā /
narindadevindabhivandieṇaṃ | jeṇam hi vantā isiṇā sa eso 
eso hu so uggatavo mahappā | jitindio saṃjao bambhayārī /
jo me tayā necchai dijjamāṇiṃ | piuṇā sayaṃ kosalieṇa rannā 
mahājaso eso mahāṇubhāgo | ghoravvao ghoraparakkamo ya /
mā eyaṃ hīleha ahīlaṇijjaṃ | mā savve teeṇa bhe niddahejjā 
eyāiṃ tīse vayaṇāi soccā | pattīi bhaddāi suhāsiyāiṃ /
isissa veyāvaḍiyaṭhayāe | jakkhā kumāre viṇivārayanti 
te ghorarūvā ṭhiya antalikkhe | 'surā tahiṃ taṃ jaṇa tālayanti /
te bhinnadehe ruhiraṃ vamante | pāsittu bhaddā iṇam āhu bhujjo 
giriṃ nahehiṃ khaṇaha | ayaṃ dantehiṃ khāyaha /
jāyateyaṃ pāehi haṇaha | je bhikkhuṃ avamannaha 
āsīviso uggatavo mahesī | ghoravvao ghoraparakkamo ya /
agaṇiṃ va pakkhanda payaṃgaseṇā | je bhikkhuyaṃ bhattakāle vaheha 
sīseṇa eyaṃ saraṇaṃ uveha | samāgayā savvajaṇeṇa tubbhe /
jai icchaha jīviyaṃ vā dhaṇaṃ vā | logaṃ pi eso kuvio ḍahejjā 
avaheḍiya piṭhisauttamaṃge | pasāriyā bāhu akammaceṭhe /
nijjheriyacche ruhiraṃ vamante | uddhaṃ muhe niggayajīhanette 
te pāsiyā khaṇḍiyakaṭhabhūe | vimaṇo visaṇṇo aha māhaṇo so /
isiṃ pasāei sabhāriyāo | hīlaṃ ca nindaṃ ca khamāha bhante 
bālehi mūḍhehi ayāṇaehiṃ | jaṃ hīliyā tassa khamāha bhante /
mahappasāyā isiṇo havanti | na hu muṇī kovaparā havanti 
puvviṃ ca iṇhiṃ ca aṇāgayaṃ ca | maṇappadoso na me atthi koi /
jakkhā hu veyāvaḍiyaṃ karenti | tamhā hu ee nihayā kumārā 
atthaṃ ca dhammaṃ ca viyāṇamāṇā | tubbhaṃ na vi kuppaha bhūipannā /
tubbhaṃ tu pāe saraṇaṃ uvemo | samāgayā savvajaṇeṇa amhe 
accemu te mahābhāga | na te kiṃci na accimo /
bhuṃjāhi sālimaṃ kūraṃ | nāṇāvaṃjaṇasaṃjuyaṃ 
imaṃ ca me atthi pabhūyam annaṃ | taṃ bhuṃjasū amha aṇuggahaṭhā /
bāḍhaṃ ti paḍicchai bhattapāṇaṃ | māsassa ū pāraṇae mahappā 
tahiyaṃ gandhodayapupphavāsaṃ | divvā tahiṃ vasuhārā ya vuṭhā /
pahayāo dunduhīo surehiṃ | āgāse aho dāṇaṃ ca ghuṭhaṃ 
sakkhaṃ khu dīsai tavoviseso | na dīsaī jāivisesa koī /
sovāgaputtaṃ hariesasāhuṃ | jasserisā iḍḍhi mahāṇubhāgā 
kiṃ māhaṇā joisamārabhantā | udaeṇa sohiṃ bahiyā vimaggaha /
jaṃ maggahā bāhiriyaṃ visohiṃ | na taṃ suiṭhaṃ kusalā vayanti 
kusaṃ ca jūvaṃ taṇakaṭham aggiṃ | sāyaṃ ca pāyaṃ udagaṃ phusantā /
pāṇāi bhūyāi viheḍayantā | bhujjo vi mandā pagareha pāvaṃ 
kahaṃ ca re bhikkhu vayaṃ jayāmo | pāvāi kammāi puṇollayāmo /
akkhāhi -e saṃjaya jakkhapūiyā | kahaṃ sujaṭhaṃ kusalā vayanti 
chajjīvakāe asamārabhantā | mosaṃ adattaṃ ca asevamāṇā /
pariggahaṃ itthio māṇamāyaṃ | eyaṃ parinnāya caranti dantā 
susaṃvuḍā paṃcahi saṃvarehiṃ | iha jīviyaṃ aṇavakaṃkhamāṇā /
vosaṭhakāi suicattadehā | mahājayaṃ jayai jannasiṭhaṃ 
ke te joī ke va te joiṭhāṇe | kā te suyā kiṃ va te kārisaṃgaṃ /
ehā ya te kayarā santi bhikkhū | kayareṇa homeṇa huṇāsi joiṃ 
tavo joī jīvo joiṭhāṇaṃ | jogā suyā sarīraṃ kārisaṃgaṃ /
kammehā saṃjamajogasantī | homaṃ huṇāmi isiṇaṃ pasatthaṃ 
ke te harae ke ya te santititthe | kahiṃ siṇāo va rayaṃ jahāsi /
āikkha -e saṃjaya jakkhapūiyā | icchāmo nāuṃ bhavao sagāse 
dhamme harae bambhe santititthe | aṇāvile attapasannalese /
jahiṃ siṇāo vimalo visuddho | susīibhūo pajahāmi dosaṃ 
eyaṃ siṇāṇaṃ kusalehi diṭhaṃ | mahāsiṇāṇa isiṇaṃ pasatthaṃ /
jahi siṇāyā vimalā visuddhā | mahārisī uttamaṃ ṭhāṇaṃ patta  tti bemi ||
     || hariesijjaṃ samattaṃ 

U/13 cittasambhūijjaṃ trayodaśam adhyayanam /
      
jāīparāio khalu | kāsi niyāṇaṃ tu hatthiṇapurammi /
culaṇīe bambhadatto | uvavanno paumagummāo 
kampille sambhūo | citto puṇa jāo purimatālammi /
seṭhikulammi visāle | dhammaṃ soūṇa pavvaio 
kampillammi ya nayare | samāgayā do vi cittasambhūyā /
suhadukkhaphalavivāgaṃ | kahenti te ekkam ekkassa 
cakkavaī mahiḍḍhīo | bambhadatto mahāyaso /
bhāyaraṃ bahumāṇeṇaṃ | imaṃ vayaṇam abbavī 
āsīmu bhāyaro do vi | annam annavasāṇugā /
annamannam aṇūrattā | annamannahiesiṇo 
dāsā dasaṇṇe āsīmu | miyā kāliṃjare nage /
haṃsā mayaṃgatīre | sovāgā kāsibhūmie 
devā ya devalogammi | āsi amhe mahiḍḍhiyā /
imā no chaṭhiyā jāī | annamanneṇa jā viṇā 
kammā niyāṇapayaḍā | tume rāya vicintiyā /
tesiṃ phalavivāgeṇa | vippaogam uvāgayā 
saccasoyappagaḍā | kammā mae purā kaḍā /
te ajja paribhuṃjāmo | kiṃ tu citte vi se tahā 
savvaṃ suciṇṇaṃ saphalaṃ narāṇaṃ | kaḍāṇa kammāṇa na mokkha atthi /
atthehi kāmehi ya uttamehiṃ | āyā mamaṃ puṇṇaphalovavee 
jāṇāhi saṃbhūya mahāṇubhāgaṃ | mahiḍḍhiyaṃ puṇṇaphalovaveyaṃ /
cittaṃ pi jāṇāhi taheva rāyaṃ | iḍḍhī juī tassa vi ya ppabhūyā 
mahattharūvā vayaṇappabhūyā | gāhāṇugīyā narasaṃghamajjhe /
jaṃ bhikkhuṇo sīlaguṇovaveyā | ihaṃ jayante samaṇo mi jāo 
uccoyae mahu kakke ya bambhe | paveiyā āvasahā ya rammā /
imaṃ gihaṃ citta dhaṇappabhūyaṃ | pasāhi paṃcālaguṇovaveyaṃ 
naehi gīehi ya vāiehiṃ | nārījaṇāhiṃ pariyārayanto /
bhuṃjāhi bhogāi imāi bhikkhū | mama royaī pavvajjā hu dukkhaṃ 
taṃ puvvaneheṇa kayāṇurāgaṃ | narāhivaṃ kāmaguṇesu giddhaṃ /
dhammassio tassa hiyāṇupehī | citto imaṃ vayaṇam udāharitthā 
savvaṃ vilaviyaṃ gīyaṃ | savvaṃ naaṃ viḍambiyaṃ /
savve ābharaṇā bhārā | savve kāmā duhāvahā 
bālābhirāmesu duhāvahesu | na taṃ suhaṃ kāmaguṇesu rāyaṃ /
virattakāmāṇa tavohaṇāṇaṃ | jaṃ bhikkhuṇaṃ sīlaguṇe rayāṇaṃ 
nariṃda jāī ahamā narāṇaṃ | sovāgajāī duhao gayāṇaṃ /
jahiṃ vayaṃ savvajaṇassa vessā | vasī ya sovāganivesaṇesu 
tīse ya jāīi u pāviyāe | vucchāmu sovāganivesaṇesu /
savvassa logassa dugaṃchaṇijjā | ihaṃ tu kammāi pure kaḍāiṃ 
so dāṇi siṃ rāya mahāṇubhāgo | mahiḍḍhio puṇṇaphalovaveo /
caittu bhogāi asāsayāiṃ | ādāṇaheuṃ abhiṇikkhamāhi 
iha jīvie rāya asāsayammi | dhaṇiyaṃ tu puṇṇāi akuvvamāṇo /
se soyaī maccumuhovaṇīe | dhammaṃ akāūṇa paraṃsi loe 
jaheha sīho va miyaṃ gahāya | maccū naraṃ nei hu antakāle /
na tassa māyā va piyā va bhāyā | kālammi tammaṃsaharā bhavaṃti 
na tassa dukkhaṃ vibhayanti nāio | na mittavaggā na suyā na baṃdhavā /
ekko sayaṃ paccaṇuhoi dukkhaṃ | kattāram eva aṇujāi kammaṃ 
ceccā dupayaṃ ca cauppayaṃ ca | khettaṃ gihaṃ dhaṇadhannaṃ ca savvaṃ /
sakammabīo avaso payāi | paraṃ bhavaṃ suṃdara pāvagaṃ vā 
taṃ ekkaṃ tucchasarīragaṃ se | ciīgayaṃ dahiya u pāvageṇaṃ /
bhajjā ya puttāvi ya nāyao ya | dāyāram annaṃ aṇusaṃkamanti 
uvaṇijjaī jīviyam appamāyaṃ | vaṇṇaṃ jarā harai narassa rāya /
paṃcālarāyā vayaṇaṃ suṇāhi | mā kāsi kammāi mahālayāiṃ 
ahaṃ pi jāṇāmi jaheha sāhū | jaṃ me tumaṃ sāhasi vakkam eyaṃ /
bhogā ime saṃgakarā havanti | je dujjayā ajjo amhārisehiṃ 
hatthiṇapurammi cittā | daṭhūṇaṃ naravaiṃ mahiḍḍhīyaṃ /
kāmabhogesu giddheṇaṃ | niyāṇam asuhaṃ kaḍaṃ 
tassa me apaḍikantassa | imaṃ eyārisaṃ phalaṃ /
jāṇamāṇo vi jaṃ dhammaṃ | kāmabhogesu mucchio 
nāgo jahā paṃkajalāvasanno | daṭhuṃ thalaṃ nābhisamei tīraṃ /
evaṃ vayaṃ kāmaguṇesu giddhā | na bhikkhuṇo maggam aṇuvvayāmo 
accei kālo taranti rāio | na yāvi bhogā purisāṇa niccā /
uvicca bhogā purisaṃ cayanti | dumaṃ jahā khīṇaphalaṃ va pakkhī 
jai taṃ si bhoge caiuṃ asatto | ajjāi kammāi karehi rāyaṃ /
dhamme ṭhio savvapayāṇukampī | to hohisi devo io viuvvī 
na tujjha bhoge caiūṇa buddhī | giddho si ārambhapariggahesu /
mohaṃ kao ettiu vippalāvu | gacchāmi rāyaṃ āmantio si 
paṃcālarāyā vi ya bambhadatto | sāhussa tassa vayaṇaṃ akāuṃ /
aṇuttare bhuṃjiya kāmabhoge | aṇuttare so narae paviṭho 
citto vi kāmehi virattakāmo | udaggacārittatavo mahesī /
aṇuttaraṃ saṃjama pālaittā | aṇuttaraṃ siddhigaiṃ gao  tti bemi ||
      || cittasaṃbhūijjaṃ samattaṃ 

U/14 usuyārijjaṃ caturdaśam adhyayanam /

devā bhavittāṇa pure bhavammī | keī cuyā egavimāṇavāsī /
pure purāṇe usuyāranāme | khāe samiddhe suralogaramme 
sakammaseseṇa purākaeṇaṃ | kulesudaggesu ya te pasūyā /
nivviṇṇasaṃsārabhayā jahāya | jiṇiṃdamaggaṃ saraṇaṃ pavannā 
pumattam āgamma kumāra do vī | purohio tassa jasā ya pattī /
visālakittī ya tahosuyāro | rāyattha devī kamalāvaī ya 
jāījarāmaccubhayābhibhūyā | bahiṃvihārābhiniviṭhacittā /
saṃsāracakkassa vimokkhaṇatthā | datthūṇa te kāmaguṇe virattā 
piyaputtagā donni vi māhaṇassa | sakammasīlassa purohiyassa /
sarittu porāṇiya tattha jāiṃ | tahā suciṇṇaṃ tavasaṃjamaṃ ca 
te kāmabhogesu asajjamāṇā | māṇussaesuṃ je yāvi divvā /
mokkhābhikaṃkhī abhijāyasaḍḍhā | tāyaṃ uvāgamma imaṃ udāhu 
asāsayaṃ datthu imaṃ vihāraṃ | bahuantarāyaṃ na ya dīham āuṃ /
tamhā gihaṃsi na raiṃ lahāmo | āmantayāmo carissāmu moṇaṃ 
aha tāyago tattha muṇīṇa tesiṃ | tavassa vāghāyakaraṃ vayāsī /
imaṃ vayaṃ veyavio vayanti | jahā na hoī asuyāṇa logo 
ahijja vee parivissa vippe | putte pariṭhappa gihaṃsi jāyā /
bhoccāṇa bhoe saha itthiyāhiṃ | āraṇṇagā hoha muṇī pasatthā 
soyaggiṇā āyaguṇindhaṇeṇaṃ | mohāṇilā pajjalaṇāhieṇaṃ /
saṃtattabhāvaṃ paritappamāṇaṃ | lālappamāṇaṃ bahuhā bahuṃ ca 
purohiyaṃ taṃ kamaso 'uṇintaṃ | nimaṃtayantaṃ ca sue dhaṇeṇaṃ ũ/
jahakkamaṃ kāmaguṇehi ceva | kumāragā te pasamikkha vakkaṃ 
veyā ahīyā na bhavanti tāṇaṃ | bhuttā diyā ninti tamaṃ tameṇaṃ ũ/
jāyā ya puttā na havanti tāṇaṃ | ko -āma te aṇumannejja eyaṃ 
khaṇamettasokkhā bahukāladukkhā | pagāmadukkhā aṇigāmasokkhā /
saṃsāramokkhassa vipakkhabhūyā | khāṇī aṇatthāṇa u kāmabhogā 
parivvayante aṇiyattakāme | aho ya rāo paritappamāṇe /
annappamatte dhaṇam esamāṇe | pappoti maccuṃ purise jaraṃ ca 
imaṃ ca me atthi imaṃ ca natthi | imaṃ ca me kicca imaṃ akiccaṃ /
taṃ evamevaṃ lālappamāṇaṃ | harā haraṃti tti kahaṃ pamāe 
dhaṇaṃ pabhūyaṃ saha itthiyāhiṃ | sayaṇā tahā kāmaguṇā pagāmā /
tavaṃ kae tappai jassa logo | taṃ savvasāhīṇam iheva tubbhaṃ 
dhaṇeṇa kiṃ dhammadhurāhigāre | sayaṇeṇa vā kāmaguṇehi ceva /
samaṇā bhavissāmu guṇohadhārī | bahiṃvihārā abhigamma bhikkhaṃ 
jahā ya aggī araṇī asanto | khīre ghayaṃ tellam ahā tilesu /
emeva tāyā sarīraṃsi sattā | saṃmucchaī nāsai nāvaciṭhe 
no indiyaggejjha amuttabhāvā | amuttabhāvā vi ya hoi nicco /
ajjhatthaheuṃ niyayassa bandho | saṃsāraheuṃ ca vayanti bandhaṃ 
jahā vayaṃ dhammam ajāṇamāṇā | pāvaṃ purā kammam akāsi mohā /
orubbhamāṇā parirakkhiyantā | taṃ neva bhujjo vi samāyarāmo 
abbhāhayaṃmi logaṃmi | savvao parivārie /
amohāhiṃ paḍantīhiṃ | gihaṃsi na raiṃ labhe 
keṇa abbhāhao logo | keṇa vā parivārio /
kā vā amohā vuttā | jāyā ciṃtāvaro hume 
maccuṇā 'bbhāhao logo | jarāe parivārio /
amohā rayaṇī vuttā | evaṃ tāya vijāṇaha 
jā jā vaccai rayaṇī | na sā paḍiniyattaī /
ahammaṃ kuṇamāṇassa | aphalā janti rāio 
jā jā vaccai rayaṇī | na sā paḍiniyattaī /
dhammaṃ ca kuṇamāṇassa | saphalā janti rāio 
egao saṃvasittāṇaṃ | duhao sammattasaṃjuyā /
pacchā jāyā gamissāmo | bhikkhamāṇā kule kule 
jassatthi maccuṇā sakkhaṃ | jassa catthi palāyaṇaṃ /
jo jāṇe na marissāmi | so hu kaṃkhe sue siyā 
ajjeva dhammaṃ paḍivajjayāmo | jahiṃ pavannā na puṇabbhavāmo /
aṇāgayaṃ neva ya atthi kiṃcī | saddhākhamaṃ -e viṇaittu rāgaṃ 
pahīṇaputtassa hu natthi vāso | vāsiṭhi bhikkhāyariyāi kālo /
sāhāhi rukkho lahaī samāhiṃ | chinnāhi sāhāhi tam eva khāṇuṃ 
paṃkhāvihūṇo vva jaheva pakkhī | bhiccavihūṇo vva raṇe narindo /
vivannasāro vaṇio vva poe | pahīṇaputto mi tahā ahaṃ pi 
susaṃbhiyā kāmaguṇā ime te | saṃpiṇḍiyā aggarasappabhūyā /
bhuṃjāmu tā kāmaguṇe pagāmaṃ | pacchā gamissāmu pahāṇamaggaṃ 
bhuttā rasā bhoi jahāi -e vao | na jīviyaṭhā pajahāmi bhoe /
lābhaṃ alābhaṃ ca suhaṃ ca dukkhaṃ | saṃcikkhamāṇo carissāmi moṇaṃ 
mā hū tumaṃ soyariyāṇa sambhare | juṇṇo va haṃso paḍisottagāmī /
bhuṃjāhi bhogāi mae samāṇaṃ | dukkhaṃ khu bhikkhāyariyāvihāro 
jahā ya bhoī taṇuyaṃ bhuyaṃgo | nimmoyaṇiṃ hicca palei mutto /
em ee jāyā payahanti bhoe | te haṃ kahaṃ nāṇugamissam ekko 
chindittu jālaṃ abalaṃ va rohiyā | macchā jahā kāmaguṇe pahāya /
dhoreyasīlā tavasā udārā | dhīrā hu bhikkhāyariyaṃ caranti 
naheva kuṃcā samaikkamantā | tayāṇi jālāṇi dalittu haṃsā /
palenti puttā ya paī ya majjhaṃ | te haṃ kahaṃ nāṇugamissam ekkā 
purohiyaṃ taṃ sasuyaṃ sadāraṃ | soccā 'bhinikkhamma pahāya bhoe /
kuḍumbasāraṃ viuluttamaṃ ca | rāyaṃ abhikkhaṃ samuvāya devī 
vantāsī puriso rāyaṃ | na so hoi pasaṃsio /
māhaṇeṇa pariccattaṃ | dhaṇaṃ ādāum icchasi 
savvaṃ jagaṃ jai tuhaṃ | savvaṃ vāvi dhaṇaṃ bhave /
savvaṃ pi te apajjattaṃ | neva tāṇāya taṃ tava 
marihisi rāyaṃ jayā tayā vā | maṇorame kāmaguṇe vihāya /
ekko hu dhammo naradeva tāṇaṃ | na vijjaī annam iheha kiṃci 
nāhaṃ rame pakkhiṇi paṃjare vā | saṃtāṇachinnā carissāmi moṇaṃ /
akiṃcaṇā ujjukaḍā nirāmisā | pariggahārambhaniyattadosā 
davaggiṇā jahā raṇṇe | ḍajjhamāṇesu jantusu /
anne sattā pamoyanti | rāgaddosavasaṃ gayā 
evameva vayaṃ mūḍhā | kāmabhogesu mucchiyā /
ḍajjhamāṇaṃ na bujjhāmo | rāgaddosaggiṇā jagaṃ 
bhoge bhoccā vamittā ya | lahubhūyavihāriṇo /
āmoyamāṇā gacchanti | diyā kāmakamā iva 
ime ya baddhā phandanti | mama hatthajjamāgayā /
vayaṃ ca sattā kāmesu | bhavissāmo jahā ime 
sāmisaṃ kulalaṃ dissa | bajjhamāṇaṃ nirāmisaṃ /
āmisaṃ savvam ujjhittā | viharissāmi nirāmisā 
giddhovamā u naccāṇaṃ | kāme saṃsāravaḍḍhaṇe /
urago suvaṇṇapāse vva | saṃkamāṇo taṇuṃ care 
nāgo vva bandhaṇaṃ chittā | appaṇo vasahiṃ vae /
eyaṃ pacchaṃ mahārāyaṃ | ussuyāri tti me suyaṃ 
caittā viulaṃ rajjaṃ | kāmabhoge ya duccae /
nivvisayā nirāmisā | ninnehā nippariggahā 
sammaṃ dhammaṃ viyāṇittā | ceccā kāmaguṇe vare /
tavaṃ pagijjhahakkhāyaṃ | ghoraṃ ghoraparakkammā 
evaṃ te kamaso buddhā | savve dhammaparāyaṇā /
jammamaccubhauvviggā | dukkhassantagavesiṇo 
sāsaṇe vigayamohāṇaṃ | puvviṃ bhāvaṇabhāviyā /
acireṇeva kāleṇa | dukkhassantam uvāgayā 
rāyā saha devīe | māhaṇo ya purohio /
māhaṇī dāragā ceva | savve te parinivvuḍa  tti bemi ||
     || usuyārijjaṃ samattaṃ  

U/15 sabhikkhū pañcadaśm adhyayanam /
 
moṇaṃ carissāmi samicca dhammaṃ | sahie ujjukaḍe niyāṇachinne /
saṃthavaṃ jahijja akāmakāme | annāyaesī parivvae sa bhikkhū 
rāovarayaṃ carejja lāḍhe | virae veyaviyāyarakkhie /
panne abhibhūya savvadaṃsī | je kamhi ci na mucchie sa bhikkhū 
akkosavahaṃ viittu dhīre | muṇī care lāḍhe niccam āyagutte /
avvaggamaṇe asaṃpahiṭhe | je kasiṇaṃ ahiyāsae sa bhikkhū 
pantaṃ sayaṇāsaṇaṃ bhaittā | sīuṇhaṃ vivihaṃ ca daṃsamasagaṃ /
avvaggamaṇe asaṃpahiṭhe | je kasiṇaṃ ahiyāsae sa bhikkhū 
no sakkaim icchaī na pūyaṃ | no vi ya vandaṇagaṃ kuo pasaṃsaṃ /
se saṃjae suvvae tavassī | sahie āyagavesae sa bhikkhū 
jeṇa puṇa jahāi jīviyaṃ | mohaṃ vā kasiṇaṃ niyacchaī /
naranāriṃ pajahe sayā tavassī | na ya koūhalaṃ uvei sa bhikkhū 
chinnaṃ saraṃ bhomam antalikkhaṃ | sumiṇaṃ lakkhaṇadaṇḍavatthuvijjaṃ /
aṃgaviyāraṃ sarassa vijayaṃ | je vijjāhiṃ na jīvai sa bhikkhū 
mantaṃ mūlaṃ vivihaṃ vejjacintaṃ | vamaṇavireyaṇadhūmaṇettasiṇāṇaṃ /
āure saraṇaṃ tigicchiyaṃ ca | taṃ parinnāya parivvae sa bhikkhū 
khattiyagaṇa ugga rāyaputtā | māhaṇa bhoiya vivihā ya sippiṇo /
no tesiṃ vayai silogapūyaṃ | taṃ parinnāya parivvae sa bhikkhū 
gihiṇo je pavvaieṇa diṭhā | appavaieṇa va saṃthuyā havijjā /
tesiṃ ihaloiyaphalaṭhā | jo saṃthavaṃ na karei sa bhikkhū 
sayaṇāsaṇapāṇabhoyaṇaṃ | vivihaṃ khāimasāimaṃ paresiṃ /
adae paḍisehie niyaṇṭhe | je tattha na paussaī sa bhikkhū 
jaṃ kiṃ ca āhārapāṇajāyaṃ | vivihaṃ khāimasāimaṃ paresiṃ laddhuṃ /
jo taṃ tiviheṇa nāṇukampe | maṇavayakāyasusaṃvuḍe sa bhikkhū 
āyāmagaṃ ceva javodaṇaṃ ca | sīyaṃ sovīrajavodagaṃ ca /
no hīlae piṇḍaṃ nīrasaṃ tu | pantakulāiṃ parivvae sa bhikkhū 
saddā vivihā bhavanti loe | divvā māṇussagā tiricchā /
bhīmā bhayabheravā urālā | soccā na vihijjaī sa bhikkhū 
vādaṃ vivihaṃ samicca loe | sahie kheyāṇugae ya koviyappā /
panne abhibhūya savvadaṃsī | uvasante aviheḍae sa bhikkhū 
asippajīvī agihe amitte | jiindie savvao vippamukke /
aṇukkasāī lahuappabhakkhī | ceccā gihaṃ egacare sa bhikkhu  tti bemi ||
     || sabhikkhuyaṃ nāma samattaṃ 

U/16 bambhacerasamāhiṭhāṇā  ṣoḍaśam adhyayanam /
 
suyaṃ me āusaṃ teṇaṃ bhagavayā evam akkhāyaṃ | iha khalu 
therehiṃ bhagavantehiṃ dasa bambhacerasamāhiṭhāṇā pannattā je 
bhikkhū soccā nisamma saṃjamabahule saṃvarabahule samāhibahule 
gutte guttindie guttabambhayārī sayā appamatte  viharejjā 
kayare khalu te therehiṃ bhagavantehiṃ dasa bambhacerasamāhiṭhāṇā 
pannattā je bhikkhū soccā nisamma saṃjamabahule saṃvarabahule 
samāhibahule gutte guttindie guttabambhayārī sayā appamatte 
viharejjā  ime khalu te therehiṃ bhagavantehiṃ dasa bambhaceraṭhāṇā 
pannattā je bhikkhū soccā nisamma saṃjamabahule saṃvarabahule 
samāhibahule gutte guttindie guttabambhayārī sayā appamatte 
viharejjā | taṃ jahā | vivittāiṃ sayaṇāsaṇāiṃ sevittā havai 
se nigganthe | no itthīpasupaṇḍagasaṃsattāiṃ sayaṇāsaṇāiṃ 
sevittā havai se nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti ce | āyariyāha 
nigganthassa khalu itthipasupaṇḍagasaṃsattāiṃ sayaṇāsaṇāiṃ sevamāṇassa 
bambhayārissa bambhacere saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā viigicchā 
vā samuppajjijjā bhedaṃ vā labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā 
dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ havejjā kevalipannattāo dhammāo 
bhaṃsejjā | tamhā no itthipasupaṇḍagasaṃsattāiṃ sayaṇāsaṇāiṃ 
sevittā havai se nigganthe 1 
  no itthīṇaṃ kahaṃ kahittā havai se nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti 
ce | āyariyāha | nigganthassa khalu itthīṇaṃ kahaṃ kahemāṇassa 
bambhayārissa bambhacere saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā viigicchā vā 
samupajjijjā bhedaṃ vā labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā 
dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ havejjā kevalipannattāo dhammāo 
bhaṃsejjā | tamhā no itthīṇaṃ kahaṃ kahejjā 2 
  no itthīṇaṃ saddhiṃ sannisejjāgae viharettā havai se 
nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti ce | āyariyāha | nigganthassa khalu 
itthīhiṃ saddhiṃ sannisejjāgayassa bambhayārissa bambhacere saṃkā 
vā kaṃkhā vā viigicchā vā samupajjijjā bhedaṃ vā labhejjā 
ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ havejjā 
kevalipannattāo dhammāo bhaṃsejjā | tamhā khalu no niggaṃthe 
itthīhiṃ saddhiṃ sannisejjāgae viharejjā 3 
  no itthīṇaṃ indiyāiṃ maṇoharāiṃ maṇoramāiṃ āloittā 
nijjhāittā havai se nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti ce | āyariyāha 
nigganthassa khalu itthīṇaṃ indiyāiṃ maṇoharāiṃ maṇoramāiṃ 
āloemāṇassa nijjhāyamāṇassa bambhayārissa bambhacere 
saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā viigicchā vā samupajjijjā bhedaṃ vā 
labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ 
havejjā kevalipannattāo dhammāo bhaṃsejjā | tamhā khalu no 
nigganthe itthīṇaṃ indiyāiṃ maṇoharāiṃ maṇoramāiṃ āloejjā 
nijjhāejjā 4 
  no itthīṇaṃ kuḍḍantaraṃsi vā dūsantaraṃsi vā bhittantaraṃsi 
vā kūiyasaddaṃ vā ruiyasaddaṃ vā gīyasaddaṃ vā hasiyasaddaṃ vā 
thaṇiyasaddaṃ vā kandiyasaddaṃ vā vilaviyasaddaṃ vā suṇettā havai 
se nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti ce | āyariyāha | nigganthassa 
khalu itthīṇaṃ kuḍḍantaraṃsi vā dūsantaraṃsi vā bhittantaraṃsi vā 
kūiyasaddaṃ vā ruiyasaddaṃ vā gīyasaddaṃ vā hasiyasaddaṃ vā thaṇiyasaddaṃ 
vā kandiyasaddaṃ vā vilaviyasaddaṃ vā suṇemāṇassa bambhayārissa 
bambhacere saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā viigicchā vā samupajjijjā 
bhedaṃ vā labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā dīhakāliyaṃ 
vā rogāyaṃkaṃ havejjā kevalipannattāo dhammāo bhaṃsejjā  
tamhā khalu no nigganthe itthīṇaṃ kuḍḍantaraṃsi vā dūsantaraṃsi 
vā bhittantaraṃsi vā kūiyasaddaṃ vā ruiyasaddaṃ vā gīyasaddaṃ vā 
hasiyasaddaṃ vā thaṇiyasaddaṃ vā kandiyasaddaṃ vā vilaviyasaddaṃ vā 
suṇemāṇe viharejjā 5 
  no nigganthe puvvarayaṃ puvvakīliyaṃ aṇusarittā havai se 
nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti ce | āyariyāha | nigganthassa khalu 
puvvarayaṃ puvvakīliyaṃ aṇusaramāṇassa bambhayārissa bambhacere 
saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā viigicchā vā samupajjijjā bhedaṃ vā 
labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ 
havejjā kevalipannattāo dhammāo bhaṃsejjā | tamhā khalu no 
nigganthe puvvarayaṃ puvvakīliyaṃ aṇusarejjā 6 
  no paṇīyaṃ āhāraṃ āharittā havai se nigganthe | taṃ 
kaham iti ce | āyariyāha | nigganthassa khalu paṇīyaṃ āhāraṃ 
āhāremāṇassa bambhayārissa bambhacere saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā 
viigicchā vā samupajjijjā bhedaṃ vā labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā 
pāuṇijjā | dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ havejjā kevalipannattāo 
dhammāo bhaṃsejjā | tamhā khalu no nigganthe paṇīyaṃ 
āhāraṃ āhārejjā 7 
  no aimāyāe pāṇabhoyaṇaṃ āhārettā havai se 
nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti ce | āyariyāha | nigganthassa khalu 
aimāyāe pāṇabhoyaṇaṃ āhāremāṇassa bambhayārissa bambhacere 
saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā viigicchā vā samupajjijjā bhedaṃ vā 
labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ 
havejjā kevalipannattāo dhammāo bhaṃsejjā | tamhā khalu no 
nigganthe aimāyāe pāṇabhoyaṇaṃ āhārejjā 8 
  no vibhūsāṇuvādī havai se nigganthe | taṃ kaham iti ce 
āyariyāha vibhūsāvattie vibhūsiyasarīre itthijaṇassa 
abhilasaṇijje havai | tao -aṃ itthijaṇeṇaṃ abhilasijjamāṇassa 
bambhacere saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā vā viigiccā vā samupajjijjā 
bhedaṃ vā labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā pāuṇijjā dīhakāliyaṃ 
vā rogāyaṃkaṃ havejjā kevalipannattāo dhammāo bhaṃsejjā | 
tamhā khalu no nigganthe vibhūsāṇuvādī havijjā 9 
  no saddarūvarasagandhaphāsāṇuvādī havai se nigganthe | taṃ 
kaham iti ce | āyariyāha | nigganthassa khalu saddarūvagandhaphāsāṇuvādissa 
bambhayārissa bambhacere saṃkā vā kaṃkhā vā 
viigiccā vā samupajjijjā bhedaṃ vā labhejjā ummāyaṃ vā 
pāuṇijjā dīhakāliyaṃ vā rogāyaṃkaṃ havejjā kevalipannattāo 
dhammāo bhaṃsejjā | tamhā khalu no saddarūvarasagandhaphāsāṇuvādī 
bhavejjā se nigganthe | dasame bambhacerasamāhiṭhāṇe 
havai 10 
jaṃ vivittam aṇāiṇṇaṃ | rahiyaṃ itthijaṇeṇa ya /
bambhacerassa rakkhaṭhā | ālayaṃ tu nisevae 
maṇapalhāyajaṇaṇī | kāmarāgavivaḍḍhaṇī /
bambhacerarao bhikkhū | thīkahaṃ tu vivajjae 
samaṃ ca saṃthavaṃ thīhiṃ | saṃkahaṃ ca abhikkhaṇaṃ /
bambhacerarao bhikkhū | niccaso parivajjae 
aṃgapaccaṃgasaṃṭhāṇaṃ | cārullaviyapehiyaṃ /
bambhacerarao thīṇaṃ | cakkhugijjhaṃ vivajjae 
kūiyaṃ ruiyaṃ gīyaṃ | hasiyaṃ thaṇiyakandiyaṃ /
bambhacerarao thīṇaṃ | soyagejjhaṃ vivajjae 
hāsaṃ kiḍḍaṃ raiṃ dappaṃ | sahasāvittāsiyāṇi ya /
bambhacerarao thīṇaṃ | nāṇucinte kayāi vi 
paṇīyaṃ bhattapāṇaṃ tu | khippaṃ mayavivaḍḍhaṇaṃ /
bambhacerarao bhikkhū | niccaso parivajjae 
dhammaladdhaṃ miyaṃ kāle | jattatthaṃ paṇihāṇavaṃ /
nāimattaṃ tu bhuṃjejjā | bambhacerarao sayā 
vibhūsaṃ parivajjejjā | sarīraparimaṇḍaṇaṃ /
bambhacerarao bhikkhū | siṃgāratthaṃ na dhārae 
sadde rūve ya gandhe ya | rase phāse taheva ya /
paṃcavihe kāmaguṇe | niccaso parivajjae 
ālao thījaṇāiṇṇo | thīkahā ya maṇoramā /
saṃthavo ceva nārīṇaṃ | tāsiṃ indiyadarisaṇaṃ 
kūiyaṃ ruiyaṃ gīyaṃ | hāsabhuttāsiyāṇi ya /
paṇīyaṃ bhattapāṇaṃ ca | aimāyaṃ pāṇabhoyaṇaṃ 
gattabhūsaṇam iṭhaṃ ca | kāmabhogā ya dujjayā /
narassattagavesissa | visaṃ tālauḍaṃ jahā 
dujjae kāmabhoge ya | niccaso parivajjae /
saṃkāthāṇāṇi savvāṇi | vajjejjā paṇihāṇavaṃ 
dhammārāme care bhikkhū | dhiimaṃ dhammasārahī /
dhammārāmarate dante | bambhacerasamāhie 
devadāṇavagandhavvā | jakkharakkhasakinnarā /
bambhayāriṃ namaṃsanti | dukkaraṃ je karanti taṃ 
esa dhamme dhuve nicce | sāsae jiṇadesie /
siddhā sijjhanti cāṇeṇa | sijjhissanti tahāvare  tti bemi ||
     || bambhacerasamāhiṭhāṇā samattā 

U/17 pāvasamaṇijjaṃ saptadaśam adhyayanam /
 
je kei u pavvaie niyaṇe | dhammaṃ suṇittā viṇaovavanne /
sudullahaṃ lahiuṃ bohilābhaṃ | viharejja pacchā ya jahāsuhaṃ tu 
sejjā daḍhā pāuraṇaṃ mi atthi | uppajjaī bhottu taheva pāuṃ /
jāṇāmi jaṃ vaai āusu tti | kiṃ nāma kāhāmi sueṇa bhante 
je keī pavvaie | niddāsīle pagāmaso /
bhoccā peccā suhaṃ suvai | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
āyariyauvajjhāehiṃ | suyaṃ viṇayaṃ ca gāhie /
te ceva khiṃsaī bāle | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
āyariyauvajjhāyāṇaṃ | sammaṃ na paḍitappai /
appaḍipūyae thaddhe | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
sammaddamāṇo pāṇāṇi | bīyāṇi hariyāṇi ya /
asaṃjae sajayamannamāṇo | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
saṃthāraṃ phalagaṃ pīḍhaṃ | nisejjaṃ pāyakambalaṃ /
appamajjiyam āruhai | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
davadavassa caraī | pamatte ya abhikkhaṇaṃ /
ullaṃghaṇe ya caṇḍe ya | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
paḍilehei pamatte | paujjhai pāyakambalaṃ /
paḍilehā aṇāutte | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
paḍilehei pamatte | se kiṃci hu nisāmiyā /
gurupāribhāvae niccaṃ | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
bahumāī pamuhare | thaddhe luddhe aṇiggahe /
asaṃvibhāgī aviyatte | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
vivādaṃ ca udīrei | ahamme attapannahā /
vuggahe kalahe ratte | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
athirāsaṇe kukuie | jattha tattha nisīyaī /
āsaṇammi aṇāutte | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
sasarakkhapāe suvaī | sejjaṃ na paḍilehai /
saṃthārae aṇāutte | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
duddhadahīvigaīo | āhārei abhikkhaṇaṃ /
arae ya tavokamme | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
atthantammi ya sūrammi | āhārei abhikkhaṇaṃ /
coio paḍicoei | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
āyariyapariccāī | parapāsaṇḍasevae /
gāṇaṃgaṇie dubbhūe | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
sayaṃ gehaṃ paricajja | paragehaṃsi vāvare /
nimitteṇa ya vavaharai | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
sannāi piṇḍaṃ jemei | necchaī sāmudāṇiyaṃ /
gihinisejjaṃ ca vāhei | pāvasamaṇi tti vuccaī 
eyārise paṃcakusīlasaṃvuḍe | rūvaṃdhare muṇipavarāṇa heṭhime /
ayaṃsi loe visam eva garahie | na se ihaṃ neva paratthaloe 
je vajjae ee sayā u dose | se suvvae hoi muṇīṇa majjhe /
ayaṃsi loe amayaṃ va pūie | ārāhae logam iṇaṃ tahā paraṃ  tti bemi ||
     ||pāvasamanijjaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/18 saṃjaijjaṃ aṣādaśam adhyayanam /
 
kampille nayare rāyā | udiṇṇabalavāhaṇe /
nāmeṇaṃ saṃjae nāmaṃ | migavvaṃ uvaṇiggae 
hayāṇīe gayāṇīe | rahāṇīe taheva ya /
pāyattāṇīe mahayā | savvao parivārie 
mie chuhittā hayagao | kampillujjāṇa kesare /
bhīe sante mie tattha | vahei rasamucchie 
aha kesarammi ujjāṇe | aṇagāre tavodhaṇe /
sajjhāyajjhāṇasaṃjutte | dhammajjhāṇaṃ jhiyāyai 
apphovamaṇḍavammi | jhāyai kkhaviyāsave /
tassāgae mige pāsaṃ | vaheī se narāhive 
aha āsagao rāyā | khippam āgamma so tahiṃ /
hae mie u pāsittā | aṇagāraṃ tattha pāsaī 
aha rāyā tattha saṃbhanto | aṇagāro maṇā hao /
mae u mandapuṇṇeṇaṃ | rasagiddheṇa ghannuṇā 
āsaṃ visajjaittāṇaṃ | aṇagārassa so nivo /
viṇaeṇa vandae pāe | bhagavaṃ ettha me khame 
aha moṇeṇa so bhagavaṃ | aṇagāre jhāṇam assie /
rāyāṇaṃ na paḍimantei | tao rāyā bhayadduo 
saṃjao aham ammīti | bhagavaṃ vāharāhi me /
kuddhe teeṇa aṇagāre | ḍahejja narakoḍio 
abhao patthivā tubbhaṃ | abhayadāyā bhavāhi ya /
aṇicce jīvalogammi | kiṃ hiṃsāe pasajjasī 
jayā savvaṃ pariccajja | gantavvam avasassa te /
aṇicce jīvalogammi | kiṃ rajjammi pasajjasī 
jīviyaṃ ceva rūvaṃ ca | vijjusaṃpāyacaṃcalaṃ /
jattha taṃ mujjhasī rāyaṃ | peccatthaṃ nāvabujjhase 
dārāṇi ya suyā ceva | mittā ya taha bandhavā /
jīvantam aṇujīvanti | mayaṃ nāṇuvvayanti ya 
nīharanti mayaṃ puttā | pitaraṃ paramadukkhiyā /
pitaro vi tahā putte | bandhū rāyaṃ tavaṃ care 
tao teṇajjie davve | dāre ya parirakkhie /
kīlanti 'nne narā rāyaṃ | haṭhatuṭhamalaṃkiyā 
teṇāvi jaṃ kayaṃ kammaṃ | suhaṃ vā jai vā duhaṃ /
kammuṇā teṇa saṃjutto | gacchaī u paraṃ bhavaṃ 
soūṇa tassa so dhammaṃ | aṇagārassa antie /
mahayā saṃveganivvedaṃ | samāvanno narāhivo 
saṃjao caiuṃ rajjaṃ | nikkhanto jiṇasāsaṇe /
gaddabhālissa bhagavao | aṇagārassa antie 
ciccā raṭhaṃ pavvaie | khattie paribhāsai /
jahā te dāsaī rūvaṃ | pasannaṃ te tahā maṇo 
kiṃ nāme kiṃ gotte | kassa ṭhāe va māhaṇe /
kahaṃ paḍiyarasī buddhe | kahaṃ viṇīe tti vuccasī 
saṃjao nāma nāmeṇaṃ | tahā gotteṇa goyamo /
gaddabhālī mamāyariyā | vijjācaraṇapāragā 
kiriyaṃ akiriyaṃ viṇayaṃ | annāṇaṃ ca mahāmuṇī /
eehiṃ cauhiṃ ṭhāṇehiṃ | meyanne kiṃ pabhāsaī 
ii pāukare buddhe | nāyae parinivvue /
vijjācaraṇasaṃpanne | sacce saccaparakkame 
paḍanti narae ghore | je narā pāvakāriṇo /
divvaṃ ca gaiṃ gacchanti | carittā dhammamāriyaṃ 
māyāvuiyam eyaṃ tu | musābhāsā niratthiyā /
saṃjamamāṇo vi ahaṃ | vasāmi iriyāmi ya 
savvee viiyā majjhaṃ | micchādiṭhī aṇāriyā /
vijjamāṇe pare loe | sammaṃ jāṇāmi appagaṃ 
aham āsi mahāpāṇe | juimaṃ varisasaovame /
jā sā pālīmahāpālī | divvā varisasaovamā 
se cue bambhalogāo | māṇusaṃ bhavamāgae /
appaṇo ya paresiṃ ca | āuṃ jāṇe jahā tahā 
nāṇāruiṃ ca chandaṃ ca | parivajjejja saṃjae /
aṇaṭhā je ya savvatthā | iya vijjāmaṇusaṃcare 
paḍikkamāmi pasiṇāṇaṃ | paramantehiṃ vā puṇo /
aho uṭhie ahorāyaṃ | ii vijjā tavaṃ care 
jaṃ ca me pucchasī kāle | sammaṃ suddheṇa ceyasā /
tāiṃ pāukare buddhe | taṃ nāṇaṃ jiṇasāsaṇe 
kiriyaṃ ca royaī dhīre | akiriyaṃ parivajjae /
diṭhīe diṭhīsaṃpanne | dhammaṃ carasu duccaraṃ 
eyaṃ puṇṇapayaṃ soccā | atthadhammovasohiyaṃ /
bharaho vi bhārahaṃ vāsaṃ | ceccā kāmāi pavvae 
sagaro vi sāgarantaṃ | bharahavāsaṃ narāhivo /
issariyaṃ kevalaṃ hiccā | dayāi parinivvuḍe 
caittā bhārahaṃ vāsaṃ | cakkavaī mahiḍḍhio /
pavvajjam abbhuvagao | maghavaṃ nāma mahājaso 
saṇaṃkumāro maṇussindo | cakkavaī mahaḍḍhio /
puttaṃ rajje ṭhaveūṇaṃ | so vi rāyā tavaṃ care 
caittā bhārahaṃ vāsaṃ | cakkavaī mahaḍḍhio /
santī santikare loe | patto gaim aṇuttaraṃ 
ikkhāgarāyavasabho | kunthū nāma narīsaro /
vikkhāyakittī bhagavaṃ | patto gaim aṇuttaraṃ 
sāgarantaṃ caittāṇaṃ | bharahaṃ naravarīsaro /
aro ya arayaṃ patto | patto gaim aṇuttaraṃ 
caittā bhārahaṃ vāsaṃ | caittā balavāhaṇaṃ /
caittā uttame bhoe | mahāpaume tavaṃ care 
egacchattaṃ pasāhittā | mahiṃ māṇanisūraṇo /
hariseṇo maṇussindo | patto gaim aṇuttaraṃ 
annio rāyasahassehiṃ | supariccāī damaṃ care /
jayanāmo jiṇakkhāyaṃ | patto gaim aṇuttaraṃ 
dasaṇṇarajjaṃ mudiyaṃ | caittāṇaṃ muṇī care /
dasaṇṇabhaddo nikkhanto | sakkhaṃ sakkeṇa coio 
namī namei appāṇaṃ | sakkhaṃ sakkeṇa coio /
caiūṇa gehaṃ vaidehī | sāmaṇṇe pajjuvaṭhio 
karakaṇḍū kaliṃgesu | paṃcālesu ya dummuho /
namī rāyā videhesu | gandhāresu ya naggaī 
ee narindavasabhā | nikkhantā jiṇasāsaṇe /
putte rajje ṭhaveūṇaṃ | sāmaṇṇe pajjuvaṭhiyā 
sovīrarāyavasabho | caittāṇa muṇī care /
udāyaṇo pavvaio | patto gaim aṇuttaraṃ 
taheva kāsīrāyā | seosaccaparakkame /
kāmabhoge pariccajja | pahaṇe kammamahāvaṇaṃ 
taheva vijao rāyā | aṇaṭhākitti pavvae /
rajjaṃ tu guṇasamiddhaṃ | payahittu mahājaso 
tahevuggaṃ tavaṃ kiccā | avvakkhitteṇa ceyasā /
mahabbalo rāyarisī | ādāya sirasā siriṃ 
kahaṃ dhīro aheūhiṃ | ummatto va mahiṃ care /
ee visesamādāya | sūrā daḍhaparakkamā 
accantaniyāṇakhamā | saccā me bhāsiyā vaī /
atariṃsu tarantege | tarissanti aṇāgayā 
kahiṃ dhīre aheūhiṃ | attāṇaṃ pariyāvase /
savvasaṃgavinimmukke | siddhe bhavai nīrae  tti bemi ||
     ||saṃjaijjaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/19 miyāputtīyaṃ ekonaviṃśatitamam adhyayanam /
 
suggīve nayare ramme | kāṇaṇujjāṇasohie /
rāyā balabhaddi tti | miyā tassaggamāhisī 
tesiṃ putte balasirī | miyāputte tti vissue /
ammāpiūṇa daie | juvarāyā damīsare 
nandaṇe so u pāsāe | kīlae saha itthihiṃ /
deve dogundage ceva | niccaṃ muiyamāṇaso 
maṇirayaṇakoimatale | pāsāyāloyaṇaṭhio /
āloei nagarassa | caukkattiyacaccare 
aha tattha aicchantaṃ | pāsaī samaṇasaṃjayaṃ /
tavaniyamasaṃjamadharaṃ | sīlaḍḍhaṃ guṇaāgaraṃ 
taṃ dehaī miyāputte | diṭhīe aṇimisāe u /
kahiṃ mannerisaṃ rūvaṃ | diṭhapuvvaṃ mae purā 
sāhussa darisaṇe tassa | ajjhavasāṇammi sohaṇe /
mohaṃgayassa santassa | jāīsaraṇaṃ samuppannaṃ 
jāīsaraṇe samuppanne | miyāputte mahiḍḍhie /
saraī porāṇiyaṃ jāiṃ | sāmaṇṇaṃ ca purā kayaṃ 
visaehi arajjanto | rajjanto saṃjamammi ya /
ammāpiyaram uvāgamma | imaṃ vayaṇam abbavī 
suyāṇi me paṃca mahavvayāṇi | naraesu dukkhaṃ ca tirikkhajoṇisu /
nivviṇṇakāmo mi mahaṇṇavāu | aṇujāṇaha pavvaissāmi ammo 
amma tāya mae bhogā | bhuttā visaphalovamā /
pacchā kaḍuyavivāgā | aṇubandhaduhāvahā 
imaṃ sarīraṃ aṇiccaṃ | asuiṃ asuisaṃbhavaṃ /
asāsayāvāsam iṇaṃ | dukkhakesāṇa bhāyaṇaṃ 
asāsae sarīrammi | raiṃ novalabhām ahaṃ /
pacchā purā va caiyavve | pheṇabubbuyasannibhe 
māṇusatte asārammi | vāhīrogāṇa ālae /
jarāmaraṇaghatthammi | khaṇaṃ pi na ramām ahaṃ 
jammaṃ dukkhaṃ jarā dukkhaṃ | rogāṇi maraṇāṇi ya /
aho dukkho hu saṃsāro | jattha kīsanti jantavo 
khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraṇṇaṃ ca | puttadāraṃ ca bandhavā /
caittāṇaṃ imaṃ dehaṃ | gantavvam avasassa me 
jaha kimpāgaphalāṇa | pariṇāmo na sundaro /
evaṃ bhuttāṇa bhogāṇaṃ | pariṇāmo na sundaro 
addhāṇaṃ jo mahantaṃ tu | appāheo pavajjaī /
gacchanto so duhī hoi | chuhātaṇhāe pīḍio 
evaṃ dhammaṃ akāūṇaṃ | jo gacchai paraṃ bhavaṃ /
gacchanto so duhī hoi | vāhīrogehiṃ pīḍio 
addhāṇaṃ jo mahantaṃ tu | sapāheo pavajjaī /
gacchanto so suhī hoi | chuhātanhāvivajjio 
evaṃ dhammaṃ pi kāūṇaṃ | jo gacchai paraṃ bhavaṃ /
gacchanto so suhī hoi | appakamme aveyaṇe 
jahā gehe palittammi | tassa gehassa jo pahū /
sārabhaṇḍāṇi nīṇei | asāraṃ avaijjhai 
evaṃ loe palittammi | jarāe maraṇeṇa ya /
appāṇaṃ tāraissāmi | tubbhehiṃ aṇumannio 
taṃ binti ammāpiyaro | sāmaṇṇa putta duccaraṃ /
guṇāṇaṃ tu sahassāiṃ | dhāreyavvāiṃ bhikkhuṇā 
samayā savvabhūesu | sattumittesu vā jage /
pāṇāivāyaviraī | jāvaj jīvāe dukkaraṃ 
niccakālappamatteṇaṃ | musāvāyavivajjaṇaṃ /
bhāsiyavvaṃ hiyaṃ saccaṃ | niccāutteṇa dukkaraṃ 
dantasohaṇam āissa | adattassa vivajjaṇaṃ /
aṇavajjesaṇijjassa | giṇhaṇā avi dukkaraṃ 
viraī abambhacerassa | kāmabhogarasannuṇā /
uggaṃ mahavvayaṃ bambhaṃ | dhāreyavvaṃ sudukkaraṃ 
dhaṇadhannapesavaggesu | pariggahavivajjaṇaṃ /
savvārambhapariccāo | nimmamattaṃ sudukkaraṃ 
cauvvihe vi āhāre | rāībhoyaṇavajjaṇā /
sannihīsaṃcao ceva | vajjeyavvo sudukkaraṃ 
chuhā taṇhā ya sīuṇhaṃ | daṃsamasagaveyaṇā /
akkosā dukkhasejjā ya | taṇaphāsā jallam eva ya 
tālaṇā tajjaṇā ceva | vahabandhaparīsahā /
dukkhaṃ bhikkhāyariyā | jāyaṇā ya alābhayā 
kāvoyā jā imā vittī | kesaloo ya dāruṇo /
dukkhaṃ bambhavvayaṃ ghoraṃ | dhāreu ya mahappaṇo 
suhoio tumaṃ puttā | sukumālo sumajjio /
na hu sī pabhū tumaṃ puttā | sāmaṇṇam aṇupāliyā 
jāvaj jīvam avissāmo | guṇāṇaṃ tu mahabbharo /
gurū u lohabhāru vva | jo puttā hoi duvvaho 
āgāse gaṃgasou vva | paḍisou vva duttaro /
bāhāhiṃ sāgaro ceva | tariyavvo guṇodahī 
vāluyākavalo ceva | nirassāe u saṃjame /
asidhārāgamaṇaṃ ceva | dukkaraṃ cariuṃ tavo 
ahī vegantadiṭhīe | caritte putta dukkare /
javā lohamayā ceva | cāveyavvā sudukkaraṃ 
jahā aggisihā dittā | pāuṃ hoi sudukkarā /
tahā dukkaraṃ kareuṃ je | tāruṇṇe samaṇattaṇaṃ 
jahā dukkhaṃ bhareuṃ je | hoi vāyassa kotthalo /
tahā dukkhaṃ kareuṃ je | kīveṇaṃ samaṇattaṇaṃ 
jahā tulāe toleuṃ | dukkaro mandaro girī /
tahā nihuyanīsaṃkaṃ | dukkaraṃ samaṇattaṇaṃ 
jahā bhuyāhiṃ tariuṃ | dukkaraṃ rayaṇāyaro /
tahā aṇuvasanteṇaṃ | dukkaraṃ damasāgaro 
bhuṃja māṇussae bhoge | paṃcalakkhaṇae tumaṃ /
bhuttabhogī tao jāyā | pacchā dhammaṃ carissasi 
so bei ammāpiyaro | evam eyaṃ jahā phuḍaṃ /
iha loe nippivāsassa | natthi kiṃcivi dukkaraṃ 
sārīramāṇasā ceva | veyaṇāo aṇantaso /
mae soḍhāo bhīmāo | asaiṃ dukkhabhayāṇi ya 
jarāmaraṇakantāre | cāurante bhayāgare /
mae soḍhāṇi bhīmāṇi | jammāṇi maraṇāṇi ya 
jahā ihaṃ agaṇī uṇho | etto 'antaguṇe tahiṃ /
naraesu veyaṇā uṇhā | assāyā veiyā mae 
jahā imaṃ ihaṃ sīyaṃ | etto 'antaguṇe tahiṃ /
naraesu veyaṇā sīyā | assāyā veiyā mae 
kandanto kaṃdukumbhīsu | uḍḍhapāo ahosiro /
huyāsaṇe jalantammi | pakkapuvvo aṇantaso 
mahādavaggisaṃkāse | marummi vairavālue /
kalambavāluyāe ya | daḍḍhapuvvo aṇantaso 
rasanto kandukumbhīsu | uḍḍhaṃ baddho abandhavo /
karavattakarakayāīhiṃ | chinnapuvvo aṇantaso 
aitikkhakaṇagāiṇṇe | tuṃge simbalipāyave /
kheviyaṃ pāsabaddheṇaṃ | kaḍḍhokaḍḍhāhiṃ dukkaraṃ 
mahājantesu ucchū vā | ārasanto subheravaṃ ũ/
pīḍio mi sakammehiṃ | pāvakammo aṇantaso 
kūvanto kolasuṇaehiṃ | sāmehiṃ sabalehi ya /
phāḍio phālio chinno | vipphuranto aṇegaso 
asīhi ayasivaṇṇāhiṃ | bhallehiṃ paisehi ya /
chinno bhinno vibhinno ya | oiṇṇo pāvakammuṇā 
avaso loharahe jutto | jalante samilājue /
coio tottajuttehiṃ | rojjho vā jaha pāḍio 
huyāsaṇe jalantammi | ciyāsu mahiso viva /
daḍḍho pakko ya avaso | pāvakammehi pāvio 
balā saṃḍāsatuṇḍehiṃ | lohatuṇḍehi pakkhihiṃ /
vilutto vilavanto haṃ | ḍhaṃkagiddhehi 'antaso 
taṇhākilanto dhāvanto | patto veyaraṇiṃ nadiṃ /
jalaṃ pāhiṃ ti cintanto | khuradhārāhiṃ vivāio 
uṇhābhitatto saṃpatto | asipattaṃ mahāvaṇaṃ /
asipattehiṃ paḍantehiṃ | chinnapuvvo aṇegaso 
muggarehiṃ musaṃṭhīhiṃ | sūlehiṃ musalehi ya /
gayāsaṃ bhaggagattehiṃ | pattaṃ dukkhaṃ aṇantaso 
khurehiṃ tikkhadhārehiṃ | churiyāhiṃ kappaṇīhi ya /
kappio phālio chinno | ukkitto ya aṇegaso 
pāsehiṃ kūḍajālehiṃ | mio vā avaso ahaṃ /
vāhio baddharuddho vā | bahū ceva vivāio 
galehiṃ magarajālehiṃ | maccho vā avaso ahaṃ /
ullio phālio gahio | mārio ya aṇantaso 
vīdaṃsaehi jālehiṃ | leppāhiṃ sauṇo viva /
gahio laggo baddho ya | mārio ya aṇantaso 
kuhāḍapharasumāīhiṃ | vaḍḍhaīhiṃ dumo viva /
kuio phālio chinno | tacchio ya aṇantaso 
caveḍamuṭhimāīhiṃ | kumārehiṃ ayaṃ piva /
tāḍio kuio bhinno | cuṇṇio ya aṇantaso 
tattāiṃ tambalohāiṃ | tauyāiṃ sīsayāṇi ya /
pāio kalakalantāiṃ | ārasanto subheravaṃ 
tuhaṃ piyāiṃ maṃsāiṃ | khaṇḍāiṃ sollagāṇi ya /
khāvio misamaṃsāiṃ | aggivaṇṇāi 'egaso 
tuhaṃ piyā surā sīhū | merao ya mahūṇi ya /
pāio mi jalantīo | vasāo ruhirāṇi ya 
niccaṃ bhīeṇa tattheṇa | duhieṇa vahieṇa ya /
paramā duhasaṃbaddhā | veyaṇā veditā mae 
tivvacaṇḍappagāḍhāo | ghorāo aidussahā /
mahabbhayāo bhīmāo | naraesu veditā mae 
jārisā māṇuse loe | tāyā dīsanti veyaṇā /
etto aṇantaguṇiyā | naraesu dukkhaveyaṇā 
savvabhavesu assāyā | veyaṇā veditā mae /
nimesantaramittaṃ pi | jaṃ sātā natthi veyaṇā 
taṃ bintammāpiyaro | chandeṇaṃ putta pavvayā /
navaraṃ puṇa sāmaṇṇe | dukkhaṃ nippaḍikammayā 
so bei ammāpiyaro | evam eyaṃ jahā phuḍaṃ /
paḍikammaṃ ko kuṇaī | araṇṇe miyapakkhiṇaṃ 
egabbhūe araṇṇe va | jahā u caraī mige /
evaṃ dhammaṃ carissāmi | saṃjameṇa taveṇa ya 
jayā migassa āyaṃko | mahāraṇṇammi jāyaī /
accantaṃ rukkhamūlammi | ko -aṃ tāhe tigicchaī 
ko vā se osahaṃ dei | ko vā se pucchaī suhaṃ /
ko se bhattaṃ ca pāṇaṃ vā | āharittu paṇāmae 
jayā ya se suhī hoi | tayā gacchai goyaraṃ /
bhattapāṇassa aṭhāe | vallarāṇi sarāṇi ya 
khāittā pāṇiyaṃ pāuṃ | vallarehiṃ sarehi ya /
migacāriyaṃ carittāṇaṃ | gacchaī migacāriyaṃ 
evaṃ samuṭhio bhikkhū | evameva aṇegae /
migacāriyaṃ carittāṇaṃ | uḍḍhaṃ pakkamaī disaṃ 
jahā mige ege aṇegacārī | aṇegavāse dhuvagoyare ya /
evaṃ muṇī goyariyaṃ paviṭhe | no hīlae no vi ya khiṃsaejjā 
migacāriyaṃ carissāmi | evaṃ puttā jahā suhaṃ /
ammāpiīhi 'unnāo | jahāi uvahiṃ tahā 
miyacāriyaṃ carissāmi | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇiṃ /
tubbhehiṃ ambaṇunnāo | gaccha putta jahā suhaṃ 
evaṃ so ammāpiyaro | aṇumāṇittāṇa bahuvihaṃ /
mamattaṃ chindaī tāhe | mahānāgo vva kaṃcuyaṃ 
iḍḍhī vittaṃ ca mitte ya | puttadāraṃ ca nāyao /
reṇuyaṃ va paḍe laggaṃ | niddhuṇittāṇa niggao 
paṃcamahavvayajutto | paṃcahi samio tiguttigutto ya /
sabbhintarabāhirao | tavokammaṃsi ujjutto 
nimmamo nirahaṃkāro | nisaṃgo cattagāravo /
samo ya savvabhūesu | tasesu thāvaresu ya 
lābhālābhe suhe dukkhe | jīvie maraṇe tahā /
samo nindāpasaṃsāsu | tahā māṇāvamāṇao 
gāravesuṃ kasāesuṃ | daṇḍasallabhaesu ya /
niyatto hāsasogāo | aniyāṇo abandhaṇo 
aṇissio ihaṃ loe | paraloe aṇissio /
vāsīcandaṇakappo ya | asaṇe aṇasaṇe tahā 
appasatthehiṃ dārehiṃ | savvao pihiyāsave /
ajjhappajjhāṇajogehiṃ | pasatthadamasāsaṇe 
evaṃ nāṇeṇa caraṇeṇa | daṃsaṇeṇa taveṇa ya /
bhāvaṇāhi ya suddhāhiṃ | sammaṃ bhāvettu appayaṃ 
bahuyāṇi u vāsāṇi | sāmaṇṇam aṇupāliyā /
māsieṇa u bhatteṇa | siddhiṃ patto aṇuttaraṃ 
evaṃ karanti saṃbuddhā | paṇḍiyā paviyakkhaṇā /
viṇiaanti bhogesu | miyāputte jahāmisī 
mahāpabhāvassa mahājasassa | miyāi puttassa nisamma bhāsiyaṃ /
tavappahāṇaṃ cariyaṃ ca uttamaṃ | gaippahāṇaṃ ca tilogavissutaṃ 
viyāṇiyā dukkhavivaddhaṇaṃ dhaṇaṃ | mamattabandhaṃ ca mahābhayāvahaṃ /
suhāvahaṃ dhammadhuraṃ aṇuttaraṃ | dhārejja nivvāṇaguṇāvahaṃ mahaṃ  tti bemi
||
     || miyāputtīyaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/20 mahāniyaṇṭhijjaṃ viṃśatitamam adhyayanam /

siddhāṇa namo kiccā | saṃjayāṇaṃ ca bhāvao /
atthadhammagaiṃ taccaṃ | aṇusaṭhiṃ suṇeha me 
pabhūyarayaṇo rāyā | seṇio magahāhivo /
vihārajattaṃ nijjāo | maṇḍikucchiṃsi ceie 
nāṇādumalayāiṇṇaṃ | nāṇāpakkhiniseviyaṃ /
nāṇākusumasaṃchannaṃ | ujjāṇaṃ nandaṇovamaṃ 
tattha so pāsaī sāhuṃ | saṃjayaṃ susamāhiyaṃ /
nisinnaṃ rukkhamūlammi | sukumālaṃ suhoiyaṃ 
tassa rūvaṃ tu pāsittā | rāiṇo tammi saṃjae /
accantaparamo āsī | aulo rūvavimhao 
aho vaṇṇo aho rūvaṃ | aho ajjassa somayā /
aho khantī aho muttī | aho bhoge asaṃgayā 
tassa pāe u vandittā | kāūṇa ya payāhiṇaṃ /
nāidūramaṇāsanne | paṃjalī paḍipucchaī 
taruṇo si ajjo pavvaio | bhogakālammi saṃjayā /
uvaṭhio si sāmaṇṇe | eyam aṭhaṃ suṇemi tā 
aṇāho mi mahārāya | nāho majjha na vijjaī /
anukampagaṃ suhiṃ vāvi | kaṃci nābhisamemahaṃ 
tao so pahasio rāyā | seṇio magahāhivo /
evaṃ te iḍḍhimantassa | kahaṃ nāho na vijjaī 
homi nāho bhayantāṇaṃ | bhoge bhuṃjāhi saṃjayā /
mittanāīparivuḍo | māṇussaṃ khu sudullahaṃ 
appaṇā vi aṇāho si | seṇiyā magahāhivā /
appaṇā aṇāho santo | kassa nāho bhavissasi 
evaṃ vutto narindo so | susaṃbhanto suvimhio /
vayaṇaṃ assuyapuvvaṃ | sāhuṇā vimhayannio 
assā hatthī maṇussā me | puraṃ anteuraṃ ca me /
bhuṃjāmi māṇuse bhoge | āṇā issariyaṃ ca me 
erise sampayaggammi | savvakāmasamappie /
kahaṃ aṇāho bhavai | mā hu bhante musaṃ vae 
na tumaṃ jāṇe aṇāhassa | atthaṃ potthaṃ ca patthivā /
jahā aṇāho bhavaī | saṇāho vā narāhivā 
suṇeha me mahārāya | avvakkhitteṇa ceyasā /
jahā aṇāho bhavaī | jahā meyaṃ pavattiyaṃ 
kosambī nāma nayarī | purāṇa purabheyaṇī /
tattha āsī piyā majjha | pabhūyadhaṇasaṃcao 
paḍhame vae mahārāya | aulā me acchiveyaṇā /
ahotthā viulo ḍāho | savvagattesu ya patthivā 
satthaṃ jahā parasatikkhaṃ | sarīravivarantare /
āvīlijja arī kuddho | evaṃ me acchiveyaṇā 
tiyaṃ me antaricchaṃ ca | uttamaṃgaṃ ca pīḍaī /
indāsaṇisamā ghorā | veyaṇā paramadāruṇā 
uvaṭhiyā me āyariyā | vijjāmantatigicchayā /
adhīyā satthakusalā | mantamūlavisārayā 
te me tigicchaṃ kuvvanti | cāuppāyaṃ jahāhiyaṃ /
na ya dukkhā vimoyanti | esā majjha aṇāhayā 
piyā me savvasāraṃ pi | dijjā hi mama kāraṇā /
na ya dukkhā vimoei | esā majjha aṇāhayā 
māyā ya me mahārāya | puttasogaduhaiyā /
na ya dukkhā vimoei | esā majjha aṇāhayā 
bhāyaro me mahārāya | sagā jeṭhakaṇiṭhagā /
na ya dukkhā vimoyanti | esā majjha aṇāhayā 
bhaiṇīo me mahārāya | sagā jeṭhakaṇiṭhagā /
na ya dukkhā vimoyanti | esā majjha aṇāhayā 
bhāriyā me mahārāya | aṇurattā aṇuvvayā /
aṃsupuṇṇehiṃ nayaṇehiṃ | uraṃ me parisiṃcaī 
annaṃ pāṇaṃ ca ṇhāṇaṃ ca | gandhamallavilevaṇaṃ /
mae nāyam aṇāyaṃ vā | sā bālā neva bhuṃjaī 
khaṇaṃ pi me mahārāya | pāsāo me na phiaī /
na ya dukkhā vimoei | esā majjha aṇāhayā 
tao haṃ evam āhaṃsu | dukkhamā hu puṇo puṇo /
veyaṇā aṇubhaviuṃ je | saṃsārammi aṇantae 
saiṃ ca jai muccejjā | veyaṇā viulā io /
khanto danto nirārambho | pavvae aṇagāriyaṃ 
evaṃ ca cintaittāṇaṃ | pasutto mi narāhivā /
pariyattantīe rāīe | veyaṇā me khayaṃ gayā 
tao kalle pabhāyammi | āpucchittāṇa bandhave /
khanto danto nirārambho | pavvaio 'agāriyaṃ 
to haṃ nāho jāo | appaṇo ya parassa ya /
savvesiṃ ceva bhūyāṇaṃ | tasāṇa thāvarāṇa ya 
appā naī veyaraṇī | appā me kūḍasāmalī /
appā kāmaduhā dheṇū | appā me nandaṇaṃ vaṇaṃ 
appā kattā vikattā ya | dukkhāṇa ya suhāṇa ya /
appā mittam amittaṃ ca | duppaṭhiyasupaṭhio 
imā hu annā vi aṇāhayā nivā | tamegacitto nihuo suṇehi /
niyaṇṭhadhammaṃ lahiyāṇa vī jahā | sīyanti ege bahukāyarā narā 
jo pavvaittāṇa mahavvayāiṃ | sammaṃ ca no phāsayaī pamāyā /
aniggahappā ya rasesu giddhe | na mūlao chinnai bandhaṇaṃ se 
āuttayā jassa na atthi kāi | iriyāe bhāsāe tahesaṇāe /
āyāṇanikkhevaduguṃchaṇāe | na dhīrajāyaṃ aṇujāi maggaṃ 
ciraṃ pi se muṇḍaruī bhavittā | athiravvae tavaniyamehi bhaṭhe /
