ciraṃ pi appāṇa kilesaittā | na pārae hoi hu saṃparāe 
polleva muṭhī jaha se asāre | ayantie kūḍakahāvaṇe vā /
rāḍhāmaṇī veruliyappagāse | amahagghae hoi hu jāṇaesu 
kusīlaliṃgaṃ iha dhāraittā | isijjhayaṃ jīviya būhaittā /
asaṃjae saṃjayalappamāṇe | viṇigghāyam āgacchai se ciraṃ pi 
visaṃ tu pīyaṃ jaha kālakūḍaṃ | haṇāi satthaṃ jaha kuggahīyaṃ /
eso vi dhammo visaovavanno | haṇāi veyāla ivāvivanno 
je lakkhaṇaṃ suviṇa pauṃjamāṇe | nimittakoūhalasaṃpagāḍhe /
kuheḍavijjāsavadārajīvī | na gacchaī saraṇaṃ tammi kāle 
tamaṃ tameṇeva u se asīle | sayā duhī vippariyāsuvei /
saṃdhāvaī naragatirikkhajoṇiṃ | moṇaṃ virāhettu asāhurūve 
ūddesiyaṃ kīyagaḍaṃ niyāgaṃ | na muṃcaī kiṃci aṇesaṇijjaṃ /
aggī vivā savvabhakkhī bhavittā | itto cue gacchai kau pāvaṃ 
na taṃ arī kaṇṭhachettā karei | jaṃ se kare appaṇiyā durappayā /
se nāhaī maccumuhaṃ tu patte | pacchāṇutāveṇa dayāvihūṇo 
niraṭhiyā naggaruī u tassa | je uttamaṭhaṃ vivajjāsamei /
ime vi se natthi pare vi loe | duhao vi se jhijjai tattha loe 
emeva hā chandakusīlarūve | maggaṃ virāhettu jiṇuttamāṇaṃ /
kurarī vivā bhogarasāṇugiddhā | niraṭhasoyā pariyāvamei 
soccāṇa mehāvi subhāsiyaṃ imaṃ | aṇusāsaṇaṃ nāṇaguṇovaveyaṃ /
maggaṃ kusīlāṇa jahāya savvaṃ | mahāniyaṇṭhāṇa vae paheṇa 
carittamāyāraguṇannie tao | aṇuttaraṃ saṃjama pāliyāṇa /
nirāsave saṃkhaviyāṇa kammaṃ | uvei ṭhāṇaṃ viuluttamaṃ dhuvaṃ 
evuggadante vi mahātavodhaṇe | mahāmuṇī mahāpainne mahāyase /
mahāniyaṇṭhijjam iṇaṃ mahāsuyaṃ | se kāheī mahayā vitthareṇaṃ 
tuṭho ya seṇio rāyā | iṇam udāhu kayaṃjalī /
aṇāhattaṃ jahābhūyaṃ | suṭhu me uvadaṃsiyaṃ 
tujjhaṃ suladdhaṃ khu maṇussajammaṃ | lābhā suladdhā ya tume mahesī /
tubbhe saṇāhā ya sabandhavā ya | jaṃ bhe ṭhiyā magge jiṇuttamāṇa 
taṃ si nāho aṇāhāṇaṃ | savvabhūyāṇa saṃjayā /
khāmemi te mahābhāga | icchāmi aṇusāsiuṃ 
pucchiūṇa mae tubbhaṃ | jhāṇavigghāo jo kao /
nimantiyā ya bhogehiṃ | taṃ savvaṃ marisehi me 
evaṃ thuṇittāṇa sa rāyasīho | aṇagārasīhaṃ paramāi bhattīe /
saoroho sapariyaṇo sabandhavo | dhammāṇuratto vimaleṇa ceyasā 
ūsasiyaromakūvo | kāūṇa ya payāhiṇaṃ /
abhivandiūṇa sirasā | aiyāo narāhivo 
iyaro vi guṇasamiddho | tiguttigutto tidaṇḍavirao ya /
vihaga iva vippamukko | viharai vasuhaṃ vigayamoho  tti bemi ||
     || mahāniyaṇṭhijjaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/21 samuddapālīyam ekaviṃśam adhyayanam /
 
campāe pālie nāma | sāvae āsi vāṇie /
mahāvīrassa bhagavao | sīse so u mahappaṇo 
nigganthe pāvayaṇe | sāvae se vi kovie /
poeṇa vavaharante | pihuṇḍaṃ nagaram āgae 
pihuṇḍe vavaharantassa | vāṇio dei dhūyaraṃ /
taṃ sasattaṃ paigijjha | sadesam aha patthio 
aha pāliyassa gharaṇī | samuddaṃmi pasavaī /
aha bālae tahiṃ jāe | samuddapāli tti nāmae 
khemeṇa āgae campaṃ | sāvae vāṇie gharaṃ /
saṃvaḍḍhaī tassa ghare | dārae se suhoie 
bāvattarī kalāo ya | sikkhaī nīikovie /
jovvaṇeṇa ya saṃpanne | surūve piyadaṃsaṇe 
tassa rūvavaiṃ bhajjaṃ | piyā āṇei rūviṇiṃ /
pāsāe kīlae ramme | devo dogundao jahā 
aha annayā kayāī | pāsāyāloyaṇe ṭhio /
vajjhamaṇḍaṇasobhāgaṃ | vajjhaṃ pāsai vajjhagaṃ 
taṃ pāsiūṇa saṃvegaṃ | samuddapālo iṇam abbavī /
aho 'subhāṇa kammāṇaṃ | nijjāṇaṃ pāvagaṃ imaṃ 
saṃbuddho so tahiṃ bhagavaṃ | paramasaṃvegam āgao /
āpucchammāpiyaro | pavvae aṇagāriyaṃ 
jahittu 'sagganthamahākilesaṃ | mahantamohaṃ kasiṇaṃ bhayāvahaṃ /
pariyāyadhammaṃ cabhiroyaejjā | vayāṇi sīlāṇi parīsahe ya 
ahiṃsasaccaṃ ca ateṇagaṃ ca | tatto ya bambhaṃ apariggahaṃ ca /
paḍivajjiyā paṃca mahavvayāṇi | carijja dhammaṃ jiṇadesiyaṃ vidū 
savvehiṃ bhūehiṃ dayāṇukampī | khantikkhame saṃjayabambhayārī /
sāvajjajogaṃ parivajjayanto | carijja bhikkhū susamāhiindie 
kāleṇa kālaṃ viharejja raṭhe | balābalaṃ jāṇiya appaṇo ya /
sīho va saddeṇa na saṃtasejjā | vayajoga succā na asaccamāhu 
uvehamāṇo u parivvaejjā | piyam appiyaṃ savva titikkhaejjā /
na savva savvattha 'bhiroyaejjā | na yāvi pūyaṃ garahaṃ ca saṃjae 
aṇegachandām iha māṇavehiṃ | je bhāvao saṃpagarei bhikkhū /
bhayabheravā tattha uinti bhīmā | divvā maṇussā aduvā tiricchā 
parīsahā duvvisahā aṇege | sīyanti jatthā bahukāyarā narā / 
se tattha patte na vahijja bhikkhū | saṃgāmasīse iva nāgarāyā 
sīosiṇā daṃsamasā ya phāsā | āyaṃkā vivihā phusanti dehaṃ /
akukkuo tattha 'hiyāsaejjā | rayāi khevejja pure kayāiṃ 
pahāya rāgaṃ ca taheva dosaṃ | mohaṃ ca bhikkhū satataṃ viyakkhaṇo /
meru vva vāeṇa akampamāṇo | parīsahe āyagutte sahejjā 
aṇunnae nāvaṇae mahesī | na yāvi pūyaṃ garahaṃ ca saṃjae /
sa ujjabhāvaṃ paḍivajja saṃjae | nivvāṇamaggaṃ virae uvei 
arairaisahe pahīṇasaṃthave | virae āyahie pahāṇavaṃ /
paramaṭhapaehiṃ ciṭhaī | chinnasoe amame akiṃcaṇe 
vivittalayaṇāi bhaejja tāī | nirovalevāi asaṃthaḍāiṃ /
isīhi ciṇṇāi mahāyasehiṃ | kāeṇa phāsejja parīsahāiṃ 
sannāṇanāṇovagae mahesī | aṇuttaraṃ cariuṃ dhammasaṃcayaṃ /
aṇuttare nāṇadhare jasaṃsī | obhāsaī sūrie vantalikkhe 
duvihaṃ khaveūṇa ya puṇṇapāvaṃ | niraṃgaṇe savvao vippamukke /
tarittā samuddaṃ va mahābhavoghaṃ | samuddapāle apuṇāgamaṃ gae  tti bemi ||
     || samuddapālīyaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/22 rahanemijjaṃ ddhāviṃśam adhyayanam /
 
soriyapuraṃmi nayare | āsi rāyā mahiḍḍhie /
vasudevu tti nāmeṇaṃ | rāyalakkhaṇasaṃjue 
tassa bhajjā duve āsī | rohiṇī devaī tahā /
tāsiṃ doṇhaṃ duve puttā | iṭhā rāmakesavā 
soriyapuraṃmi nayare | āsī rāyā mahiḍḍhie /
samuddavijae nāmaṃ | rāyalakkhaṇasaṃjue 
tassa bhajjā sivā nāma | tīse putto mahāyaso /
bhagavaṃ ariṭhanemi tti | loganāhe damīsare 
so 'riṭhanemināmo u | lakkhaṇassarasaṃjuo /
aṭhasahassalakkhaṇadharo | goyamo kālagacchavī 
vajjarisahasaṃghayaṇo | samacauraṃso jhasoyaro /
tassa rāyamaīkannaṃ | bhajjaṃ jāyai kesavo 
aha sā rāyavarakannā | susīlā cārupehaṇī /
savvalakkhaṇasaṃpannā | vijjusoyāmaṇippabhā 
ahāha jaṇao tīse | vāsudevaṃ mahiḍḍhiyaṃ /
ihāgacchaū kumāro | jā se kannaṃ dadāmi haṃ 
savvosahīhiṃ ṇhavio | kayakouyamaṃgalo /
divvajuyalaparihio | ābharaṇehiṃ vibhūsio 
mattaṃ ca gandhahatthi | vāsudevassa jeṭhagaṃ /
ārūḍho sohae ahiyaṃ | sire cūḍāmaṇī jahā 
aha ūsieṇa chatteṇa | cāmarāhi ya sohie /
dasāracakkeṇa ya so | savvao parivārio 
cauraṃgiṇīe senāe | raiyāe jahakkamaṃ /
turiyāṇa sannināeṇa | divveṇa gagaṇaṃ phuse 
eyārisāe iḍḍhīe | jutīe uttamāi ya /
niyagāo bhavaṇāo | nijjāo vaṇhipuṃgavo 
aha so tattha nijjanto | dissa pāṇe bhayaddue /
vāḍehiṃ paṃjarehiṃ ca | sanniruddhe sudukkhie 
jīviyantaṃ tu saṃpatte | maṃsaṭhā bhakkhiyavvae /
pāsettā se mahāpanne | sārahiṃ iṇam abbavī 
kassa aṭhā ime pāṇā | ee savve suhesiṇo /
vāḍehiṃ paṃjarehiṃ ca | sanniruddhā ya acchahiṃ 
aha sārahī tao bhaṇai | ee bhaddā u pāṇiṇo /
tujjhaṃ vivāhakajjaṃmi | bhoyāveuṃ bahuṃ jaṇaṃ 
soūṇa tassa vayaṇaṃ | bahupāṇiviṇāsaṇaṃ /
cintei se mahāpanno | sāṇukkose jiehiu 
jai majjha kāraṇā ee | hammanti subahū jiyā /
na me eyaṃ tu nissesaṃ | paraloge bhavissaī 
so kuṇḍalāṇa juyalaṃ | suttagaṃ ca mahāyaso /
ābharaṇāṇi ya savvāṇi | sārahissa paṇāmae 
maṇapariṇāme ya kae | devā ya jahoiyaṃ samoiṇṇā /
savviḍḍhīi saparisā | nikkhamaṇaṃ tassa kāuṃ je 
devamaṇussaparivuḍo | sīyārayaṇaṃ tao samārūḍho /
nikkhamiya bāragāo | revayayaṃmi ṭhio bhagavaṃ 
ujjāṇaṃ saṃpatto | oiṇṇo uttimāu sīyāo /
sāhassīi parivuḍo | aha nikkhamaī u cittāhiṃ 
aha se sugandhagandhie | turiyaṃ maukuṃcie /
sayam eva luṃcaī kese | paṃcamuṭhīhiṃ samāhio 
vāsudevo ya -aṃ bhaṇai | luttakesaṃ jiindiyaṃ /
icchiyamaṇorahaṃ turiyaṃ | pāvasū taṃ damīsarā 
nāṇeṇaṃ daṃsaṇeṇaṃ ya | caritteṇa taheva ya /
khantīe muttīe | vaḍḍhamāṇo bhavāhi ya 
evaṃ te rāmakesavā | dasārā ya bahū jaṇā /
ariṭhaṇemiṃ vandittā | abhigayā bāragāpuriṃ 
soūṇa rāyakannā | pavvajjaṃ sā jiṇassa u /
nīhāsā ya nirāṇandā | sogeṇa u samutthiyā 
rāīmaī vicintei | dhiratthu mama jīviyaṃ /
jā haṃ teṇa pariccattā | seyaṃ pavvaiuṃ mama 
aha sā bhamarasannibhe | kuccaphaṇagasāhie /
sayameva luṃcaī kese | dhiimantā vavassiyā 
vāsudevo ya -aṃ bhaṇai | luttakesaṃ jiindiyaṃ /
saṃsārasāgaraṃ ghoraṃ | tara kanne lahuṃ lahuṃ 
sā pavvaiyā santī | pavvāvesī tahiṃ bahuṃ /
sayaṇaṃ pariyaṇaṃ ceva | sīlavantā bahussuyā 
giriṃ revatayaṃ jantī | vāseṇullā u antarā /
vāsante andhayāraṃmi | anto layaṇassa sā ṭhiyā 
cīvarāiṃ visārantī | jahā jāya tti pāsiyā /
rahanemī bhaggacitto | pacchā diṭho ya tīi vi 
bhīyā ya sā tahiṃ daṭhuṃ | egante saṃjayaṃ tayaṃ /
bāhāhiṃ kāu saṃgopphaṃ | vevamāṇī nisīyaī 
aha so vi rāyaputto | samuddavijayaṃgao /
bhīyaṃ paveviyaṃ daṭhuṃ | imaṃ vakkaṃ udāhare 
rahanemī ahaṃ bhadde | surūve cārubhāsiṇi /
mamaṃ bhayāhi suyaṇu | na te pīlā bhavissaī 
ehi tā bhuṃjimo bhoe | māṇussaṃ khu sudullahaṃ /
bhuttabhogī puṇo pacchā | jiṇamaggaṃ carissamo 
daṭhūṇa rahanemiṃ taṃ | bhaggujjoyaparājiyaṃ /
rāīmaī asambhantā | appāṇaṃ saṃvare tahiṃ 
aha sā rāyavarakannā | suṭhiyā niyamavvae /
jāī kulaṃ ca sīlaṃ ca | rakkhamāṇī tayaṃ vae 
jai si rūveṇa vesamaṇo | lalieṇa nalakuvvaro /
tahā vi te na icchāmi | jai si sakkhaṃ purandaro 
dhiratthu te jasokāmī | jo taṃ jīviyakāraṇā /
vantaṃ icchasi āvāuṃ | seyaṃ te maraṇaṃ bhave 
ahaṃ ca bhogarāyassa | taṃ ca si andhagavaṇhiṇo /
mā kule gandhaṇā homo | saṃjamaṃ nihuo cara 
jai taṃ kāhisi bhāvaṃ | jā jā dacchasi nārio /
vāyāiddho vva haḍho | aṭhiappā bhavissasi 
govālo bhaṇḍavālo vā | jahā tad davvaṇissaro /
evaṃ aṇissaro taṃ pi | sāmaṇṇassa bhavissasi 
tīse so vayaṇaṃ soccā | saṃjayāe subhāsiyaṃ /
aṃkuseṇa jahā nāgo | dhamme saṃpaḍivāio 
maṇagutto vayagutto | kāyagutto jiindio /
sāmaṇṇaṃ niccalaṃ phāse | jāvaj jīvaṃ daḍhavvao 
uggaṃ tavaṃ carittāṇaṃ | jāyā doṇṇi vi kevalī /
savvaṃ kammaṃ khavittāṇaṃ | siddhiṃ pattā aṇuttaraṃ 
evaṃ karenti saṃbuddhā | paṇḍiyā paviyakkhaṇā /
viṇiyaanti bhogesu | jahā so purisottamo  tti bemi ||
     || rahanemijjaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/23 kesigoyamijjaṃ trayoviṃśam adhyayanam /

jiṇe pāsi tti nāmeṇa | arahā logapūio /
saṃbuddhappā ya savvannū | dhammatitthayare jiṇe 
tassa logapadīvassa | āsi sīse mahāyase /
kesīkumārasamaṇe | vijjācaraṇapārage 
ohināṇasue buddhe | sīsasaṃghasamāule /
gāmāṇugāmaṃ rīyante | sāvatthiṃ puram āgae 
tinduyaṃ nāma ujjāṇaṃ | tammī nagaramaṇḍale /
phāsue sijjasaṃthāre | tattha vāsam uvāgae 
aha teṇeva kāleṇaṃ | dhammatitthayare jiṇe /
bhagavaṃ vaddhamāṇi tti | savvalogammi vissue 
tassa logapadīvassa | āsi sīse mahāyase /
bhagavaṃ goyame nāmaṃ | vijjācaraṇapārae 
bārasaṃgaviū buddhe | sīsasaṃghasamāule /
gāmāṇugāmaṃ rīyante | se vi sāvatthim āgae 
koṭhagaṃ nāma ujjāṇaṃ | tammī nagaramaṇḍale /
phāsue sijjasaṃthāre | tattha vāsam uvāgae
kesīkumārasamaṇe | goyame ya mahāyase /
ubhao vi tattha vihariṃsu | allīṇā susamāhiyā 
ubhao sīsasaṃghāṇaṃ | saṃjayāṇaṃ tavassiṇaṃ /
tattha cintā samuppannā | guṇavantāṇa tāiṇaṃ 
keriso vā imo dhammo | imo dhammo va keriso /
āyāradhammapaṇihī | imā vā sā va kerisī 
cāujjāmo ya jo dhammo | jo imo paṃcasikkhio /
desio vaddhamāṇeṇa | pāseṇa ya mahāmuṇī 
acelao ya jo dhammo | jo imo santaruttaro /
egakajjapavannāṇaṃ | visese kiṃ nu kāraṇaṃ 
aha te tattha sīsāṇaṃ | vinnāya pavitakkiyaṃ /
samāgame kayamaī | ubhao kesigoyamā 
goyame paḍirūvannū | sīsasaṃghasamāule /
jeṭhaṃ kulam avekkhanto | tinduyaṃ vaṇam āgao 
kesī kumārasamaṇe | goyamaṃ dissamāgayaṃ /
paḍirūvaṃ paḍivattiṃ | sammaṃ saṃpaḍivajjaī 
palālaṃ phāsuyaṃ tattha | paṃcamaṃ kusataṇāṇi ya /
goyamassa nisejjāe | khippaṃ saṃpaṇāmae 
kesīkumārasamaṇe | goyame ya mahāyase /
ubhao nisaṇṇā sohanti | candasūrasamappabhā 
samāgayā bahū tattha | pāsaṇḍā kougā miyā /
gihatthāṇaṃ caṇegāo | sāhassīo samāgayā 
devadāṇavagandhavvā | jakkharakkhasakinnarā /
adissāṇaṃ ca bhūyāṇaṃ | āsī tattha samāgamo 
pucchāmi te mahābhāga | kesī goyamam abbavī /
tao kesiṃ buvantaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
puccha bhante jahicchaṃ te | kesiṃ goyamam abbavī /
tao kesī aṇunnāe | goyamaṃ iṇam abbavī 
cāujjāmo ya jo dhammo | jo imo paṃcasikkhio /
desio vaddhamāṇeṇa | pāseṇa ya mahāmuṇī 
egakajjapavannāṇaṃ | visese kiṃ nu kāraṇaṃ /
dhamme duvihe mehāvi | kahaṃ vippaccao na te 
tao kesiṃ buvantaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī /
pannā samikkhae dhamma | tattaṃ tattaviṇicchiyaṃ 
purimā ujjujaḍā u | vaṃkajaḍā ya pacchimā /
majjhimā ujjupannā u | teṇa dhamme duhā kae 
purimāṇaṃ duvvisojjho u | carimāṇaṃ duraṇupālao /
kappo majjhimagāṇaṃ tu | suvisojjho supālao 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
acelago ya jo dhammo | jo imo santaruttaro /
desio vaddhamāṇeṇa | pāseṇa ya mahājasā 
egakajjapavannāṇaṃ | visese kiṃ nu kāraṇaṃ /
liṃge duvihe mehāvī | kahaṃ vippaccao na te 
kesim evaṃ buvāṇaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī /
vinnāṇeṇa samāgamma | dhammasāhaṇam icchiyaṃ 
paccayatthaṃ ca logassa | nāṇāvihavigappaṇaṃ /
jattatthaṃ gahaṇatthaṃ ca | loge liṃgapaoyaṇaṃ 
aha bhave painnā u | mokkhasabbhūyasāhaṇā /
nāṇaṃ ca daṃsaṇaṃ ceva | carittaṃ ceva nicchae 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
aṇegāṇaṃ sahassāṇaṃ | majjhe ciṭhasi goyamā /
te ya te ahigacchanti | kahaṃ te nijjiyā tume 
ege jie jiyā paṃca | paṃca jie jiyā dasa /
dasahā u jiṇittāṇaṃ | savvasattū jiṇāmahaṃ 
sattū ya ii ke vutte | kesī goyamam abbavī /
tao kesiṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
egappā ajie sattū | kasāyā indiyāṇi ya /
te jiṇittu jahānāyaṃ | viharāmi ahaṃ muṇī 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
dīsanti bahave loe | pāsabaddhā sarīriṇo /
mukkapāso lahubbhūo | kahaṃ viharasī muṇī 
te pāse savvaso chittā | nihantūṇa uvāyao /
mukkapāso lahubbhūo | viharāmi ahaṃ muṇī 
pāsā ya ii ke vuttā | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
rāgaddosādao tivvā | nehapāsā bhayaṃkarā /
te chindittā jahānāyaṃ | viharāmi jahakkammaṃ 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
antohiyayasaṃbhūyā | layā ciṭhai goyamā /
phalei visabhakkhīṇi | sā u uddhariyā kahaṃ 
taṃ layaṃ savvaso chittā | uddharittā samūliyaṃ /
viharāmi jahānāyaṃ | mukko mi visabhakkhaṇaṃ 
layā ya ii kā vuttā | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
bhavataṇhā layā vuttā | bhīmā bhīmaphalodayā /
tam uddhiccā jahānāyaṃ | viharāmi jahāsuhaṃ 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
saṃpajjaliyā ghorā | aggī ciṭhai goyamā /
je ḍahanti sarīratthe | kahaṃ vijjhāviyā tume 
mahāmehappasūyāo | gijjha vāri jaluttamaṃ /
siṃcāmi sayayaṃ dehaṃ | sittā no va ḍahanti me 
aggī ya ii ke vuttā | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
kasāyā aggiṇo vuttā | suyasīlatavo jalaṃ /
suyadhārābhihayā santā | bhinnā hu na ḍahanti me 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
ayaṃ sāhasio bhīmo | duṭhasso paridhāvaī /
jaṃsi goyamamārūḍho | kahaṃ teṇa na hīrasi 
padhāvantaṃ nigiṇhāmi | suyarassīsamāhiyaṃ /
na me gacchai ummaggaṃ | maggaṃ ca paḍivajjaī 
āse ya ii ke vutte | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
maṇo sāhasio bhīmo | duṭhasso paridhāvaī /
taṃ sammaṃ tu nigiṇhāmi | dhammasikkhāi kanthagaṃ 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
kuppahā bahavo loe | jehiṃ nāsanti jantuṇo /
addhāṇe kaha vaante | taṃ na nāsasi goyamā 
je ya maggeṇa gacchanti | je ya ummaggapaṭhiyā /
te savve veiyā majjhaṃ | to na nassāmahaṃ muṇī 
magge ya ii ke vutte | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
kuppavayaṇapāsaṇḍī | savve ummaggapaṭhiyā /
sammaggaṃ tu jiṇakkhāyaṃ | esa magge hi uttame 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
mahāudagavegeṇa | vujjhamāṇāṇa pāṇiṇaṃ /
saraṇaṃ gaī paiṭhā ya | dīvaṃ kaṃ mannasī muṇī 
atthi ego mahādīvo | vārimajjhe mahālao /
mahāudagavegassa | gaī tattha na vijjaī 
dīve ya ii ke vutte | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
jarāmaraṇavegeṇaṃ | vujjhamāṇāṇa pāṇiṇaṃ /
dhammo dīvo paiṭhā ya | gaī saraṇam uttamaṃ 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
aṇṇavaṃsi mahohaṃsi | nāvā viparidhāvaī /
jaṃsi goyamamārūḍho | kahaṃ pāraṃ gamissasi 
jā u sassāviṇī nāvā | na sā pārassa gāmiṇī /
jā nirassāviṇī nāvā | sā u pārassa gāmiṇī 
nāvā ya ii kā vuttā | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
sarīram āhu nāva tti | jīve vuccai nāvio /
saṃsāro aṇṇavo vutto | jaṃ taranti mahesiṇo 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
andhayāre tame ghore | ciṭhanti pāṇiṇo bahū /
ko karissai ujjoyaṃ | savvalogaṃmi pāṇiṇaṃ 
uggao vimalo bhāṇū | savvaloyapabhaṃkaro /
so karissai ujjoyaṃ | savvaloyaṃmi pāṇiṇaṃ 
bhāṇū ya ii ke vutte | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
uggao khīṇasaṃsāro | savvannū jiṇabhakkharo /
so karissai ujjoyaṃ | savvaloyaṃmi pāṇiṇaṃ 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
anno vi saṃsao majjhaṃ | taṃ me kahasu goyamā 
sārīramāṇase dukkhe | bajjhamāṇāṇa pāṇiṇaṃ /
khemaṃ sivam aṇābāhaṃ | ṭhāṇaṃ kiṃ mannasī muṇī 
atthi egaṃ dhuvaṃ ṭhāṇaṃ | logaggaṃmi durāruhaṃ /
jattha natthi jarā maccū | vāhiṇo veyaṇā tahā 
ṭhāṇe ya ii ke vutte | kesī goyamam abbavī /
kesim evaṃ buvaṃtaṃ tu | goyamo iṇam abbavī 
nivvāṇaṃ ti abāhaṃ ti | siddhī logaggam eva ya /
khemaṃ sivaṃ aṇābāhaṃ | jaṃ caranti mahesiṇo 
taṃ ṭhāṇaṃ sāsayaṃ vāsaṃ | loyaggaṃmi durāruhaṃ /
jaṃ saṃpattā na soyanti | bhavohantakarā muṇī 
sāhu goyama pannā te | chinno me saṃsao imo /
namo te saṃsayātīta | savvasuttamahoyahī 
evaṃ tu saṃsae chinne | kesī ghoraparakkame /
abhivandittā sirasā | goyamaṃ tu mahāyasaṃ 
paṃcamahavvayadhammaṃ | paḍivajjai bhāvao /
purimassa pacchimaṃmi | magge tattha suhāvahe 
kesīgoyamao niccaṃ | tammi āsi samāgame /
suyasīlasamukkaṃso | mahatthatthaviṇicchao 
tosiyā parisā savvā | sammaggaṃ samuvaṭhiyā /
saṃthuyā te pasīyantu | bhayavaṃ kesigoyame  tti bemi ||
      || kesigoyamijjaṃ samattaṃ 

U/24 samiīo catuviṃśaṃ adhyayanam /
 
aṭha pavayaṇamāyāo | samiī guttī taheva ya /
paṃceva ya samiīo | tao guttīo āhiyā 
iriyābhāsesaṇādāṇe | uccāre samiī iya /
maṇaguttī vayaguttī | kāyaguttī ya aṭhamā 
eyāo aṭha samiīo | samāseṇa viyāhiyā /
duvālasaṃgaṃ jiṇakkhāyaṃ | māyaṃ jattha u pavayaṇaṃ 
ālambaṇeṇa kāleṇa | maggeṇa jayaṇāya ya /
caukāraṇaparisuddhaṃ | saṃjae iriyaṃ rie 
tattha ālambaṇaṃ nāṇaṃ | daṃsaṇaṃ caraṇaṃ tahā /
kāle ya divase vutte | magge uppahavajjie 
davvao khettao ceva | kālao bhāvao tahā /
jāyaṇā cauvvihā vuttā | taṃ me kittayao suṇa 
davvao cakkhusā pehe | jugamittaṃ ca khettao /
kālao jāva rīijjā | uvautte ya bhāvao 
indiyatthe vivajjittā | sajjhāyaṃ ceva paṃcahā /
tam muttī tap purakkāre | uvautte riyaṃ rie 
kohe māṇe ya māyāe | lobhe ya uvauttayā /
hāse bhae moharie | vikahāsu taheva ca 
eyāiṃ aṭha ṭhāṇāiṃ | parivajjittu saṃjae /
asāvajjaṃ miyaṃ kāle | bhāsaṃ bhāsijja pannavaṃ 
gavesaṇāe gahaṇe ya | paribhogesaṇāya ya /
āhārovahisejjāe | ee tinni visohae 
uggamuppāyaṇaṃ paḍhame | bīe sohejja esaṇaṃ /
paribhoyaṃmi caukkaṃ | visohejja jayaṃ jaī 
ohovahovaggahiyaṃ | bhaṇḍagaṃ duvihaṃ muṇī /
giṇhanto nikkhivanto vā | pauṃjejja imaṃ vihiṃ 
cakkhusā paḍilehittā | pamajjejja jayaṃ jaī /
āie nikkhivejjā vā | duhao vī samie sayā 
uccāraṃ pāsavaṇaṃ | khelaṃ siṃghāṇajalliyaṃ /
āhāraṃ uvahiṃ dehaṃ | annaṃ vāvi tahāvihaṃ 
aṇāvāyam asaṃloe | aṇovāe ceva hoi saṃloe /
āvāyam asaṃloe | āvāe ceva saṃloe 
aṇāvāyam asaṃloe | parassaṇuvaghāie /
same ajjhusire yāvi | acirakālakayaṃmi ya 
vitthiṇṇe dūram ogāḍhe | nāsanne vilavajjie /
tasapāṇabīyarahie | uccārāīṇi vosire 
eyāo paṃca samiīo | samāseṇa viyāhiyā /
etto ya tatto guttīo | vocchāmi aṇupuvvaso 
saccā taheva mosā ya | saccamosā taheva ya /
cautthī asaccamosā ya | maṇaguttīo cauvvihā 
saṃrambhasamārambhe | ārambhe ya taheva ya /
maṇaṃ pavattamāṇaṃ tu | niyattejja jayaṃ jaī 
saccā taheva mosā ya | saccamosā taheva ya /
cautthī asaccamosā ya | vaiguttī cauvvihā 
saṃrambhasamārambhe | ārambhe ya taheva ya /
vayaṃ pavattamāṇaṃ tu | niyattejja jayaṃ jaī 
ṭhāṇe nisīyaṇe ceva | taheva ya tuyaaṇe /
ullaṃghaṇapallaṃghaṇe | indiyāṇa ya juṃjaṇe 
saṃrambhasamārambhe | ārambhaṃmi taheva ya /
kāyaṃ pavattamāṇaṃ tu | niyattejja jayaṃ jaī 
eyāo paṃca samiīo | caraṇassa ya pavattaṇe /
guttī niyattaṇe vuttā | asubhatthesu savvaso 
esā pavayaṇamāyā | je sammaṃ āyare muṇī /
se khippaṃ savvasaṃsārā | vippamuccai paṇḍie  tti bemi ||
     || samiīo samattāu 

U/25 jannaijjaṃ paṃcaviṃśam adhyayanam/

māhaṇakulasaṃbhūo | āsi vippo mahāyaso /
jāyāī jamajannaṃmi | jayaghosi tti nāmao 
indiyaggāmaniggāhī | maggagāmī mahāmuṇī /
gāmāṇuggāmaṃ rīyaṃte | patte vāṇārasiṃ puriṃ 
vāṇārasīe bahiyā | ujjāṇaṃmi maṇorame /
phāsue sejjasaṃthāre | tattha vāsam uvāgae 
aha teṇeva kāleṇaṃ | purīe tattha māhaṇe /
vijayaghosi tti nāmeṇa | jannaṃ jayai veyavī 
aha se tattha aṇagāre | māsakkhamaṇapāraṇe /
vijayaghosassa jannaṃmi | bhikkhamaṭhā uvaṭhie 
samuvaṭhiyaṃ tahiṃ santaṃ | jāyago paḍisehae /
na hu dāhāmi te bhikkhaṃ | bhikkhū jāyāhi annao 
je ya veyaviū vippā | jannaṭhā ya je diyā /
joisaṃgaviū je ya | je ya dhammāṇa pāragā 
je samatthā samuddhattuṃ | param appāṇam eva ya /
tesiṃ annamiṇaṃ deyaṃ | bho bhikkhū savvakāmiyaṃ 
so tattha eva paḍisiddho | jāyageṇa mahāmuṇī /
na vi ruṭho na vi tuṭho | uttimaṭhagavesao 
nannaṭhaṃ pāṇaheuṃ vā | na vi nivvāhaṇāya vā /
tesiṃ vimokkhaṇaṭhāe | iṇaṃ vayaṇam abbavī 
navi jāṇasi veyamuhaṃ | navi jannāṇa jaṃ muhaṃ /
nakkhattāṇa muhaṃ jaṃ ca | jaṃ ca dhammāṇa vā muhaṃ 
je samatthā samuddhattuṃ | param appāṇam eva ya /
na te tumaṃ viyāṇāsi | aha jāṇāsi to bhaṇa 
tassakkhevapamokkhaṃ tu | avayanto tahiṃ dio /
sapariso paṃjalī houṃ | pucchaī taṃ mahāmuṇiṃ 
veyāṇaṃ ca muhaṃ būhi | būhi jannāṇa jaṃ muhaṃ /
nakkhattāṇa muhaṃ būhi | būhi dhammāṇa vā muhaṃ 
je samatthā samuddhattuṃ | param appāṇam eva ya /
eyaṃ me saṃsayaṃ savvaṃ | sāhū kahasu pucchio 
aggihuttamuhā veyā | jannaṭhī veyasā muhaṃ /
nakkhattāṇa muhaṃ cando | dhammāṇa kāsavo muhaṃ 
jahā candaṃ gahāīyā | ciṭhantī paṃjalīuḍā /
vandamāṇā namaṃsantā | uttamaṃ maṇahāriṇo 
ajāṇagā jannavāī | vijjāmāhaṇasaṃpayā /
gūḍhā sajjhāyatavasā | bhāsacchannā ivaggiṇo 
jo loe bambhaṇo vutto | aggīva mahio jahā /
sayā kusalasaṃdiṭhaṃ | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
jo na sajjai āgantuṃ | pavvayanto na soyaī /
ramai ajjavayaṇaṃmi | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ  
jāyarūvaṃ jahāmaṭhaṃ | niddhantamalapāvagaṃ /
rāgadosabhayāīyaṃ | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
tavassiyaṃ kisaṃ dantaṃ | avaciyamaṃsasoṇiyaṃ /
suvvayaṃ pattanivvāṇaṃ | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
tasapāṇe viyāṇettā | saṃgaheṇa ya thāvare /
jo na hiṃsai tiviheṇa | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
kohā vā jai vā hāsā | lohā vā jai vā bhayā /
musaṃ na vayaī jo u | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
cittamantam acittaṃ vā | appaṃ vā jai vā bahuṃ /
na giṇhāi adattaṃ je | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
divvamāṇusatericchaṃ | jo na sevai mehuṇaṃ /
maṇasā kāyavakkeṇaṃ | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
jahā pomaṃ jale jāyaṃ | novalippai vāriṇā /
evaṃ alittaṃ kāmehiṃ | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
aloluyaṃ muhājīviṃ | aṇagāraṃ akiṃcanaṃ /
asaṃsattaṃ gihatthesu | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
jahittā puvvasaṃjogaṃ | nāisaṃge ya bandhave /
jo na sajjai bhogesuṃ | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
pasubandhā savvaveyā ya | jaṭhaṃ ca pāvakammuṇā /
na taṃ tāyanti dussīlaṃ | kammāṇi balavanti hi 
na vi muṇḍieṇa samaṇo | na oṃkāreṇa bambhaṇo /
na muṇī raṇṇavāseṇaṃ | kusacīreṇa tāvaso 
samayāe samaṇo hoi | bambhacereṇa bambhaṇo /
nāṇeṇa u muṇī hoi | taveṇa hoi tāvaso 
kammuṇā bambhaṇo hoi | kammuṇā hoi khattio /
vaiso kammuṇā hoi | suddo havai kammuṇā 
ee pāukare buddhe | jehiṃ hoi siṇāyao /
savvakammavinimmukkaṃ | taṃ vayaṃ būma māhaṇaṃ 
evaṃ guṇasamāuttā | je bhavanti diuttamā /
te samatthā u uddhattuṃ | param appāṇam eva ya 
evaṃ tu saṃsae chinne | vijayaghose ya māhaṇe /
samudāya tayaṃ taṃ tu | jayaghosaṃ mahāmuṇiṃ 
tuṭhe ya vijayaghose | iṇam udāhu kayaṃjalī /
māhaṇattaṃ jahābhūyaṃ | suṭhu me uvadaṃsiyaṃ 
tubbhe jaiyā jannāṇaṃ | tubbhe veyaviūviū /
joisaṃgaviū tubbhe | tubbhe dhammāṇa pāragā 
tubbhe samatthā uddhattuṃ | param appāṇam eva ya /
tam aṇuggahaṃ karehamhaṃ | bhikkheṇaṃ bhikkhu uttamā 
na kajjaṃ majjha bhikkheṇa | khippaṃ nikkhamasū diyā /
mā bhamihisi bhayāvae | ghore saṃsārasāgare 
uvalevo hoi bhogesu | abhogī novalippaī /
bhogī bhamai saṃsāre | abhogī vippamuccaī 
ullo sukkho ya do chūḍhā | golayā maiyāmayā /
do vi āvaḍiyā kuḍḍe | jo ullo so 'ttha laggaī 
evaṃ lagganti dummehā | je narā kāmalālasā /
virattā u na lagganti | jahā se sukkhagolae 
evaṃ se vijayaghose | jayaghosassa antie /
aṇagārassa nikkhanto | dhammaṃ soccā aṇuttaraṃ 
khavittā puvvakammāiṃ | saṃjameṇa taveṇa ya /
jayaghosavijayaghosā | siddhiṃ pattā aṇuttaraṃ   || tti bemi ||
     || jannaijjaṃ samattaṃ 

U/26 sāmāyārī ṣaḍviṃśatitamam adhyayanam /
 
sāmāyāriṃ pavakkhāmi | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇiṃ /
jaṃ carittāṇa nigganthā | tiṇṇā saṃsārasāgaraṃ 
paḍhamā āvassiyā nāma | biiyā ya nisīhiyā ũ/
āpucchaṇā ya taiyā | cautthī paḍipucchaṇā 
paṃcamī chandaṇā nāma | icchākāro ya chaṭhao /
sattamo micchakāro u | tahakkāro ya aṭhamo 
abbhuṭhāṇaṃ ca navamaṃ | dasamī uvasaṃpadā /
esā dasaṃgā sāhūṇaṃ | sāmāyarī paveiyā 
gamaṇe āvassiyaṃ kujjā | ṭhāṇe kujja nisīhiyaṃũ/
āpucchaṇaṃ sayaṃkaraṇe | parakaraṇe paḍipucchaṇaṃ 
chandaṇā davvajāeṇaṃ | icchākāro ya sāraṇe /
micchākāro ya nindāe | tahakkāro paḍissue 
abbhuṭhāṇaṃ gurūpūyā | acchaṇe uvasaṃpadā /
evaṃ dupaṃcasaṃjuttā | sāmāyārī paveiyāũ
puvvillaṃmi caubbhāe | āiccaṃmi samuṭhie /
bhaṇḍayaṃ paḍilehittā | vandittā ya tao guruṃ 
pucchijja paṃjaliuḍo | kiṃ kāyavvaṃ mae iha /
icchaṃ nioiuṃ bhante | veyāvacce va sajjhāe 
veyāvacce niutteṇa | kāyavvaṃ agilāyao /
sajjhāe vā niutteṇa | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇe 
divasassa cauro bhāge | bhikkhū kujjā viyakkhaṇo /
tao uttaraguṇe kujjā | diṇabhāgesu causu vi 
paḍhamaṃ porisi sajjhāyaṃ | bīyaṃ jhāṇaṃ jhiyāyaī /
taiyāe bhikkhāyariyaṃ | puṇo cautthīi sajjhāyaṃ 
āsāḍhe māse dupayā | pose māse cauppayā /
cittāsoesu māsesu | tippayā havai porisī 
aṃgulaṃ sattaratteṇaṃ | pakkheṇaṃ ca duraṃgulaṃ /
vaḍḍhae hāyae vāvi | māseṇaṃ cauraṃgulaṃ 
āsāḍhabahulapakkhe | bhaddavae kattie ya pose ya /
phagguṇavāisāhesu ya | boddhavvā omarattāo 
jeṭhāmūle āsāḍhasāvaṇe | chahiṃ aṃgulehiṃ paḍilehā /
aṭhahiṃ bīyatayaṃmi | taie dasa aṭhahiṃ cautthe 
rattiṃ pi cauro bhāge | bhikkhū kujjā viyakkhaṇo /
tao uttaraguṇe kujjā | rāibhāesu causu vi 
paḍhamaṃ porisi sajjhāyaṃ | bīyaṃ jhāṇaṃ jhiyāyaī /
taiyāe niddamokkhaṃ tu | cautthī bhujjo vi sajjhāyaṃ 
jaṃ nei jayā rattiṃ | nakkhattaṃ taṃmi nahacaubbhāe /
saṃpatte viramejjā | sajjhāyaṃ paosakālammi 
tammeva ya nakkhatte | gayaṇacaubbhāgasāvasesaṃmi /
verattiyaṃ pi kālaṃ | paḍilehittā muṇī kujjā 
puvvillaṃmi caubbhāe | paḍilehittāṇa bhaṇḍayaṃ /
guruṃ vandittu sajjhāyaṃ | kujjā dukkhavimokkhaṇaṃ 
porisīe caubbhāe | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
apaḍikkamittā kālassa | bhāyaṇaṃ paḍilehae 
muhapottiṃ paḍilehittā | paḍilehijja gocchagaṃ /
gocchagalaiyaṃgulio | vatthāiṃ paḍilehae 
uḍḍhaṃ thiraṃ aturiyaṃ | puvvaṃ tā vattham eva paḍilehe /
to biiyaṃ papphoḍe | taiyaṃ ca puṇo pamajjijja 
aṇaccāviyaṃ avaliyaṃ | aṇāṇubandhim amosaliṃ ceva /
chappurimā nava khoḍā | pāṇīpāṇivisohaṇaṃ 
ārabhaḍā sammaddā | vajjeyavvā ya mosalī taiyā /
papphoḍaṇā cautthī | vikkhittā veiyā chaṭhī 
pasiḍhilapalambalolā | egā mosā aṇegarūvadhuṇā /
kuṇai pamāṇipamāyaṃ | saṃkiyagaṇaṇovagaṃ kujjā 
aṇūṇāirittapaḍilehā | avivaccāsā taheva ya /
paḍhamaṃ payaṃ pasatthaṃ | sesāṇi ya appasatthāiṃ 
paḍilehaṇaṃ kuṇanto | mihokahaṃ kuṇai jaṇavayakahaṃ vā /
dei va paccakkhāṇaṃ | vāei sayaṃ paḍicchai vā 
puḍhavīṇāukkāe | teū-vāū-vaṇassai-tasāṇaṃ /
paḍilehaṇāpamatto | chaṇhaṃ pi virāhao hoi 
puḍhavīṇāukkāe | teū-vāū-vaṇassai-tasāṇaṃ /
paḍilehaṇāāutto | chaṇhaṃ saṃrakkhao hoi 
taiyāe porisīe | bhattaṃ pāṇaṃ gavesae /
chaṇhaṃ annayarāe | kāraṇaṃmi samuṭhie 
veyaṇa-veyāvacce | iriyaṭhāe ya saṃjamaṭhāe /
taha pāṇavattiyāe | chaṭhaṃ puṇa dhammacintāe 
niggantho dhiimanto | nigganthī vi na karejja chahiṃ ceva /
thāṇehi u imehiṃ | aṇaikkamaṇāi se hoi 
āyaṃke uvasagge | titikkhayā bambhaceraguttīsu /
pāṇidayā tavaheuṃ | sarīravoccheyaṇaṭhāe 
avasesaṃ bhaṇḍagaṃ gijjha | cakkhusā paḍilehae /
param addhajoyaṇāo | vihāraṃ viharae muṇī 
cautthīe porisīe | nikkhivittāṇa bhāyaṇaṃ /
sajjhāyaṃ tao kujjā | savvabhāvavibhāvaṇaṃ 
porisīe caubbhāe | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
paḍikkamittā kālassa | sejjaṃ tu paḍilehae 
pāsavaṇuccārabhūmiṃ ca | paḍilehijja jayaṃ jaī /
kāussaggaṃ tao kujjā | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇaṃ 
devasiyaṃ ca aīyāraṃ | cintijjā aṇupuvvaso /
nāṇe ya daṃsaṇe ceva | carittammi taheva ya 
pāriyakāussaggo | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
desiyaṃ tu aīyāraṃ | āloejja jahakkamaṃ 
paḍikkamittu nissallo | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
kāussaggaṃ tao kujjā | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇaṃ 
pāriyakāussaggo | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
thuimaṃgalaṃ ca kāūṇa | kālaṃ saṃpaḍilehae 
paḍhamaṃ porisi sajjhāyaṃ | bitiyaṃ jhāṇaṃ jhiyāyaī /
taiyāe niddamokkhaṃ tu | sajjhāyaṃ tu cautthie 
porisīe cautthīe | kālaṃ tu paḍilehiyā /
sajjhāyaṃ tu tao kujjā | abohento asaṃjae 
porisīe caubbhāe | vandiūṇa tao guruṃ /
paḍikkamittu kālassa | kālaṃ tu paḍilehae 
āgae kāyavossagge | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇe /
kāussaggaṃ tao kujjā | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇaṃ 
rāiyaṃ ca aīyāraṃ | cintijja aṇupuvvaso /
nāṇaṃmi daṃsaṇaṃmi ya | carittaṃmi tavaṃmi ya 
pāriyakāussaggo | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
rāiyaṃ tu aīyāraṃ | āloejja jahakkamaṃ 
paḍikkamittu nissalo | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
kāussaggaṃ tao kujjā | savvadukkhavimokkhaṇaṃ 
kiṃ tavaṃ paḍivajjāmi | evaṃ tattha vicintae /
kāussaggaṃ tu pārittā | vandaī ya tao guruṃ 
pāriyakāussaggo | vandittāṇa tao guruṃ /
tavaṃ tu paḍivajjejjā | kujjā siddhāṇa saṃthavaṃ 
esā sāmāyārī | samāseṇa viyāhiyā /
jaṃ carittā bahū jīvā | tiṇṇā saṃsārasāgaraṃ  tti bemi ||
     || sāmāyārī samattā 
     
U/27 khaluṃkijjaṃ saptaviṃśatitamam adhyayanam /
 
there gaṇahare gagge | muṇī āsi visārae /
āiṇṇe gaṇibhāvammi | samāhiṃ paḍisaṃdhae 
vahaṇe vahamāṇassa | kantāraṃ aivattaī /
joge vahamāṇassa | saṃsāro aivattaī 
khaluṃke jo u joei | vihammāṇo kilissaī /
asamāhiṃ ca veei | tottao se ya bhajjaī 
egaṃ ḍasai pucchaṃmi | egaṃ vindhai 'bhikkhaṇaṃ /
ego bhaṃjai samilaṃ | ego uppahapaṭhio 
ego paḍai pāseṇaṃ | nivesai nivajjaī /
ukkuddai upphiḍai | saḍhe bālagavī vae 
māī muddheṇa paḍai | kuddhe gacche paḍippahaṃ /
mayalakkheṇa ciṭhaī | vegeṇa ya pahāvaī 
chinnāle chindai selliṃ | duddanto bhaṃjae jugaṃ /
se vi ya sussuyāittā | ujjahittā palāyae 
khaluṃkā jārisā jojjā | dussīsā vi hu tārisā /
joiyā dhammajāṇammi | bhajjantī dhiidubbalā 
iḍḍhīgāravie ege | ege 'ttha rasagārave /
sāyāgāravie ege | ege sucirakohaṇe 
bhikkhālasie ege | ege omāṇabhīrue /
thaddhe ege aṇusasammī | heūhiṃ kāraṇehi ya 
so vi antarabhāsillo | dosam eva pakuvvaī /
āyariyāṇaṃ tu vayaṇaṃ | paḍikūlei 'bhikkhaṇaṃ 
na sā mamaṃ viyāṇāi | na ya sā majjha dāhiī /
niggayā hohiī manne | sāhū anno 'ttha vaccau 
pesiyā paliuṃcanti te | pariyanti samantao /
rāyaveṭhiṃ ca mannantā | karenti bhiuḍiṃ muhe 
vāiyā saṃgahiyā ceva | bhattapāṇeṇa posiyā /
jāyapakkhā jahā haṃsā | pakkamanti diso disiṃ 
aha sārahī vicintei | khaluṃkehiṃ samāgao /
kiṃ majjha duṭhasīsehiṃ | appā me avasīyaī 
jārisā mama sīsāo | tārisā galigaddahā /
galigaddahe jahittāṇaṃ | daḍhaṃ pagiṇhaī tavaṃ 
miumaddavasaṃpanno | gambhīro susamāhio /
viharai mahiṃ mahappā | sīlabhūeṇa appaṇā  tti bemi ||
     || khaluṃkijjaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/28 mokkhamaggagaī aṣāviṃśatitamam adhyayanam /
 
mokkhamaggagaiṃ taccaṃ | suṇeha jiṇabhāsiyaṃ /
caukāraṇasaṃjuttaṃ | nāṇadaṃsaṇalakkhaṇaṃ 
nāṇaṃ ca daṃsaṇaṃ ceva | carittaṃ ca tavo tahā /
esa maggu tti pannatto | jiṇehiṃ varadaṃsihiṃ 
nāṇaṃ ca daṃsaṇaṃ ceva | carittaṃ ca tavo tahā /
eyamaggam aṇuppattā | jīvā gacchanti soggaiṃ 
tattha paṃcavihaṃ nāṇaṃ | suyaṃ ābhinibohiyaṃ /
ohināṇaṃ tu taiyaṃ | maṇanāṇaṃ ca kevalaṃ 
eyaṃ paṃcavihaṃ nāṇaṃ | davvāṇa ya guṇāṇa ya /
pajjavāṇa ya savvesiṃ | nāṇaṃ nāṇīhi daṃsiyaṃ 
guṇāṇam āsao davvaṃ | egadavvassiyā guṇā /
lakkhaṇaṃ pajjavāṇaṃ tu | ubhao assiyā bhave 
dhammo ahammo āgāsaṃ | kālo puggala-jantavo /
esa logo tti pannatto | jiṇehiṃ varadaṃsihiṃ 
dhammo ahammo āgāsaṃ | davvaṃ ikkikkam āhiyaṃ /
aṇantāṇi ya davvāṇi | kālo puggala-jantavo 
gailakkhaṇo u dhammo | ahammo ṭhāṇalakkhaṇo /
bhāyaṇaṃ savvadavvāṇaṃ | nahaṃ ogāhalakkhaṇaṃ 
vattaṇālakkhaṇo kālo | jīvo uvaogalakkhaṇo /
nāṇeṇaṃ daṃsaṇeṇaṃ ca | suheṇa ya duheṇa ya 
nāṇaṃ ca daṃsaṇaṃ ceva | carittaṃ ca tavo tahā /
vīriyaṃ uvaogo ya | eyaṃ jīvassa lakkhaṇaṃ 
saddandhayāraṇujjoo | pahā chāyā tave i vā /
vaṇṇarasagandhaphāsā | puggalāṇaṃ tu lakkhaṇaṃ 
egattaṃ ca puhattaṃ ca | saṃkhā saṃṭhāṇam eva ya /
saṃjogā ya vibhāgā ya | pajjavāṇaṃ tu lakkhaṇaṃ 
jīvājīvā ya bandho ya | puṇṇaṃ pāvāsavā tahā /
saṃvaro nijjarā mokkho | santee tahiyā nava 
tahiyāṇaṃ tu bhāvāṇaṃ | sabbhāve uvaesaṇaṃ /
bhāveṇaṃ saddahantassa | sammattaṃ taṃ viyāhiyaṃ 
nisagguvaesaruī | āṇaruī sutta-bīyaruim eva /
abhigama-vitthāraruī | kiriyā-saṃkheva-dhammaruī 
bhūyattheṇāhigayā | jīvājīvā ya puṇṇapāvaṃ ca /
sahasammuiyāsavasaṃvaro ya | roei u nisaggo 
jo jiṇadiṭhe bhāve | cauvvihe saddahāi sayam eva /
emeva nannaha ttiya | sa nisaggarui tti nāyavvo 
ee ceva u bhāve | uvaiṭhe jo pareṇa saddahaī /
chaumattheṇa jiṇeṇa va | uvaesarui tti nāyavvo 
rāgo doso moho | annāṇaṃ jassa avagayaṃ hoi /
āṇāe roeṃto | so khalu āṇāruī nāmaṃ 
jo suttam ahijjanto | sueṇa ogāhaī u sammattaṃ /
aṃgeṇa bahireṇa va | so suttarui tti nāyavvo 
egeṇa aṇegāiṃ | payāiṃ jo pasaraī u sammattaṃ /
udae vva tellabindū | so bīyarui tti nāyavvo 
so hoi abhigamaruī | suyanāṇaṃ jeṇa atthao diṭhaṃũ/
ekkārasa aṃgāiṃ | paiṇṇagaṃ diṭhivāo ya 
davvāṇa savvabhāvā | savvapamāṇehi jassa uvaladdhā /
savvāhi nayavihīhiṃ | vitthārarui tti nāyavvo 
daṃsaṇanāṇacaritte | tavaviṇae savvasamiiguttīsu /
jo kiriyābhāvaruī | so khalu kiriyāruī nāma 
aṇabhiggahiyakudiṭhī | saṃkhevarui tti hoi nāyavvo /
avisārao pavayaṇe | aṇabhiggahio ya sesesu 
jo atthikāyadhammaṃ | suyadhammaṃ khalu carittadhammaṃ ca /
saddahai jiṇābhihiyaṃ | so dhammarui tti nāyavvo 
paramatthasaṃthavo vā | sudiṭhaparamatthasevaṇaṃ vā vi /
vāvannakudaṃsaṇavajjaṇā ya | sammattasaddahaṇā 
natthi carittaṃ sammatta | vihūṇaṃ daṃsaṇe u bhaiyavvaṃ /
sammattacarittāiṃ | jugavaṃ puvvaṃ va sammattaṃ 
nādaṃsaṇissa nāṇaṃ | nāṇeṇa viṇā na hunti caraṇaguṇā /
aguṇissa natthi mokkho | natthi amokkhassa nivvāṇaṃ 
nissaṃkiya-nikkaṃkhi | nivvitigicchā amūḍhadiṭhī ya /
uvavūha-thirīkaraṇe | vacchalla-pabhāvaṇe aṭha 
sāmāiyattha paḍhamaṃ | cheovaṭhāvaṇaṃ bhave bīyaṃ /
parihāravisuddhīyaṃ | suhumaṃ taha saṃparāyaṃ ca 
akasāyam ahakkhāyaṃ | chaumatthassa jiṇassa vā /
eyaṃ cayarittakaraṃ | cārittaṃ hoi āhiyaṃ 
tavo ya duviho vutto | bāhirabbhantaro tahā /
bāhiro chavviho vutto | emevabbhantaro tavo 
nāṇeṇa jāṇaī bhāve | daṃsaṇeṇa ya saddahe /
caritteṇa nigiṇhāi | taveṇa parisujjhaī 
khavettā puvvakammāiṃ | saṃjameṇa taveṇa ya /
savvadukkhapahīṇaṭhā | pakkamanti mahesiṇo  tti bemi ||
     || mokkhamaggagaī samattā 
     
U/29 sammattaparakkame ekonatriṃśam adhyayanam /
 
suyaṃ me āusaṃ teṇaṃ bhagavayā evam akkhāyaṃ | iha khalu 
sammattaparakkame nāma ajjhayaṇe samaṇeṇa bhagavayā mahāvīreṇaṃ 
kāsaveṇaṃ eveie jaṃ sammaṃ saddahittā pattiyāittā royaittā 
phāsittā pālaittā tīrittā kittaittā sohaittā ārāhittā 
āṇāe aṇupālaittā bahave jīvā sijjhanti bujjhanti 
muccanti parinivvāyanti savvadukkhāṇamantaṃ karenti | tassa -aṃ 
ayamaṭhe evamāhijjai taṃ jahā | saṃvege 1 nivvee 2 dhammasaddhā 3 
gurusāhammiyasurasūsa-yā 4 āloyaṇayā 5 nindaṇayā 6 
garihaṇayā 7 sāmāie 8 cauvvīsatthave 9 vandaṇe 10 
paḍikkamaṇe 11 kāussagge 12 paccakkhāṇe 13 thavathuīmaṃgale 14 
kālapaḍilehaṇayā 15 pāyacchittakaraṇe 16 khamāvayaṇayā 17 
sajjhāe 18 vāyaṇayā 19 paḍipucchaṇayā 20 
paḍiyaaṇayā 21 aṇuppehā 22 dhammakahā 23 suyassa 
ārāhaṇayā 24 egaggamaṇasaṃnivesaṇayā 25 saṃjame 26 
tave 27 vodāṇe 28 suhasāe 29 appaḍibaddhayā 30 vicittasayaṇāsaṇasevaṇayā 31 
viṇiyaaṇayā 32 saṃbhogapaccakkhāṇe 33 
uvahipaccakkhāṇe 34 āhārapaccakkhāṇe 35 
kasāyapaccakkhāṇe 36 jogapaccakkhāṇe 37 sarīrapaccakkhāṇe 38 
sahāyapaccakkhāṇe 39 bhattapaccakkhāṇe 40 sabbhāvapaccakkhāṇe 41 
paḍirūvaṇayā 42 veyāvacce 43 ||savvaguṇasaṃpuṇṇayā 44 
vīyarāgayā 45 khantī 46 muttī 47 maddave 48 ajjave 49 
bhāvasacce 50 karaṇasacce 51 jogasacce 52 maṇaguttayā 53  
vayaguttayā 54 kāyaguttayā 55 maṇasamādhāraṇayā 56 vayasamādhāraṇayā 57

kāyasamādhāraṇayā 58 nāṇasaṃpannayā 59 
daṃsaṇasaṃpannayā 60 carittasaṃpannayā 61 soindiyaniggahe 62 
cakkhindiyaniggahe 63 ghāṇindiyaniggahe 64 jibbhindiyaniggahe 65 
phāsindiyaniggahe 66 kohavijae 67 māṇavijae 68 
māyāvijae 69 lohavijae 70 pejjadosamicchādaṃsaṇavijae 71 
selesī 72 akammayā 73 
     1 saṃvegeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | saṃvegeṇaṃ aṇuttaraṃ 
dhammasaddhaṃ jaṇayai | aṇuttarāe dhammasaddhāe saṃvegaṃ havvamāgacchai 
aṇantāṇubandhikohamāṇamāyālobhe khavei | kammaṃ na 
bandhai | tappaccaiyaṃ ca -aṃ micchattavisohiṃ kāūṇa daṃsaṇārāhae 
bhavai | daṃsaṇavisohīe ya -aṃ visuddhāe atthegaie teṇeva 
bhavaggahaṇeṇaṃ sijjhaī | sohīe ya -aṃ visuddhāe taccaṃ puṇo 
       bhavaggahaṇaṃ nāikkamai 1 
     2 nivvedeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | nivveeṇaṃ divvamāṇusatericchiesu 
       kāmabhogesu nivveyaṃ havvamāgacchai | savvavisaesu 
       virajjai savvavisaesu virajjamāṇe ārambhapariccāyaṃ karei | 
       ārambhapariccāyaṃ karemāṇe saṃsāramaggaṃ vocchindai siddhimaggaṃ 
       paḍivanne ya bhavai 2 
     3 dhammasaddhāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | dhammasaḍdhāe 
       -aṃ sāyāsokkhesu rajjamāṇe virajjai | āgāradhammaṃ ca -aṃ 
       cayai aṇagārie -aṃ jīve sārīramāṇasāṇaṃ dukkhāṇaṃ 
       cheyaṇabheyaṇasaṃjogāīṇaṃ voccheyaṃ karei avvābāhaṃ ca suhaṃ 
       nivvattei 3 
     4 gurusāhammiyasussūsaṇāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | 
       gurusāhammiyasussūsaṇāe -aṃ viṇayapaḍivattiṃ jaṇayai | viṇayapaḍivanne 
       ya -aṃ jīve aṇaccāsāyaṇasīle neraiyatirikkhajoṇiyamaṇussadevaduggaīo 
       nirumbhai vaṇṇasaṃjalaṇabhattibahumāṇayāe 
       maṇussadevagaīo nibandhai siddhiṃ soggaiṃ ca visohei 
       pasatthāiṃ ca -aṃ viṇayamūlāiṃ savvakajjāiṃ sāhei 
       anne ya bahave jīve viṇiittā bhavai 4 
     5 āloyaṇāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | āloyaṇāe 
       -aṃ māyāniyāṇamicchādaṃsaṇasallāṇaṃ mokkhamaggavigghāṇaṃ  
       aṇantasaṃsārabandhaṇāṇaṃ uddharaṇaṃ karei | ujjubhāvaṃ ca 
       jaṇayai | ujjubhāvapaḍivanne ya -aṃ jīve amāī itthīveyanapuṃsagaveyaṃ 
       ca na bandhai | puvvabaddhaṃ ca -aṃ nijjarei 5 
     6 nindaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | nindaṇayāe 
       -aṃ pacchāṇutāvaṃ jaṇayai | pacchāṇutāveṇaṃ virajjamāṇe karaṇaguṇaseḍhiṃ 
       paḍivajjai karaṇaguṇaseḍhīpaḍivanne ya -aṃ aṇagāre 
       mohaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ ugghāei 6 
     7 garahaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | garahaṇayāe 
       apurekkāraṃ jaṇayai | apurekkāragae -aṃ jīve appasatthehiṃto 
       jogehiṃto niyattei pasatthe ya paḍivajjai pasatthajogapaḍivanne 
       ya -aṃ aṇagāre aṇantaghāipajjave khavei 7 
     8 sāmāieṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | sāmāieṇaṃ 
       sāvajjajogaviraiṃ jaṇayai 8 
     9 cauvvīsatthaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | cauvvīsatthaeṇaṃ daṃsaṇavisohiṃ 
       jaṇayai 9 
    10 vandaṇaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | vandaṇaeṇaṃ nīyāgoyaṃ 
       kammaṃ khavei | uccāgoyaṃ kammaṃ nibandhai | sohaggaṃ ca -aṃ apaḍihayaṃ

       āṇāphalaṃ nivvattei dāhiṇabhāvaṃ ca -aṃ jaṇayai 10 
    11 paḍikkamaṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | paḍikkamaṇeṇaṃ vayachiddāṇi 
       pihei pihiyavayachidde puṇa jīve niruddhāsave 
       asabalacaritte aṭhasu pavayaṇamāyāsu uvautte apuhatte suppaṇihiṃdie 
       viharai 11 
    12 kāussaggeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | kāussaggeṇaṃ tīyapaḍuppannaṃ 
       pāyacchittaṃ visohei | visuddhapāyacchitte ya jīve nivvuyahiyae 
       ohariyabharu vva bhāravahe pasatthajjhāṇovagae suhaṃ 
       suheṇaṃ viharai 12 
    13 paccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | paccakkhāṇeṇaṃ āsavadārāīiṃ 
       nirumbhai | paccakkhāṇeṇaṃ icchānirohaṃ jaṇayai | icchānirohaṃ 
      gae ya -aṃ jīve savvadavvesu viṇīyataṇhe sīibhūe 
      viharai 13 
    14 thavathuimaṃgaleṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | thavathuimaṃgaleṇaṃ 
       nāṇadaṃsaṇacarittabohilābhaṃ jaṇayai | nāṇadaṃsaṇacarittabohilābhasaṃpanne

       ya -aṃ jīve antakiriyaṃ kappavimāṇovavattigaṃ 
       ārāhaṇaṃ ārāhei 14 
    15 kālapaḍilehaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai 
       kālapaḍilehaṇayāe nāṇāvaraṇijjaṃ kammaṃ khavei 15 
    16 pāyacchittakaraṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | pāyacchittakaraṇeṇaṃ 
       pāvavisohiṃ jaṇayai niraiyāre vāvi bhavai | sammaṃ ca -aṃ 
       pāyacchittaṃ paḍivajjamāṇe maggaṃ  ca maggaphalaṃ ca visohei 
       āyāraṃ ca āyāraphalaṃ ca ārāhei 16 
    17 khamāvaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | khamāvaṇayāe 
       palhāyaṇabhāvaṃ jaṇayai | palhāyaṇabhāvam uvagae ya savvapāṇabhūyajīvasattesu

       mettībhāvam uppāei | mettībhāvam uvagae yāvi 
       jīve bhāvavisohiṃ kāūṇa nibbhae bhavai 17 
    18 sajjhāeṇa bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | sajjhāeṇa nāṇāvaraṇijjaṃ 
       kammaṃ khavei 18 
    19 vāyaṇāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | vāyaṇāe nijjaraṃ 
       jaṇayai suyassa ya aṇāsāyaṇāe vaae | suyassa 
       aṇāsāyaṇāe vaamāṇe titthadhammaṃ avalambai | titthadhammaṃ 
       avalambamāṇe mahānijjare mahāpajjavasāṇe bhavai 19 
    20 paḍipucchaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | paḍipucchaṇayāe 
       suttatthatadubhayāiṃ visohei | kaṃkhāmohaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ vocchindai 20 
    21 pariyaaṇāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | pariyaaṇāe vaṃjaṇāiṃ 
       jaṇayai vaṃjaṇaladdhiṃ ca uppāei 21 
    22 aṇuppehāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | aṇuppehāe 
       āuyavajjāo sattakammappagaḍīo ghaṇiyabandhaṇabaddhāo siḍhilabandhaṇabaddhāo

       pakarei dīhakālaṭhiiyāo hassakālaṭhiiyāo 
       pakarei tivvāṇubhāvāo mandāṇubhāvāo 
       pakarei [ bahupaesaggāo appapaesaggāo pakarei ] āuyaṃ ca -aṃ 
       kammaṃ siyā bandhai siyā no bandhai | asāyāveyaṇijjaṃ ca -aṃ 
       kammaṃ no bhujjo bhujjo uvaciṇāi aṇāiyaṃ ca -aṃ aṇavadaggaṃ 
       dīhamaddhaṃ cāurantaṃ saṃsārakantāraṃ khippām eva vīivayai 22 
    23 dhammakahāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | dhammakahāe nijjaraṃ 
       jaṇayai dhammakahāe -aṃ pavayaṇaṃ pabhāvei | pavayaṇapabhāveṇaṃ 
       jīve āgamesassa bhaddattāe kammaṃ nibandhai 23 
    24 suyassa ārāhaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai 
       suyassa annāṇaṃ khavei na ya saṃkilissai 24 
    25 egaggamaṇasaṃnivesaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ ja-yai 
       egaggamaṇasaṃnivesaṇayāe cittanirohaṃ karei 25 
    26 saṃjamaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | saṃjamaeṇaṃ aṇaṇhayattaṃ 
      jaṇayai 26 
    27 taveṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | taveṇaṃ vodāṇaṃ 
       jaṇayai 27 
    28 vodāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | vodāṇeṇaṃ akiriyaṃ 
       jaṇayai akiriyāe bhavittā tao pacchā sijjhai bujjhai 
       muccai parinivvāyai savvadukkhāṇam antaṃ karei 28 
    29 suhasāeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | suhasāeṇaṃ aṇussuyattaṃ 
       jaṇayai aṇussuyāe -aṃ jīve aṇukampae aṇubbhaḍe 
       vigayasoge carittamohaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ khavei 29 
    30 appaḍibaddhayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | appaḍibaddhayāe 
       nissaṃgattaṃ jaṇayai | nissaṃgateṇaṃ jīve ege egaggacitte diyā 
       ya rāo ya asajjamāṇe  appaḍibaddhe yāvi viharai 30 
    31 vivittasayaṇāsaṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai 
         vivittasayaṇāsaṇayāe carittaguttiṃ  jaṇayai | carittagutte ya -aṃ jīve vivittāhāre

         daḍhacaritte egantarae mokkhabhāvapaḍivanne aṭhavihakammagaṇṭhiṃ 
         nijjarei 31 
    32 viniyaayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | viniyaayāe 
         pāvakammāṇaṃ akaraṇayāe abbhuṭhei | puvvabaddhāṇa ya nijjaraṇayāe 
         taṃ niyattei tao pacchā cāurantaṃ saṃsārakantāraṃ 
        vīivayai 32 
    33 saṃbhogapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | saṃbhogapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
       ālambaṇāiṃ khavei | nirālambaṇassa ya āyayaṭhiyā jogā 
       bhavanti | saeṇaṃ lābheṇaṃ saṃtussai paralābhaṃ no āsādei 
       paralābhaṃ no takkei no pīhei no patthei no abhilasai 
       paralābhaṃ aṇassāyamāṇe atakkemāṇe apīhamāṇe apatthemāṇe 
       aṇabhilasamāṇe duccaṃ suhasejjaṃ uvasaṃpajjittā -aṃ 
       viharai 33 
    34 uvahipaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | uvahipaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
       apalimanthaṃ jaṇayai | niruvahie -aṃ jīve nikkaṃkhī uvahimantareṇa 
       ya na saṃkilissaī 34 
    35 āhārapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | āhārapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
       jīviyāsaṃsappaogaṃ vocchindai | jīviyāsaṃsappaogaṃ vocchindittā 
       jīve āhāram antareṇaṃ na saṃkilissai 35 
    36 kasāyapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | kasāyapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
       vīyarāgabhāvaṃ jaṇayai | vīyarāgabhāvapaḍivanne vi ya -aṃ jīve 
       samasuhadukkhe bhavai 36 
    37 jogapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | jogapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
        ajogattaṃ jaṇayai | ajogī -aṃ jīve navaṃ kammaṃ na bandhai 
        puvvabaddhaṃ nijjarei 37 
    38 sarīrapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | sarīrapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
        siddhāisayaguṇakittaṇaṃ nivvattei | siddhāisayaguṇasaṃpanne ya -aṃ 
        jīve logaggam uvagae paramasuhī bhavai 38 
    39 sahāyapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | sahāyapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
       egībhāvaṃ jaṇayai | egībhāvabhūe vi ya -aṃ jīve egattaṃ 
       bhāvemāṇe appajhaṃjhe appakalahe appakasāe appatumaṃtume 
       saṃjamabahule saṃvarabahule samāhie yāvi bhavai 39 
    40 bhattapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | bhattapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ aṇegāiṃ

       bhavasayāiṃ nirumbhai 40 
    41 sabbhāvapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai sabbhāvapaccakkhāṇeṇaṃ 
       aniyaiṃ jaṇayai | aniyaipaḍivanne ya aṇagāre cattāri 
       kevalikammaṃse khavei taṃ jahā veyaṇijjaṃ āuyaṃ nāmaṃ goyaṃ 
      tao pacchā sijjhai bujjhai muccai savvadukkhāṇam antaṃ karei 41 
    42 paḍirūvayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | paḍirūvayāe lāghaviyaṃ 
      jaṇayai laghubhūe -aṃ jīve appamatte pāgaḍaliṃge pasatthaliṃge 
     visuddhasammatte sattasamiisamatte savvapāṇabhūyajīvasattesu 
     vīsasaṇijjarūve appaḍilehe jiindie viulatavasamiisamannāgae 
     yāvi bhavai 42 
    43 veyāvacceṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | veyāvacceṇaṃ titthayaranāmagottaṃ 
       kammaṃ nibandhai 43 
    44 savvaguṇasaṃpannayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | savvaguṇasaṃpannayāe 
      apuṇarāvattiṃ jaṇayai | apuṇarāvattiṃ pattae ya -aṃ jīve 
      sārīramāṇasāṇaṃ dukkhāṇaṃ no bhāgī bhavai 44 
    45 vīyarāgayāeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | vīyarāgayāeṇaṃ nehāṇubandhaṇāṇi

       taṇhāṇubandhaṇāṇi ya vocchindai maṇunnāmaṇunnesu 
       saddapharisarūvarasagandhesu ceva virajjai 45 
    46 khantīe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | khantīe parīsahe 
       jiṇai 46 
    47 muttīe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | muttīe akiṃcaṇaṃ 
       jaṇayai akiṃcaṇe ya jīve atthalolāṇaṃ apatthaṇijjo 
       bhavai 47 
    48 ajjavayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | ajjavayāe kāujjuyayaṃ 
       bhāvujjuyayaṃ bhāsujjuyayaṃ avisaṃvāyaṇaṃ jaṇayai | avisaṃvāyaṇasaṃpannayāe

       -aṃ jīve dhammassa ārāhae bhavai 48 
    49 maddavayāeṇa bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | maddavayāe aṇussiyattaṃ 
       jaṇayai aṇussiyatteṇa jīve miumaddavasaṃpanne aṭha 
       mayaṭhāṇāiṃ niṭhāvei 49 
    50 bhāvasacceṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | bhāvasacceṇaṃ bhāvavisohiṃ 
       jaṇayai bhāvavisohīe vaamāṇe jīve arahantapannattassa 
      dhammassa ārāhaṇayāe abbhuṭhei | arahantapannattassa dhammassa 
      ārāhaṇayāe abbhuṭhittā paralogadhammassa ārāhae havai 50 
    51 karaṇasacceṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | karaṇasacceṇaṃ karaṇasattiṃ 
       jaṇayai | karaṇasacce vaamāṇe jīve jahā vāī tahā kārī 
      yāvi bhavai 52 
    52 jogasacceṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | jogasacceṇaṃ jogaṃ 
      visohei 52 
    53 maṇaguttayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | maṇaguttayāe jīve 
      egaggaṃ jaṇayai | egaggacitte -aṃ jīve maṇagutte saṃjamārāhae 
      bhavai 53 
    54 vayaguttayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | vayaguttayāe nivviyāraṃ 
       ja-yai nivviyāre -aṃ jīve vaigutte ajjhappajogasāhaṇajutte 
      yāvi bhavai 54 
    55 kāyaguttayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | kāyaguttayāe 
      saṃvaraṃ jaṇayai saṃvareṇaṃ kāyagutte puṇo pāvāsavanirohaṃ 
      karei 55 
    56 maṇasamāhāraṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai 
       maṇasamāhāraṇayāe egaggaṃ jaṇayai | egaggaṃ jaṇaittā nāṇapajjave jaṇayai 
       nāṇapajjave jaṇaittā sammattaṃ visohei micchattaṃ ca nijjarei 56 
    57 vayasamāhāraṇayāe bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | vayasamāhāraṇayāe  
       vayasāhāraṇadaṃsaṇapajjave visohei | vayasāhāraṇadaṃsaṇapajjave 
      visohittā sulahabohiyattaṃ nivvattei dullahabohiyattaṃ nijjarei 57 
    58 kāyasamāhāraṇayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai 
       kāyasamāhāraṇayāe carittapajjave visohei | carittapajjave visohittā ahakkhāyacarittaṃ

       visohei ahakkhāyacarittaṃ visohettā cattāri 
       kevalikammaṃse khavei | tao pacchā sijjhai bujjhai muccai 
       parinivvāyai savvadukkhāṇam antaṃ karei 58 
    59 nāṇasaṃpannayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | nāṇasaṃpannayāe 
       jīve saddabhāvāhigamaṃ jaṇayai | nāṇasaṃpanne -aṃ jīve cāurante 
       saṃsārakantāre na viṇassai jahā sūī sasuttā na viṇassai 
       tahā jīve sasutte saṃsāre na viṇassai | nāṇaviṇayatavacarittajoge 
       saṃpāuṇai sasamayaparasamayavisārae ya asaṃghāyaṇijje 
       bhavai 59 
    60 daṃsaṇasaṃpannayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | daṃsaṇasaṃpannayāe  
       bhavamicchattacheyaṇaṃ karei paraṃ na vijjhāyai | paraṃ avijjhāemāṇe 
       aṇuttareṇaṃ nāṇadaṃsaṇeṇaṃ appāṇaṃ saṃjoemāṇe sammaṃ 
       bhāvemāṇe viharai 60 
    61 carittasaṃpannayāe -aṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | carittasaṃpannayāe 
       selesībhāvaṃ jaṇayai | selesiṃ paḍivanne ya aṇagāre cattāri 
       kevalikammaṃse khavei | tao pacchā sijjhai bujjhai muccai 
       savvadukkhāṇam antaṃ karei 61 
    62 soindiyaniggaheṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | soindiyaniggaheṇaṃ 
      maṇunnāmaṇunnesu saddesu rāgadosaniggahaṃ jaṇayai tappaccaiyaṃ kammaṃ 
      na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 62 
    63 cakkhindiyaniggaheṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | cakkhindiyaniggaheṇaṃ 
       maṇunnāmaṇunnesu rūvesu rāgadosaniggahaṃ jaṇayai tappacaiyaṃ 
       kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 63 
    64 ghāṇindiyaniggaheṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | ghāṇindiyaniggaheṇaṃ 
       maṇunnāmaṇunnesu gandhesu rāga dosaniggahaṃ jaṇayai tappaccaiyaṃ 
       kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 64 
    65 jibbhindiyaniggaheṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | jibbhindiyaniggaheṇaṃ 
      maṇunnāmaṇunnesu rasesu rāgadosaniggahaṃ jaṇayai tappaccaiyaṃ 
      kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 65 
    66 phāsindiyaniggaheṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | phāsindiyaniggaheṇaṃ 
       maṇunnāmaṇunnesu phāsesu rāgadosaniggahaṃ jaṇayai tappaccaiyaṃ 
       kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 66 
    67 kohavijaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | kohavijaeṇaṃ khantiṃ 
       jaṇayai kohaveyaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 67 
    68 māṇavijaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | māṇavijaeṇaṃ maddavaṃ 
        jaṇayai māṇaveyaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 68 
    69 māyāvijaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | māyāvijaeṇaṃ 
       ajjavaṃ jaṇayai māyāveyaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca 
       nijjarei 69 
    70 lobhavijaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ jaṇayai | lobhavijaeṇaṃ saṃtosaṃ 
       jaṇayai lobhaveyaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ na bandhai puvvabaddhaṃ ca nijjarei 70 
    71 pijjadosamicchādaṃsaṇavijaeṇaṃ bhante jīve kiṃ 
  jaṇayai | pijjadosamicchādaṃsaṇavijaeṇaṃ nāṇadaṃsaṇacarittārāhaṇayāe abbhuṭhei |
aṭhavihassa 
        kammassa kammagaṇṭhivimoyaṇayāe tappaḍhamayāe jahāṇupuvvīe 
       aṭhavīsaivihaṃ mohaṇijjaṃ kammaṃ ugghāei paṃcavihaṃ 
       nāṇāvaraṇijjaṃ navavihaṃ daṃsaṇāvaraṇijjaṃ paṃcavihaṃ antarāiyaṃ 
       ee tinni vi kammaṃse jugavaṃ khavei | tao pacchā aṇuttaraṃ 
       kasiṇaṃ paḍipuṇṇaṃ nirāvaraṇaṃ vitimiraṃ visuddhaṃ logālogappabhāvaṃ 
       kevalavaranāṇadaṃsaṇaṃ samuppāḍei | jāva sajogī bhavai 
       tāva iriyāvahiyaṃ kammaṃ nibandhai suhapharisaṃ dusamayaṭhiiyaṃ | taṃ 
       paḍhamasamae baddhaṃ biiyasamae veiyaṃ taiyasamae nijjiṇṇaṃ taṃ 
       baddhaṃ puṭhaṃ udīriyaṃ veiyaṃ nijjiṇṇaṃ seyāle ya akammaṃ cāvi 
       bhavai 71 
    72 aha āuyaṃ pālaittā antomuhuttaddhāvasesāe joganirohaṃ 
       karemāṇe suhumakiriyaṃ appaḍivāiṃ sukkajjhāṇaṃ jhāyamāṇe 
       tappaḍhamayāe maṇajogaṃ nirumbhai vaijogaṃ nirumbhai kāyajogaṃ 
       nirumbhai āṇapāṇunirohaṃ karei īsi paṃcarahassakkharuccāraṇaṭhāe 
        ya -aṃ aṇagāre samucchinnakiriyaṃ aniyaisukkajjhāṇaṃ 
       jhiyāyamāṇe veyaṇijjaṃ āuyaṃ nāmaṃ gottaṃ ca ee cattāri 
       kammaṃse jugavaṃ khavei 72 
    73 tao orāliyateyakammāiṃ savvāhiṃ vippajahaṇāhiṃ 
       vippajahittā ujjuseḍhipatte aphusamāṇagaī uḍḍhaṃ egasamaeṇaṃ 
       aviggaheṇaṃ tattha gantā sāgārovautte sijjhai bujjhai jāva 
       antaṃ karei 73 
    74 esa khalu sammattaparakkamassa ajjhayaṇassa aṭhe samaṇeṇaṃ 
       bhagavayā mahāvīreṇaṃ āghavie pannavie parūvie daṃsie 
       uvadaṃsie 74  tti bemi ||
             || sammattaparakkame samatte 

U/30 tavamaggaṃ triṃśam adhyayanam /
 
jahā u pāvagaṃ kammaṃ | rāgadosasamajjiyaṃ /
khavei tavasā bhikkhū | tam egaggamaṇo suṇa 
pāṇivahamusāvāyā | adattamehuṇapariggahā virao /
rāībhoyaṇavirao | jīvo bhavai aṇāsavo 
paṃcasamio tigutto | akasāo jiindio /
agāravo ya nissallo | jīvo hoi aṇāsavo 
eesiṃ tu vivaccāse | rāgadosasamajjiyaṃ /
khavei u jahā bhikkhū | tam egaggamaṇo suṇa 
jahā mahātalāyassa | sanniruddhe jalāgame /
ussiṃcaṇāe tavaṇāe | kameṇaṃ sosaṇā bhave 
evaṃ tu saṃjayassāvi | pāvakammanirāsave /
bhavakoḍīsaṃciyaṃ kammaṃ | tavasā nijjarijjai 
so tavo duviho vutto | bāhirabbhantaro tahā /
bāhiro chavviho vutto | evam abbhantaro tavo 
aṇasaṇam ūṇoyariyā | bhikkhāyariyā ya rasapariccāo /
kāyakileso saṃlīṇayā ya | bajjho tavo hoi 
ittariya maraṇakālā ya | aṇasaṇā duvihā bhave /
ittariya sāvakaṃkhā | niravakaṃkhā u biijjiyā 
jo so ittariyatavo | so samāseṇa chavviho /
seḍhitavo payaratavo | ghaṇo ya taha hoi vaggo ya 
tatto ya vaggavaggo | paṃcamo chaṭhao paiṇṇatavo /
maṇaicchiyacittattho | nāyavvo hoi ittario 
jā sā aṇasaṇā maraṇe | duvihā sā viyāhiyā /
saviyāramaviyārā | kāyaciṭhaṃ paī bhave 
ahavā saparikammā | aparikammā ya āhiyā /
nīhārimaṇīhārī | āhāraccheo dosu vi 
omoyaraṇaṃ paṃcahā | samāseṇa viyāhiyaṃ /
davvao khettakāleṇaṃ | bhāveṇaṃ pajjavehi ya 
jo jassa u āhāro | tatto omaṃ tu jo kare /
jahanneṇegasitthāī | evaṃ davveṇa ū bhave 
gāme nagare taha rāyahāṇi | nigame ya āgare pallī /
kheḍe kabbaḍadoṇamuha | paaṇamaḍambasaṃbāhe 
āsamapae vihāre | sannivese samāyaghose ya /
thaliseṇākhandhāre | satthe saṃvaakoe ya 
vāḍesu va racchāsu va | gharesu vā evam ittiyaṃ khettaṃ /
kappai u evamāī | evaṃ khetteṇa ū bhave 
peḍā ya addhapeḍā | gomuttipayaṃgavīhiyā ceva /
sambukkāvaāyaya | gantuṃpaccāgayā chaṭhā 
divasassa porusīṇaṃ | cauṇhaṃ pi u jattio bhave kālo /
evaṃ caramāṇo khalu | kālomāṇaṃ muṇeyavvaṃ 
ahavā taiyāe porisīe | ūṇāi ghāsam esanto /
caubhāgūṇāe vā | evaṃ kāleṇa ū bhave 
itthī vā puriso vā | alaṃkio vā nalaṃkio vā vi /
annayaravayattho vā | annayareṇaṃ va vattheṇaṃ 
anneṇa viseseṇaṃ | vaṇṇeṇaṃ bhāvam aṇumuyante u /
evaṃ caramāṇo khalu | bhāvomāṇaṃ muṇeyavvaṃ 
davve khette kāle | bhāvammi ya āhiyā u je bhāvā /
eehi omacarao | pajjavacarao bhave bhikkhū 
aṭhavihagoyaraggaṃ tu | tahā satteva esaṇā /
abhiggahā ya je anne | bhikkhāyariyam āhiyā 
khīradahisappimāī | paṇīyaṃ pāṇabhoyaṇaṃ /
parivajjaṇaṃ rasāṇaṃ tu | bhaṇiyaṃ rasavivajjaṇaṃ 
ṭhāṇā vīrāsaṇāīyā | jīvassa u suhāvahā /
uggā jahā dharijjanti | kāyakilesaṃ tam āhiyaṃ 
egantam aṇāvāe | itthīpasuvivajjie /
sayaṇāsaṇasevaṇayā | vivittasayaṇāsaṇaṃ 
eso bāhiragatavo | samāseṇa viyāhio /
abbhintaraṃ tavaṃ etto | vucchāmi aṇupuvvaso 
pāyacchittaṃ viṇao | veyāvaccaṃ taheva sajjhāo /
jhāṇaṃ ca viossaggo | eso abbhintaro tavo 
āloyaṇārihāīyaṃ | pāyacchittaṃ tu dasavihaṃ /
jaṃ bhikkhū vahaī sammaṃ | pāyacchittaṃ tam āhiyaṃ 
abbhuṭhāṇaṃ aṃjalikaraṇaṃ | tahevāsaṇadāyaṇaṃ ũ/
gurubhattibhāvasussūsā | viṇao esa viyāhio 
āyariyamāīe | veyāvaccammi dasavihe /
āsevaṇaṃ jahāthāmaṃ | veyāvaccaṃ tam āhiyaṃ 
vāyaṇā pucchaṇā ceva | taheva pariyaaṇā /
aṇuppehā dhammakahā | sajjhāo paṃcahā bhave 
aṭharuddāṇi vajjittā | jhāejjā susamāhie /
dhammasukkāiṃ jhāṇāiṃ | jhāṇaṃ taṃ tu buhāvae 
sayaṇāsaṇaṭhāṇe vā | je u bhikkhū na vāvare /
kāyassa viussaggo | chaṭho so parikittio 
evaṃ tavaṃ tu duvihaṃ | je sammaṃ āyare muṇī /
se khippaṃ savvasaṃsārā | vippamuccai paṇḍio  tti bemi ||
     || tavamaggaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/31 caraṇavihī ekatriṃśam adhyayanam /
 
caraṇavihiṃ pavakkhāmi | jīvassa u suhāvahaṃ /
jaṃ carittā bahū jīvā | tiṇṇā saṃsārasāgaraṃ 
egao viraiṃ kujjā | egao ya pavattaṇaṃ /
asaṃjame niyattiṃ ca | saṃjame ya pavattaṇaṃ 
rāgadose ya do pāve | pāvakammapavattaṇe /
je bhikkhū rumbhaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
daṇḍaṇaṃ gāravāṇaṃ ca | sallāṇaṃ ca tiyaṃ tiyaṃ /
je bhikkhū cayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
divve ya je uvasagge | tahā tericchamāṇuse /
je bhikkhū sahaī jayaī | se na acchai maṇḍale 
vigahākasāyasannāṇaṃ | jhāṇāṇaṃ ca duyaṃ tahā /
je bhikkhū vajjaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
vaesu indiyatthesu | samiīsu kiriyāsu ya /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
lesāsu chasu kāesu | chakke āhārakāraṇe /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
piṇḍoggahapaḍimāsu | bhayaṭhāṇesu sattasu /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
madesu bambhaguttīsu | bhikkhudhammaṃmi dasavihe /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
uvāsagāṇaṃ paḍimāsu | bhikkhūṇaṃ paḍimāsu ya /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
kiriyāsu bhūyagāmesu | paramāhammiesu ya /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
gāhāsolasaehiṃ | tahā asaṃjamammi ya /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
bambhammi nāyajjhayaṇesu | ṭhāṇesu ya samāhie /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
egavīsāe sabale | bāvīsāe parīsahe /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
tevīsāi sūyagaḍe | rūvāhiesu suresu a /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
paṇuvīsabhāvaṇāsu | uddesesu dasāiṇaṃ /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
aṇagāraguṇehiṃ ca | pagappammi taheva ya /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
pāvasuyapasaṃgesu | mohaṭhāṇesu ceva ya /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
siddhāiguṇajogesu | tettīsāsāyaṇāsu ya /
je bhikkhū jayaī niccaṃ | se na acchai maṇḍale 
īi eesu ṭhāṇesu | je bhikkhū jayaī sayā /
khippaṃ so savvasaṃsārā | vippamuccai paṇḍio  tti bemi ||
     || caraṇavihī samattā 
     
U/32 pamāyaṭhāṇaṃ dvātriṃśam adhyayanam /
 
accantakālassa samūlagassa | savvassa dukkhassa u jo pamokkho /
taṃ bhāsao me paḍipuṇṇacittā | suṇeha egantahiyaṃ hiyatthaṃ 
nāṇassa savvassa pagāsaṇāe | annāṇamohassa vivajjaṇāe /
rāgassa dosassa ya saṃkhaeṇaṃ | egantasokkhaṃ samuvei mokkhaṃ 
tassesa maggo guruviddhasevā | vivajjaṇā bālajaṇassa dūrā /
sajjhāyaegantanisevaṇā ya | suttatthasaṃcintaṇayā dhiī ya 
āhāram icche miyam esaṇijjaṃ | sahāyam icche niuṇatthabuddhiṃ /
nikeyam icchejja vivegajoggaṃ | samāhikāme samaṇe tavassī 
na ya labhejjā niuṇaṃ sahāyaṃ | guṇāhiyaṃ vā guṇao samaṃ vā /
ekko vi pāvāi vivajjayanto | viharejja kāmesu asajjamāṇo 
jahā ya aṇḍappabhavā balāgā | aṇḍaṃ balāgappabhavaṃ jahā ya /
emeva mohāyayaṇaṃ khu taṇhā | mohaṃ ca taṇhāyayaṇaṃ vayanti 
rāgo ya doso vi ya kammabīyaṃ | kammaṃ ca mohappabhavaṃ vayanti /
kammaṃ ca jāimaraṇassa mūlaṃ | dukkhaṃ ca jāīmaraṇaṃ vayanti 
dukkhaṃ hayaṃ jassa na hoi moho | moho hao jassa na hoi taṇhā /
taṇhā hayā jassa na hoi loho | loho hao jassa na kiṃcaṇāiṃ 
rāgaṃ ca dosaṃ ca taheva mohaṃ | uddhattukāmeṇa samūlajālaṃ /
je je uvāyā paḍivajjiyavvā | te kittaissāmi ahāṇupuvviṃ 
rasā pagāmaṃ na niseviyavvā | pāyaṃ rasā dittikarā narāṇaṃ /
dittaṃ ca kāmā samabhiddavanti | dumaṃ jahā sāuphalaṃ va pakkhī 
jahā davaggī paurindhaṇe vaṇe | samāruo novasamaṃ uvei /
evindiyaggī vi pagāmabhoiṇo | na bambhayārissa hiyāya kassaī 
vivittasejjāsaṇajantiyāṇaṃ | omāsaṇāṇaṃ damiindiyāṇaṃ /
na rāgasattū dharisei cittaṃ | parāio vāhirivosahehiṃ 
jahā birālāvasahassa mūle | na mūsagāṇaṃ vasahī pasatthā /
emeva itthīnilayassa majjhe | na bambhayārissa khamo nivāso 
na rūvalāvaṇṇavilāsahāsaṃ | na jaṃpiyaṃ iṃgiyapehiyaṃ vā /
itthīṇa cittaṃsi nivesaittā | daṭhuṃ vavasse samaṇe tavassī 
adaṃsaṇaṃ ceva apatthaṇaṃ ca | acintaṇaṃ ceva akittaṇaṃ ca /
itthījaṇassāriyajhāṇajuggaṃ | hiyaṃ sayā bambhavae rayāṇaṃ 
kāmaṃ tu devīhi vibhūsiyāhiṃ | na cāiyā khobhaiuṃ tiguttā /
tahā vi egantahiyaṃ ti naccā | vivittavāso muṇiṇaṃ pasattho 
mokkhābhikaṃkhissa u māṇavassa | saṃsārabhīrussa ṭhiyassa dhamme /
neyārisaṃ duttaram atthi loe | jahitthio bālamaṇoharāo 
ee ya saṃge samaikkamittā | suduttarā ceva bhavanti sesā /
jahā mahāsāgaram uttarittā | naī bhave avi gaṃgāsamāṇā 
kāmāṇugiddhippabhavaṃ khu dukkhaṃ | savvassa logassa sadevagassa /
jaṃ kāiyaṃ māṇasiyaṃ ca kiṃci | tassantagaṃ gacchai vīyarāgo 
jahā ya kiṃpāgaphalā maṇoramā | raseṇa vaṇṇeṇa ya bhujjamāṇā /
te khuḍḍae jīviya paccamāṇā | eovamā kāmaguṇā vivāge 
je indiyāṇaṃ visayā maṇunnā | na tesu bhāvaṃ nisire kayāi /
na yāmaṇunnesu maṇaṃ pi kujjā | samāhikāme samaṇe tavassī 
cakkhussa rūvaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | taṃ rāgaheuṃ tu maṇunnam āhu /
taṃ dosaheuṃ amaṇunnam āhu | samo ya jo tesu sa vīyarāgo 
rūvassa cakkhuṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | cakkhussa rūvaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti /
rāgassa heuṃ samaṇunnam āhu | dosassa heuṃ amaṇunnam āhu 
rūvesu jo gehim uvei tivvaṃ | akāliyaṃ pāvai se viṇāsaṃ /
rāgāure se jaha vā payaṃge | āloyalole samuvei maccuṃ 
je yāvi dosaṃ samuvei tivvaṃ | taṃsi kkhaṇe se u uvei dukkhaṃ /
duddantadoseṇa saeṇa jantū | na kiṃci rūvaṃ avarujjhaī se 
egantaratte ruiraṃsi rūve | atālise se kuṇaī paosaṃ /
dukkhassa saṃpīlam uvei bāle | na lippaī teṇa muṇī virāgā 
rūvāṇugāsāṇugae ya jīve | carācare hiṃsai -egarūve /
cittehi te paritāvei bāle | pīlei attaṭhagurū kiliṭhe 
rūvāṇuvāeṇa pariggaheṇa | uppāyaṇe rakkhaṇasannioge /
vae vioge ya kahaṃ suhaṃ se | saṃbhogakāle ya atittalābhe 
rūve atitte ya pariggahaṃmi | sattovasatto na uvei tuṭhiṃ /
atuṭhidoseṇa duhī parassa | lobhāvile āyayaī adattaṃ 
taṇhābhibhūyassa adattahāriṇo | rūve atittassa pariggahe ya /
māyāmusaṃ vaḍḍhai lobhadosā | tatthāvi dukkhā na vimuccaī se 
mosassa pacchā ya puratthao ya | paogakāle ya duhī durante /
evaṃ adattāṇi samāyayanto | rūve atitto duhio aṇisso 
rūvāṇurattassa narassa evaṃ | katto suhaṃ hojja kayāi kiṃci /
tatthovabhoge vi kilesadukkhaṃ | nivvattaī jassa kaeṇa dukkhaṃ 
emeva rūvammi gao paosaṃ | uvei dukkhohaparaṃparāo /
paduṭhacitto ya ciṇāi kammaṃ | jaṃ se puṇo hoi duhaṃ vivāge 
rūve viratto maṇuo visogo | eeṇa dukkhohaparaṃpareṇa /
na lippae bhavamajjhe vi santo | jaleṇa vā pokkhariṇīpalāsaṃ 
soyassa saddaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | taṃ rāgaheuṃ tu maṇunnam āhu /
taṃ dosaheuṃ amaṇunnam āhu | samo ya jo tesu sa vīyarāgo 
saddassa soyaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | soyassa saddaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti /
rāgassa heuṃ samaṇunnam āhu | dosassa heuṃ amaṇunnam āhu 
saddesu jo gehim uvei tivvaṃ | akāliyaṃ pāvai se viṇāsaṃ /
rāgāure hariṇamige va muddhe | sadde atitte samuvei maccuṃ 
je yāvi dosaṃ samuvei tivvaṃ | taṃsi kkhaṇe se u uvei dukkhaṃ /
duddantadoseṇa saeṇa jantū | na kiṃci saddaṃ avarujjhaī se 
egantaratte ruiraṃsi sadde | atālise se kuṇaī paosaṃ /
dukkhassa saṃpīlam uvei bāle | na lippaī teṇa muṇī virāgo 
saddāṇugāsāṇugae ya jīve | carācare hiṃsai 'egarūve /
cittehi te paritāvei bāle | pīlei attaṭhagurū kiliṭhe 
saddāṇuvāeṇa pariggaheṇa | uppāyaṇe rakkhaṇasannioge /
vae vioge ya kahaṃ suhaṃ se | saṃbhogakāle ya atittalābhe 
sadde atitte ya pariggahaṃmi | sattovasatto na uvei tuṭhiṃ /
atuṭhidoseṇa duhī parassa | lobhāvile āyayaī adattaṃ 
taṇhābhibhūyassa adattahāriṇo | sadde atittassa pariggahe ya /
māyāmusaṃ vaḍḍhai lobhadosā | tatthāvi dukkhā na vimuccaī se 
mosassa pacchā ya puratthao ya | paogakāle ya duhī durante /
evaṃ adattāṇi samāyayanto | sadde atitto duhio aṇisso 
saddāṇurattassa narassa evaṃ | katto suhaṃ hojja kayāi kiṃci /
tatthovabhoge vi kilesadukkhaṃ | nivvattaī jassa kaeṇa dukkhaṃ 
emeva saddammi gao paosaṃ | uvei dukkhohaparaṃparāo /
paduṭhacitto ya ciṇāi kammaṃ | jaṃ se puṇo hoi duhaṃ vivāge 
sadde viratto maṇuo visogo | eeṇa dukkhohaparaṃpareṇa /
na lippae bhavamajjhe vi santo | jaleṇa vā pokkhariṇīpalāsaṃ 
ghāṇassa gandhaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | taṃ rāgaheuṃ tu maṇunnam āhu /
taṃ dosaheuṃ amaṇunnam āhu | samo ya jo tesu sa vīyarāgo 
gandhassa ghāṇaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | ghāṇassa gandhaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti /
rāgassa heuṃ samaṇunnam āhu | dosassa heuṃ amaṇunnam āhu 
gandhesu jo gehim uvei tivvaṃ | akāliyaṃ pāvai se viṇāsaṃ /
rāgāure osahagandhagiddhe | sappe bilāo viva nikkhamante 
je yāvi dosaṃ samuvei tivvaṃ | taṃsi kkhaṇe se u uvei dukkhaṃ /
duddantadoseṇa saeṇa jantū | na kiṃci gandhaṃ avarujjhaī se 
egantaratte ruiraṃsi gandhe | atālise se kuṇaī paosaṃ /
dukkhassa saṃpīlam uvei bāle | na lippaī teṇa muṇī virāgo 
gandhāṇugāsāṇugae ya jīve | carācare hiṃsai 'egarūve /
cittehi te paritāvei bāle | pīlei attaṭhagurū kiliṭhe 
gandhāṇuvāeṇa pariggaheṇa | uppāyaṇe rakkhaṇasannioge /
vae vioge ya kahaṃ suhaṃ se | saṃbhogakāle ya atittalābhe 
gandhe atitte ya pariggahaṃmi | sattovasatto na uvei tuṭhiṃ /
atuṭhidoseṇa duhī parassa | lobhāvile āyayaī adattaṃ 
taṇhābhibhūyassa adattahāriṇo | gandhe atittassa pariggahe ya /
māyāmusaṃ vaḍḍhai lobhadosā | tatthāvi dukkhā na vimuccaī se 
mosassa pacchā ya puratthao ya | paogakāle ya duhī durante /
evaṃ adattāṇi samāyayanto | gandhe atitto duhio aṇisso 
gandhāṇurattassa narassa evaṃ | katto suhaṃ hojja kayāi kiṃci /
tatthovabhoge vi kilesadukkhaṃ | nivvattaī jassa kaeṇa dukkhaṃ 
emeva gandhammi gao paosaṃ | uvei dukkhohaparaṃparāo /
paduṭhacitto ya ciṇāi kammaṃ | jaṃ se puṇo hoi duhaṃ vivāge 
gandhe viratto maṇuo visogo | eeṇa dukkhohaparaṃpareṇa /
na lippaī bhavamajjhe vi santo | jaleṇa vā pokkhariṇīpalāsaṃ 
jibbhāe rasaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | taṃ rāgaheuṃ tu maṇunnam āhu /
taṃ dosaheuṃ amaṇunnam āhu | samo ya jo tesu sa vīyarāgo 
rasassa jibbhaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | jibbhāe rasaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti /
rāgassa heuṃ samaṇunnam āhu | dosassa heuṃ amaṇunnam āhu 
rasesu jo gehim uvei tivvaṃ | akāliyaṃ pāvai se viṇāsaṃ /
rāgāure vaḍisavibhinnakāe | macche jahā āmisabhogagiddhe 
je yāvi dosaṃ samuvei tivvaṃ | taṃsi kkhaṇe se u uvei dukkhaṃ /
duddantadoseṇa saeṇa jantū | na kiṃci rasaṃ avarujjhaī se 
egantaratte ruiraṃsi rase | atālise se kuṇaī paosaṃ /
dukkhassa saṃpīlam uvei bāle | na lippaī teṇa muṇī virāgo 
rasāṇugāsāṇugae ya jīve | carācare hiṃsai 'egarūve /
cittehi te paritāvei bāle | pīlei attaṭhagurū kiliṭhe 
rasāṇuvāeṇa pariggaheṇa | uppāyaṇe rakkhaṇasannioge /
vae vioge ya kahaṃ suhaṃ se | saṃbhogakāle ya atittalābhe 
rase atitte ya pariggahaṃmi | sattovasatto na uvei tuṭhiṃ /
atuṭhidoseṇa duhī parassa | lobhāvile āyayaī adattaṃ 
taṇhābhibhūyassa adattahāriṇo | rase atittassa pariggahe ya /
māyāmusaṃ vaḍḍhai lobhadosā | tatthāvi dukkhā na vimuccaī se 
mosassa pacchā ya puratthao ya | paogakāle ya duhī durante /
evaṃ adattāṇi samāyayanto | rase atitto duhio aṇisso 
rasāṇurattassa narassa evaṃ | katto suhaṃ hojja kayāi kiṃci /
tatthovabhoge vi kilesadukkha | nivvattaī jassa kaeṇa dukkhaṃ 
emeva rasammi gao paosaṃ | uvei dukkhohaparaṃparāo /
paduṭhacitto ya ciṇāi kammaṃ | jaṃ se puṇo hoi duhaṃ vivāge 
rase viratto maṇuo visogo | eeṇa dukkhohaparaṃpareṇa /
na lippaī bhavamajjhe vi santo | jaleṇa vā pokkhariṇīpalāsaṃ 
kāyassa phāsaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | taṃ rāgaheuṃ tu maṇunnam āhu /
taṃ dosaheuṃ amaṇunnam āhu | samo ya jo tesu sa vīyarāgo 
phāsassa kāyaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | kāyassa phāsaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti /
rāgassa heuṃ samaṇunnam āhu | dosassa heuṃ amaṇunnam āhu 
phāsesu jo gehim uvei tivvaṃ | akāliyaṃ pāvai se viṇāsaṃ /
rāgāure sīyajalāvasanne | gāhaggahīe mahise vivanne 
je yāvi dosaṃ samuvei tivvaṃ | taṃsi kkhaṇe se u uvei dukkhaṃ /
duddantadoseṇa saeṇa jantū | na kiṃci phāsaṃ avarujjhaī se 
egantaratte ruiraṃsi phāse | atālise se kuṇaī paosaṃ /
dukkhassa saṃpīlam uvei bāle | na lippaī teṇa muṇī virāgo 
phāsāṇugāsāṇugae ya jīve | carācare hiṃsai 'egarūve /
cittehi te paritāvei bāle | pīlei attaṭhagurū kiliṭhe 
phāsāṇuvāeṇa pariggaheṇa | uppāyaṇe rakkhaṇasannioge /
vae vioge ya kahaṃ suhaṃ se | saṃbhogakāle ya atittalābhe 
phāse atitte ya pariggahaṃmi | sattovasatto na uvei tuṭhiṃ /
atuṭhidoseṇa duhī parassa | lobhāvile āyayaī adattaṃ 
taṇhābhibhūyassa adattahāriṇo | phāse atittassa pariggahe ya /
māyāmusaṃ vaḍḍhai lobhadosā | tatthāvi dukkhā na vimuccaī se 
mosassa pacchā ya puratthao ya | paogakāle ya duhī durante /
evaṃ adattāṇi samāyayanto | phāse atitto duhio aṇisso 
phāsāṇurattassa narassa evaṃ | katto suhaṃ hojja kayāi kiṃci /
tatthovabhoge vi kilesadukkhaṃ | nivvattaī jassa kaeṇa dukkhaṃ 
emeva phāsammi gao paosaṃ | uvei dukkhohaparaṃparāo /
paduṭhacitto ya ciṇāi kammaṃ | jaṃ se puṇo hoi duhaṃ vivāge 
phāse viratto maṇuo visogo | eeṇa dukkhohaparaṃpareṇa /
na lippaī bhavamajjhe vi santo | jaleṇa vā pokkhariṇīpalāsaṃ 
maṇassa bhāvaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | taṃ rāgaheuṃ tu maṇunnam āhu /
taṃ dosaheuṃ amaṇunnam āhu | samo ya jo tesu sa vīyarāgo 
bhāvassa maṇaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti | maṇassa bhāvaṃ gahaṇaṃ vayanti /
rāgassa heuṃ samaṇunnam āhu | dosassa heuṃ amaṇunnam āhu 
bhāvesu jo gehim uvei tivvaṃ | akāliyaṃ pāvai se viṇāsaṃ /
rāgāure kāmaguṇesu giddhe | kareṇumaggāvahie gaje vā 
je yāvi dosaṃ samuvei tivvaṃ | taṃsi kkhaṇe se u uvei dukkhaṃ /
duddantadoseṇa saeṇa jantū | na kiṃci bhāvaṃ avarujjhaī se 
egantaratte ruiraṃsi bhāve | atālise se kuṇaī paosaṃ /
dukkhassa saṃpīlam uvei bāle | na lippaī teṇa muṇī virāgo 
bhāvāṇugāsāṇugae ya jīve | carācare hiṃsai 'egarūve /
cittehi te paritāvei bāle | pīlei attaṭhagurū kiliṭhe 
bhāvāṇuvāeṇa pariggaheṇa | uppāyaṇe rakkhaṇasannioge /
vae vioge ya kahaṃ suhaṃ se | saṃbhogakāle ya atittalābhe 
bhāve atitte ya pariggahaṃmi | sattovasatto na uvei tuṭhiṃ /
atuṭhidoseṇa duhī parassa | lobhāvile āyayaī adattaṃ 
taṇhābhibhūyassa adattahāriṇo | bhāve atittassa pariggahe ya /
māyāmusaṃ vaḍḍhai lobhadosā | tatthāvi dukkhā na vimuccaī se 
mosassa pacchā ya puratthao ya | paogakāle ya duhī durante /
evaṃ adattāṇi samāyayanto | bhāve atitto duhio aṇisso 
bhāvāṇurattassa narassa evaṃ | katto suhaṃ hojja kayāi kiṃci /
tatthovabhoge vi kilesadukkhaṃ | nivvattaī jassa kaeṇa dukkhaṃ 
emeva bhāvammi gao paosaṃ | uvei dukkhohaparaṃparāo /
paduṭhacitto ya ciṇāi kammaṃ | jaṃ se puṇo hoi duhaṃ vivāge 
bhāve viratto maṇuo visogo | eeṇa dukkhohaparaṃpareṇa /
na lippaī bhavamajjhe vi santo | jaleṇa vā pokkhariṇīpalāsaṃ 
evindiyatthā ya maṇassa atthā | dukkhassa heuṃ maṇuyassa rāgiṇo /
te ceva thovaṃ pi kayāi dukkhaṃ | na vīyarāgassa karenti kiṃci 
na kāmabhogā samayaṃ uventi | na yāvi bhogā vigaiṃ uventi /
je tappaosī ya pariggahī ya | so tesu mohā vigaiṃ uvei 
kohaṃ ca māṇaṃ ca taheva māyaṃ | lohaṃ dugucchaṃ araiṃ raiṃ ca /
hāsaṃ bhayaṃ sogapumitthiveyaṃ | napuṃsaveyaṃ vivihe ya bhāve 
āvajjaī evam aṇegarūve | evaṃvihe kāmaguṇesu satto /
anne ya eyappabhave visese | kāruṇṇadīṇe hirime baisse 
kappaṃ na icchijja sahāyalicchū | pacchāṇutāve na tavappabhāvaṃ /
evaṃ viyāre amiyappayāre | āvajjaī indiyacoravasse 
tao se jāyanti paoyaṇāiṃ | nimajjiuṃ mohamahaṇṇavammi /
suhesiṇo dukkhaviṇoyaṇaṭhā | tappaccayaṃ ujjamae ya rāgī 
virajjamāṇassa ya indiyatthā | saddāiyā tāvaiyappagārā /
na tassa savve vi maṇunnayaṃ vā | nivvattayantī amaṇunnayaṃ vā 
evaṃ sasaṃkappavikappaṇāsuṃ | saṃjāyaī samayam uvaṭhiyassa /
atthe asaṃkappayao tao se | pahīyae kāmaguṇesu taṇhā 
sa vīyarāgo kayasavvakicco | khavei nāṇāvaraṇaṃ khaṇeṇaṃ /
taheva jaṃ daṃsaṇam āvarei | jaṃ cantarāyaṃ pakarei kammaṃ 
savvaṃ tao jāṇai pāsae ya | amohaṇe hoi nirantarāe /
aṇāsave jhāṇasamāhijutte | āukkhae mokkham uvei suddhe 
so tassa savvassa duhassa mukko | jaṃ bāhaī sayayaṃ jantum eyaṃ /
dīhāmayaṃ vippamukko pasattho | to hoi accantasuhī kayattho 
aṇāikālappabhavassa eso | savvassa dukkhassa pamokkhamaggo /
viyāhio jaṃ samuvicca sattā | kameṇa accantasuhī bhavanti 
     || pamāyaṭhānaṃ samattaṃ 
     
U/33 kammapayaḍī  trayatriṃśam adhyayanam /
 
aṭha kammāiṃ vocchāmi | āṇupuvviṃ jahākamaṃ /
jehiṃ baddho ayaṃ jīvo | saṃsāre parivaaī 
nāṇassāvaraṇijjaṃ | daṃsaṇāvaraṇaṃ tahā /
veyaṇijjaṃ tahā mohaṃ | āukammaṃ taheva ya 
nāmakammaṃ ca goyaṃ ca | antarāyaṃ taheva ya /
evam eyāi kammāiṃ | aṭheva u samāsao 
nāṇāvaraṇaṃ paṃcavihaṃ | suyaṃ ābhiṇibohiyaṃ /
ohināṇaṃ ca taiyaṃ | maṇanāṇaṃ ca kevalaṃ 
niddā taheva payalā | niddāniddā payalapayalā ya /
tatto ya thīṇagiddhī u | paṃcamā hoi nāyavvā 
cakkhumacakkhūohissa | daṃsaṇe kevale ya āvaraṇe /
evaṃ tu navavigappaṃ | nāyavvaṃ daṃsaṇāvaraṇaṃ 
veyaṇīyaṃ pi ya duvihaṃ | sāyam asāyaṃ ca āhiyaṃ /
sāyassa u bahū bheyā | emeva asāyassa vi 
mohaṇijjaṃ pi duvihaṃ | daṃsaṇe caraṇe tahā /
daṃsaṇe tivihaṃ vuttaṃ | caraṇe duvihaṃ bhave 
sammattaṃ ceva micchattaṃ | sammāmicchattam eva ya /
eyāo tinni payaḍīo | mohaṇijjassa daṃsaṇe 
carittamohaṇaṃ kammaṃ | duvihaṃ taṃ viyāhiyaṃ /
kasāyamohaṇijjaṃ tu | nokasāyaṃ taheva ya 
solasavihabheeṇaṃ | kammaṃ tu kasāyajaṃ /
sattavihaṃ navavihaṃ vā | kammaṃ ca nokasāyajaṃ 
neraiyatirikkhāuṃ | maṇussāuṃ taheva ya /
devāuyaṃ cautthaṃ tu | āuṃ kammaṃ cauvvihaṃ 
nāmaṃ kammaṃ tu duvihaṃ | suhamasuhaṃ ca āhiyaṃ /
subhassa u bahū bheyā | emeva asuhassa vi 
goyaṃ kammaṃ duvihaṃ | uccaṃ nīyaṃ ca āhiyaṃ /
uccaṃ aṭhavihaṃ hoi | evaṃ nīyaṃ pi āhiyaṃ 
dāṇe lābhe ya bhoge ya | uvabhoge vīrie tahā /
paṃcaviham antarāyaṃ | samāseṇa viyāhiyaṃ 
eyāo mūlapayaḍīo | uttarāo ya āhiyā /
paesaggaṃ khettakāle ya | bhāvaṃ ca uttaraṃ suṇa 
savvesiṃ ceva kammāṇaṃ | paesaggam aṇantagaṃ /
gaṇṭhiyasattāīyaṃ | anto siddhāṇa āhiyaṃ 
savvajīvāṇa kammaṃ tu | saṃgahe chaddisāgayaṃ /
savvesu vi paesesu | savvaṃ savveṇa baddhagaṃ 
udahīsarisanāmāṇa | tīsaī koḍikoḍīo /
ukkosiyā ṭhiī hoi | antomuhuttaṃ jahanniyā 
āvaraṇijjāṇa duṇhaṃ pi | veyaṇijje taheva ya /
antarāe ya kammammi | ṭhiī esā viyāhiyā 
udahīsarisanāmāṇa | sattariṃ koḍikoḍīo /
mohaṇijjassa ukkosā | antomuhuttaṃ jahanniyā 
tettīsa sāgarovamā | ukkoseṇa viyāhiyā /
ṭhiī u āukammassa | antomuhuttaṃ jahanniyā 
udahīsarisanāmāṇa | vīsaī koḍikoḍīo /
nāmagottāṇaṃ ukkosā | aṭha muhuttā jahanniyā 
siddhāṇaṇantabhāgo ya | aṇubhāgā havanti u /
savvesu vi paesaggaṃ | savvajīve aicchiyaṃ 
tamhā eesi kammāṇaṃ | aṇubhāgā viyāṇiyā /
eesi saṃvare ceva | khavaṇe ya jae buho  tti bemi ||
      || kammapayaḍī samattā 
     
U/34 lesajjhayaṇaṃ catustriṃśam adhyayanam /
 
lesajjhayaṇaṃ pavakkhāmi | āṇupuvviṃ jahakkamaṃ /
chaṇhaṃ pi kammalesāṇaṃ | aṇubhāve suṇeha me 
nāmāiṃ vaṇṇarasagandha | phāsapariṇāmalakkhaṇaṃ /
ṭhāṇaṃ ṭhiiṃ gaiṃ cāuṃ | lesāṇaṃ tu suṇeha me 
kiṇhā nīlā ya kāū ya | teū pamhā taheva ya /
sukkalesā ya chaṭhā ya | nāmāiṃ tu jahakkamaṃ 
jīmūyaniddhasaṃkāsā | gavalariṭhagasannibhā /
khaṃjaṇanayaṇanibhā | kiṇhalesā u vaṇṇao 
nīlāsogasaṃkāsā | cāsapicchasamappabhā /
veruliyaniddhasaṃkāsā | nīlalesā u vaṇṇao 
ayasīpupphasaṃkāsā | koilacchadasannibhā /
pārevayagīvanibhā | kāūlesā u vaṇṇao 
hiṃguladhāusaṃkāsā | taruṇāiccasannibhā /
suyatuṇḍapaīvanibhā | teūlesā u vaṇṇao 
hariyālabheyasaṃkāsā | haliddābheyasamappabhā /
saṇāsaṇakusumanibhā | pamhalesā u vaṇṇao 
saṃkhaṃkakundasaṃkāsā | khīrapūrasamappabhā /
rayayahārasaṃkāsā | sukkalesā u vaṇṇao 
jaha kaḍuyatumbagaraso | nimbaraso kaḍuyarohiṇiraso vā /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | raso ya kiṇhāe nāyavvo 
jaha tigaḍuyassa ya raso | tikkho jaha hatthipippalīe vā /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | raso u nīlāe nāyavvo 
jaha taruṇaambagaraso | tuvarakaviṭhassa vāvi jārisao /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | raso u kāūe nāyavvo 
jaha pariṇiyambagaraso | pakkakaviṭhassa vāvi jārisao /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | raso u teūe nāyavvo 
varavāruṇīe va raso | vivihāṇa va āsavāṇa jārisao /
mahumerayassa va raso | etto pamhāe paraeṇaṃ 
khajjūramuddiyaraso | khīraraso khaṇḍasakkararaso vā /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | raso u sukkāe nāyavvo 
jaha gomaḍassa gandho | suṇagamaḍassa va jahā ahimaḍassa /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | lesāṇaṃ appasatthāṇaṃ 
jaha surahikusumagandho | gandhavāsāṇa pissamāṇāṇaṃ /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | pasatthalesāṇa tiṇhaṃ pi 
jaha karagayassa phāso | gojibbhāe ya sāgapattāṇaṃ /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | lesāṇaṃ appasatthāṇaṃ 
jaha būrassa va phāso | navaṇīyassa va sirīsakusumāṇaṃ /
etto vi aṇantaguṇo | pasatthalesāṇa tiṇhaṃ pi 
tiviho va navaviho vā | sattāvīsaivihekkasīo vā /
dusao teyālo vā | lesāṇaṃ hoi pariṇāmo 
paṃcāsavappavatto | tīhiṃ agutto chasuṃ avirao ya /
tivvārambhapariṇao | khuḍḍo sāhasio naro 
niddhandhasapariṇāmo | nissaṃso ajiindio /
eyajogasamāutto | kiṇhalesaṃ tu pariṇame 
issā amarisa atavo | avijjamāyā ahīriyā /
gehī paose ya saḍhe | pamatte rasalolue 
sāyagavesae ya ārambhāo avirao | khuḍḍo sāhassio naro /
eyajogasamāutto | nīlalesaṃ tu pariṇame 
vaṃke vaṃkasamāyāre | niyaḍille aṇujjue /
paliuṃcagaovahie | micchadiṭhī aṇārie 
upphāsagaduṭhavāī ya | teṇe yāvi ya maccharī /
eyajogasamāutto | kāūlesaṃ tu pariṇame 
nīyāvattī acavale | amāī akuūhale /
viṇīyaviṇae dante | jogavaṃ uvahāṇavaṃ 
piyadhamme daḍhadhamme | vajjabhīrū hiesae /
eyajogasamāutto | teūlesaṃ tu pariṇame 
payaṇukohamāṇe ya | māyālobhe ya payaṇue /
pasantacitte dantappā | jogavaṃ uvahāṇavaṃ 
tahā payaṇuvāī ya | uvasante jiindie /
eyajogasamāutto | pamhalesaṃ tu pariṇame 
aaruddāṇi vajjittā | dhammasukkāṇi jhāyae /
pasantacitte dantappā | samie gutte ya guttisu 
sarāge vīyarāge vā | uvasante jiindie /
eyajogasamāutto | sukkalesaṃ tu pariṇame 
asaṃkhijjāṇosappiṇīṇa | ussappiṇīṇa je samayā /
saṃkhāīyā logā | lesāṇa havanti ṭhāṇāiṃ 
muhuttaddhaṃ tu jahannā | tettīsā sāgarā muhuttahiyā /
ukkosā hoi ṭhiī | nāyavvā kiṇhalesāe 
muhuttaddhaṃ tu jahannā | dasa udahī paliyam asaṃkhabhāgam abbhahiyā /
ukkosā hoi ṭhiī | nāyavvā nīlalesāe 
muhutaddhaṃ tu jahannā | tiṇṇudahī paliyam asaṃkhabhāgam abbhahiyā /
ukkosā hoi ṭhiī | nāyavvā kāulesāe 
muhutaddhaṃ tu jahannā | doṇṇudahī paliyam asaṃkhabhāgam abbhahiyāũ/
ukkosā hoi ṭhiī | nāyavvā teulesāe 
muhuttaddhaṃ tu jahannā | dasa honti ya sāgarā muhuttahiyā /
ukkosā hoi ṭhiī | nāyavvā pamhalesāe 
muhuttaddhaṃ tu jahannā | tettīsaṃ sāgarā muhuttahiyā /
ukkosā hoi ṭhiī | nāyavvā sukkalesāe 
esā khalu lesāṇaṃ | oheṇa ṭhiī vaṇṇiyā hoi /
causu vi gaīsu etto | lesāṇa ṭhiiṃ tu vocchāmi 
dasa vāsasahassāiṃ | kāūe ṭhiī jahanniyā hoi /
tiṇṇudahī paliovama | asaṃkhabhāgaṃ ca ukkosā 
tiṇṇudahī paliovama | saṃkhabhāgo jahanneṇa nīlaṭhiī /
dasaudahī paliovama | asaṃkhabhāgaṃ ca ukkosā 
dasaudahī paliovama | asaṃkhabhāgaṃ jahanniyā hoi /
tettīsasāgarāiṃ | ukkosā hoi kiṇhāe lesāe 
esā neraiyāṇaṃ | lesāṇa ṭhiī u vaṇṇiyā hoi /
teṇa paraṃ vocchāmi | tiriyamaṇussāṇa devāṇaṃ 
antomuhuttam addhaṃ | lesāṇa jahiṃ jahiṃ jāu /
tiriyāṇa narāṇaṃ vā | vajjittā kevalaṃ lesaṃ 
muhuttaddhaṃ tu jahannā | ukkosā hoi puvvakoḍīo /
navahi varisehi ūṇā | nāyavvā sukkalesāe 
esā tiriyanarāṇaṃ | lesāṇa ṭhiī u vaṇṇiyā hoi /
teṇa paraṃ vocchāmi | lesāṇa ṭhiīu devāṇaṃ 
dasa vāsasahassāiṃ | kiṇhāe ṭhiī jahanniyā hoi /
paliyam asaṃkhijja imo | ukkoso hoi kiṇhāe 
jā kiṇhāe ṭhiī khalu | ukkosā sā u samayam abbhahiyā /
jahanneṇaṃ nīlāe | paliyam asaṃkhaṃ ca ukkosā 
jā nīlāe ṭhiī khalu | ukkosā sā u samayam abbhahiyā /
jahanneṇaṃ kāūe | paliyam asaṃkhaṃ ca ukkosā 
teṇa paraṃ vocchāmi | teūlesā jahā suragāṇaṃ /
bhavaṇavaivāṇamantara | joisavemāṇiyāṇaṃ ca 
paliovamaṃ jahannaṃ | ukkosā sāgarāo dunnahiyā /
paliyam asaṃkhejjeṇaṃ | hoi bhāgeṇa teūe 
dasa vāsasahassāiṃ | teūe ṭhiī jahanniyā hoi /
dunnudahī paliovama | asaṃkhabhāga ca ukkosā 
jā teūe ṭhiī khalu | ukkosā sā u samayam abbhahiyā /
jahanneṇaṃ pamhāe | dasa u muhuttāhiyāi ukkosā 
jā pamhāe ṭhiī khalu | ukkosā sā u samayam abbhahiyā /
jahanneṇaṃ sukkāe | tettīsa muhuttam abbhahiyā 
kiṇhā nīlā kāū | tinni vi eyāo ahammalesāo /
eyāhi tihi vi jīvo | duggaiṃ uvavajjaī 
teū pamhā sukkā | tinni vi eyāo dhammalesāo /
eyāhi tihi vi jīvo | suggaiṃ uvavajjaī 
lesāhiṃ savvāhiṃ | paḍhame samayammi pariṇayāhiṃ tu /
na hu kassai uvavāo | pare bhave atthi jīvassa 
lesāhiṃ savvāhiṃ | carime samayammi pariṇayāhiṃ tu /
na hu kassai uvavāo | pare bhave hoi jīvassa 
antamuhuttammi gae | antamuhuttammi sesae ceva /
lesāhi pariṇayāhiṃ | jīvā gacchanti paraloyaṃ 
tamhā eyāsi lesāṇaṃ | āṇubhāve viyāṇiyā /
appasatthāo vajjittā | pasatthāo 'hiṭhie muṇi  tti bemi ||
     || lesajjhayaṇaṃ samattaṃ 

U/35 aṇagārajjhayaṇaṃ pañcatriṃśam adhyayanam /
suṇeha me egaggamaṇā | maggaṃ buddhehi desiyaṃ /
jamāyaranto bhikkhū | dukkhāṇantakare bhave 
gihavāsaṃ pariccajja | pavajjām assie muṇī /
ime saṃge viyāṇijjā | jehiṃ sajjanti māṇavā 
taheva hiṃsaṃ aliyaṃ | cojjaṃ abambhasevaṇaṃ /
icchākāmaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca | saṃjao parivajjae 
maṇoharaṃ cittagharaṃ | malladhūveṇa vāsiyaṃ /
sakavāḍaṃ paṇḍurullovaṃ | maṇasā vi na patthae 
indiyāṇi u bhikkhussa | tārisammi uvassae /
dukkarāiṃ nivāreuṃ | kāmarāgavivaḍḍhaṇe 
susāṇe sunnagāre vā | rukkhamūle va ikkao /
pairikke parakaḍe vā | vāsaṃ tatthābhiroyae 
phāsuyammi aṇābāhe | itthīhiṃ aṇabhiddue /
tattha saṃkappae vāsaṃ | bhikkhū paramasaṃjae 
na sayaṃ gihāiṃ kuvvijjā | -eva annehiṃ kārae /
gihakammasamārambhe | bhūyāṇaṃ dissae vaho 
tasāṇaṃ thāvarāṇaṃ ca | suhumāṇaṃ bādarāṇa ya /
tamhā gihasamārambhaṃ | saṃjao parivajjae 
taheva bhattapāṇesu | payaṇe payāvaṇesu ya /
pāṇabhūyadayaṭhāe | na paye na payāvae 
jaladhannanissiyā jīvā | puḍhavīkaṭhanissiyā /
hammanti bhattapāṇesu | tamhā bhikkhū na payāvae 
visappe savvao-dhāre | bahū pāṇaviṇāsaṇe /
